# Progress tracker

Tracks feature units per the workflow in `CLAUDE.md`. One section per unit.

> **Older history is archived.** Units before Spec 21 live in [`progress-archive.md`](progress-archive.md), kept out of this file to save context. This file holds Spec 21 onward.

## Spec 211 ã Procurement terminology & level clarity, U1ãU6 (2026-06-27)

Status: **shipping U1** (code-only, NO schema). Spec: `211-procurement-terminology-clarity.md`. Evidence: `docs/procurement-uxui-audit-2026-06.md` (multi-agent UX audit, 85 surfaces / 91 verified findings).

Operator report: admins can't intuitively distinguish a PO (Á¿Á¡Á¡ˆÁ¡ÝÁ¿Á¡Á¡Á¡ñÁ¿Á¡Ù) from its PO-items. The headline cause (audit `po-vs-items-01`, confirmed **high**, independently rediscovered û9): a PO has no status column ã its roll-up is derived from member PRs ã so `PURCHASE_ORDER_STATUS_LABEL` and `PURCHASE_REQUEST_STATUS_LABEL` shared the byte-identical strings `Á¡ˆÁ¡ÝÁ¿Á¡Á¡Á¡ñÁ¿Á¡ÙÁ¿Á¡ËÁ¿Á¡Ï` (PR purchased / PO ordered) and `Á¡Á¡°Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¡Á¡ˆÁ¿Á¡` (PR on_route / PO in_transit). On the PO detail the order pill and a line pill then read the same word.

**U1 (this unit):** split the PO roll-up vocabulary in `src/lib/i18n/labels.ts` ã `ordered: Á¡ˆÁ¡ÝÁ¿Á¡Á¡Á¡ñÁ¿Á¡ÙÁ¿Á¡ËÁ¿Á¡Ï ã Á¡ÙÁ¡ÙÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¡ˆÁ¡ÝÁ¿Á¡Á¡Á¡ñÁ¿Á¡ÙÁ¿Á¡ËÁ¿Á¡Ï`, `in_transit: Á¡Á¡°Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¡Á¡ˆÁ¿Á¡ ã Á¡Á¡°Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¡Á¡ˆÁ¿Á¡Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¿Á¡Á¿Á¡` (PR map untouched; `open`/`partially_received`/`received` already order-scoped). Test-first: added a cross-map invariant in `tests/unit/i18n-labels.test.ts` ã the PR-status and PO-status maps must share NO string value (regression guard), plus pins for the two new strings. Display-only (logic keys on enums), so all PO surfaces (detail header, grid PO header row, phone PO card, delivery page) inherit it with no other code change. Verify limitation: not exercised in a live browser (PO detail needs LINE auth + seeded PO data); the unit test asserts the exact rendered strings the surfaces consume.

**U2 (PR #?? ã shipping):** visually type the IDs. New `src/lib/purchasing/format-id.ts` SSOT (`formatPoNumber`/`formatPrNumber`, zero-pad 4) routed through all 16 PR/PO render sites ã fixes the bare-`PR-7`-vs-`PR-0007` drift (the grid/basket/create-sheet showed bare numbers, everything else 4-padded). New server-safe `<PoNumberTag>` (a `bg-sunk` chip with the Package icon) marks every PO number as an order, visually distinct from the plain-mono PR number ã applied on the worklist grid PO header + phone PO card, the PO detail header, the delivery detail eyebrow, and the PRãPO parent link. Notifications keep their own copy of the formatter (`compose-notification.ts` is danger-path ã U8). Test-first `tests/unit/format-id.test.ts`; no existing test broke (purchase-request-card already rendered `PR-0007`). Code-only.

**U3 (PR #?? ã shipping):** de-overload `Á¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡È` on the worklist grid (`procurement-grid.tsx` only). The word labelled the item column, the bundle hint, the selection count AND the drawer doc count ã colliding with its line-count meaning on the same screen. Renamed: column header `Á¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡È`ã`Á¡ˆÁ¡ÇÁ¿Á¡Á¡Á¡çÁ¿Á¡Á¡ÙÁ¡Á¡ñÁ¿Á¡Ù`; bundle hint `Á¿Á¡ËÁ¡ñÁ¡ÙÁ¡Á¡¨Á¡ËÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡ÈãÎ`ã`Á¿Á¡ËÁ¡ñÁ¡ÙÁ¡Á¡¨Á¡ËÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡°Á¡Á¡ÙãÎ`; selection `Á¿Á¡ËÁ¡ñÁ¡ÙÁ¡ {n} Á¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡È`ã`Á¿Á¡ËÁ¡ñÁ¡ÙÁ¡ {n} Á¡Á¡°Á¡Á¡Ù`; drawer doc fact `{n} Á¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡È`ã`{n} Á¿Á¡Á¡ËÁ¿`. The legitimate PO line-count (`{n} Á¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡È`) is KEPT. Test-first `procurement-grid-terminology.test.tsx` (header rename; the bundle-hint case was dropped ã rendering the bundle path mounts the create-PO sheet's `useRouter`, which the grid-health test also avoids). Accounting register `Á¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡È`ã`Á¿Á¡Á¡Á¡ÙÁ¡Á¡ñÁ¿Á¡Ù` moved to U9. Code-only.

**U5 (PR #?? ã shipping):** PO membership visible in EVERY worklist band, not just the `in_transit` PO group. The page now fetches `po_number` for every PO any row belongs to (`poNumberById`, all bands), bakes it onto `ProcurementGridRecord.po_number`, and passes `poNumber` to `PurchaseRequestCard`. The desktop grid renders a `<PoNumberTag>` chip per row outside `in_transit` (which keeps its PoHeaderRow group); the phone card renders the chip whenever the request belongs to a PO. Required-field add to `ProcurementGridRecord` ã updated all 4 constructors (page, grid-health test, terminology test, phone-basket test, grid-preview page). Test-first: extended `purchase-request-card.test.tsx` (chip shows with poNumber, absent without). Code-only.

**U6 (PR #?? ã shipping):** make the level legible in nav. The nav landmark named the whole purchasing area `Á¡Á¡°Á¡Á¡ÙÁ¡Á¡ñÁ¿Á¡Ù` (the PR term) in every role's tab set, and a **PO** detail's back-chip read `Á¡Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¡Á¡°Á¡Á¡ÙÁ¡Á¡ñÁ¿Á¡Ù`. Renamed `Á¡Á¡°Á¡Á¡ÙÁ¡Á¡ñÁ¿Á¡Ù` ã neutral `Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¡Á¡Á¡ñÁ¿Á¡Ù` in both nav sources (`hub-nav.tsx` desktop strip û3 sets + `bottom-tab-bar.tsx` phone bar û3 sets) + the worklist page title/kicker; back-chips on the PO detail and PR detail ã `Á¡Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¡Á¡Á¡ñÁ¿Á¡Ù`. The PR-concept `Á¡Á¡°Á¡Á¡ÙÁ¡Á¡ñÁ¿Á¡Ù` stays for the request list/empty-state/create buttons. Test-first: flipped the existing nav assertions in `hub-nav.test.tsx` + `bottom-tab-bar.test.tsx` to expect `Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¡Á¡Á¡ñÁ¿Á¡Ù` (7 red ã green). Code-only. **Deferred ã U6b:** breadcrumb + `?from=` PRãPO back-href.

**U4 (PR #?? ã shipping, operator-directed reframe):** status icons app-wide. Operator asked to "use icons to distinguish statuses, consistent with detail pages" ã better than restyling the PO pill colour (which would regress the spec-20 sun-readable solid fills). New SSOT `src/lib/status-icons.ts` (icon maps + accessors for all 7 StatusPill domains, `Record<Enum, LucideIcon>` = type-enforced totality) + an optional `icon` prop on `StatusPill` (backward-compatible). A one-agent-per-file **workflow** added `icon={domainIcon(sameArg)}` to all **28** call sites across **18** files, so the glyph renders identically on the worklist and every detail page/card/tracker. Test-first `status-icons.test.ts` (totality). Verified: tsc + eslint clean (run direct ã corepack flaked to pnpm 11.9.0 mid-run, recovered), 1796/1796 tests. Code-only. Feedback-status pills use a separate mechanism ã follow-up.

Remaining units queued in the spec: U6b (breadcrumb + PRãPO referrer), U7 (band-label SSOT), U10 (term SSOT), U11 (buy-action). U8 notifications + U9 accounting are danger-path ã operator-held.

## Spec 206 ã WHT certificate recording UI (2026-06-26)

Status: **SHIPPED ã 2026-06-26** (code-only, NO schema/db:push). Audit gap **G11** ã
the last accounting back-office write gap. The `record_wht_certificate` RPC, the
`wht_certificates`/`wht_rates` tables, the GL-posting trigger, the pure
`validateWhtCertificate` validator, and the read-only register `/accounting/wht`
all existed since spec 149 U6, but the validator was **orphaned** ã no write
surface. This unit adds the "+ Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¡Á¡Á¡ÑÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¡¨Á¡ÝÁ¡Á¡ Á¡ýÁ¡ˋÁ¡ç" form over the existing RPC.

**Live-DB gate verification (the key find).** Before wiring the gate I queried the
live RPC: `record_wht_certificate` admits `pm/super/project_director` ã the
migration _file_ shows pm/super, but `ãÎ0751ãÎ_project_director_rpc_gates.sql`
widened it live (the "live-body re-source trap"). Same for `create_client_billing`

- `post_journal_entry` (both pd live). So the gate reuses **`PM_ROLES`** (the
  role-home SSOT) via `isManagerRole`, NOT a fresh `[pm,super]` literal ã matching
  the journal/G8 precedent and the live RPC. Among ACCOUNTING_ROLES reachers only
  super_admin is a manager, so today the write affordance lights up for super_admin
  only (auto-widens if spec 166 re-adds PM/PD to the page gate).

**TDD:** `resolveWhtRate(incomeType, override, rates)` (mirrors the RPC's
`coalesce(p_wht_rate, default_rate)` ã finite override wins incl. 0; else the
income-type default; unknown+no-override ã null) written RED-first (6 cases) then
GREEN. `validateWhtCertificate` unchanged (still the amount gate). **Files:**
`resolveWhtRate` in `wht-certificate.ts`; `loadWhtFormData` in `load-registers.ts`
(income types + 3 party masters, parallel reads); `wht/actions.ts`
`recordWhtCertificate` (gate PM_ROLES, pre-validate, deducted-needs-party friendly
error, omit-optional args, call on auth.supabase, revalidate); `wht/record-wht-form.tsx`
(`'use client'` bottom-sheet ã direction/form/income-typeãrate-autofill/13-digit
tax id/base/party[supplier|contractor for Á¿Á¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡¨Á¡ÝÁ¡, client for Á¡Á¡¿Á¡Á¡¨Á¡ÝÁ¡]/date/note +
live wht_amount preview); wired into `wht/page.tsx` (canWrite = isManagerRole,
parallel load). Reuses `AccountingActionResult` + `ACCOUNTING_ACTION_ERROR` from
`billing-actions.ts`. Verified: typecheck ôñ lint ôñ full vitest **1723/1723** green.
Visual preview skipped (no dev-auth path ã LINE OAuth only; the form is a 1:1 twin
of the shipped spec-204 billing form). Money renders via the canonical `baht()`
SSOT.

**Open questions / follow-ups:**

- `BILLING_WRITE_ROLES = [pm,super]` (spec 204) is now confirmed **stale vs its
  live RPC** (which admits project_director) ã a pre-existing UI under-grant (PD
  can post billings per the RPC but the form never offers it). Not a security hole;
  flagged for the role-set SSOT consolidation (architecture-audit **rank 2**:
  fold billing/journal/wht's identical pm/super/pd accounting-write sets into one
  `ACCOUNTING_WRITE_ROLES`). Not fixed here (scope).
- `pay_source_table`/`pay_source_id` linking (cert ã its source payment), WHT-cert
  auto-record at billing certify, and Á¡ .Á¡.Á¡. PDF generation remain deferred.

## Gap G8 ã manual journal-entry UI (2026-06-25)

Status: **SHIPPED ã 2026-06-25** (code-only, NO schema/db:push). Audit gap **G8** ã
the `post_journal_entry` / `reverse_journal_entry` RPCs existed since spec 149 with
no screen. New `/accounting/journal` (general journal): a multi-line entry form
(date + memo + account-picker/debit/credit rows, one-sided enforced at input, LIVE
double-entry balance preview via `validateJournalLines`) + a recent-entries list
with a per-entry Á¡Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡È (reverse) control. **Gate = `PM_ROLES`** (pm/super/
project_director ã exactly who the RPCs admit; verified LIVE that a later migration
widened the gate to add project_director, NOT what the original migration file
shows). Placed in /accounting but gated to PM_ROLES (the journal-POST capability is
distinct from accounting-VIEW; only super_admin overlaps = today's operator); entry
point on the accounting landing shown only to `isManagerRole` so accounting-role
gets no dead link. **TDD:** `canReverseJournalEntry(status, alreadyReversed)`
predicate (mirrors the RPC guard ã original stays 'posted' after reversal since
append-only, so reversibility needs both) written RED-first then GREEN. **Loader**
`load-manual-journals.ts` parallelises fetches (specs 147/148) + one account map
resolves picker labels AND line codes (no N+1). **Riders (audit rank 7+12):**
standardised the new action on `requireActionRole`; hoisted the shared
`ACCOUNTING_ACTION_ERROR` next to `AccountingActionResult` and pointed billings at
it (DRY); wired the previously-dormant `validateJournalLines` (rank 12 ã its
intended consumer). Verified: typecheck ôñ lint ôñ full vitest 1698/1698 ôñ build
green; loader queries confirmed against live schema. Visual preview skipped (no
dev-auth path ã LINE OAuth only). **Open:** PM/PD have no nav entry point (can't
reach /accounting landing); accounting-role can't post manual JEs (RPC excludes it,
accounting is v3) ã both deferred, not blockers. Money renders via the canonical
`baht()` SSOT (audit rank 1 consolidation is a separate follow-up unit).

## Spec 204 ã client billing + retention write UI (2026-06-25)

Status: **SHIPPED ã 2026-06-25** (code-only, NO schema/db:push). Audit gap **G10** ã the
single biggest "backend-shipped-no-UI" gap. Spec 149 U5 shipped the client_billings /
retention_receivables tables, the create/certify/mark-due/release RPCs, the GL-posting
triggers, and the read-only registers ã but no UI to create a claim, certify it (book
AR/revenue/VAT/WHT + accrue retention), mark retention due, or release it. The GL had a
cost side, no revenue side. This unit adds the write surfaces.

- TDD (RED first): `tests/unit/billing-actions.test.ts` (status predicates
  canCertifyBilling/canMarkRetentionDue/canReleaseRetention mirroring the RPC guards) ã
  `src/lib/accounting/billing-actions.ts` (+ `BILLING_WRITE_ROLES` SSOT =
  [project_manager, super_admin], matching the RPC gate exactly ã NOT project_director).
- Actions: `billings/actions.ts` (createClientBilling, certifyClientBilling), `retention/
actions.ts` (markRetentionDue, releaseRetention) ã gate the AUTHED session, call the RPC
  on auth.supabase (never admin), revalidate both registers.
- UI: `CreateBillingForm` (BottomSheet + live computeBillingBreakdown preview), certify via
  ConfirmActionButton on draft/submitted rows; `RetentionRowActions` (mark-due date +
  release). Controls gated to BILLING_WRITE_ROLES (beta: super_admin only; auto-widens when
  spec 166 re-adds PM). Accounting role stays READ-ONLY on billing/retention (RPC = pm/super).
- QUALITY (architecture-first bar): extracted the copy-pasted server-action role-check into
  a shared `requireActionRole()` in `src/lib/auth/action-gate.ts` (periods/billings/retention
  now use it); extracted `baht()` into `src/lib/i18n/labels.ts` (3 of ~12 inline copies
  migrated); parallelized the billings-page reads (no waterfall, spec 147/148). Adversarial
  `/code-review high` ã 3 real findings FIXED (rate-field reset leak across claims; canWrite
  hardcodedãSSOT drift; baht DRY); rest refuted (input type=date guards dates; emptyã error).
- Verify: typecheck + lint + full vitest green; pgTAP 85/86 + client-billing.test already
  cover the RPCs/math. Operator visual-confirm on /accounting/billings + /accounting/retention
  as super_admin.

Open follow-ups (architecture-audit sweep): accountingãcertify yes/no (a spec/product call ã
RPC currently pm/super); migrate the remaining ~9 inline `baht` copies and the rest of the
server-action files to `requireActionRole()`.

## Spec 202 U1 ã per-item equipment daily-rate UI (2026-06-25)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-25** (no DB; lint ôñ typecheck ôñ vitest 1682 green).
The 2026-06-25 lifecycle review found
spec 146 (equipment rental money) fully built in the DB + validators but with **zero
UI / call sites** ã `equipment_usage_logs` is unpopulatable, so `wp_profit`'s equipment
term is structurally Á¡¢0. Spec 202 activates it; U1 is the dependency root (pricing).

Pure app code ã `set_equipment_daily_rate` (spec 146 U1) + `validateEquipmentDailyRate`
already exist; this wires the missing UI. Mirrors the catalog sell-rate money control.

**Test-first** (RED): `set-daily-rate.test.tsx` (new) + extend `equipment-manager.test.tsx`
(price control shows for the money audience, hidden on the site_admin field view).

**App:** `setEquipmentDailyRate` action ã `set_equipment_daily_rate` definer;
`SetDailyRate` component (BottomSheet, `Á¡¢x/Á¡ÏÁ¡ÝÁ¡`); `dailyRates` prop threaded through
`EquipmentManager`/`EquipmentRow`, rendered only under `canManageRegistry`; `/equipment`
admin-reads `daily_rate` for the money audience only.

## Spec 200 ã assign a worker to a project (the missing UI) (2026-06-24)

## Spec 198 ã divert a delivered WP-bound line into the store, U2 (2026-06-24)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-24** (ADR 0064; mig 20260813000900; pgTAP
216; lint ôñ typecheck ôñ vitest ôñ db:test). **SPEC 198 COMPLETE (U1+U2).**
Operator chose Option 3 (AskUserQuestion) ã the cost-clean version of "pre-fill
Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ý from a delivery." Investigation found the simple pre-fill has no target
(store-bound lines already auto-check-in via spec 195 P3; stocking a WP-bound
line as-is double-counts), so U2 is an inventory **diversion with a GL transfer**.

**ADR 0064** ã divert a delivered WP-bound purchase into the store (cost transfer
WP-WIP ã Inventory). Surfaced the GL risk + the design BEFORE building; operator
approved "build it + push (with ADR)."

**GL transfer (net):** reverse the WP purchase (Dr 2100 AP / Cr 1400 WP-WIP) +
the new stock_receipt (Dr 1500 Inventory / Cr 2100 AP) ã WP-WIP 0 ôñ Inventory
+cost ôñ **AP unchanged**. A later Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡ returns it Dr 1400 / Cr 1500 (cost lands on
the WP once, at usage ã the store-bound model).

**DB (migs 20260813000900 + 20260813001000):**

- New `divert_purchase_to_store(p_request_id)` definer RPC ã gate `SITE_STAFF`
  (procurement read-only in the store, spec 197), membership `can_see_project`,
  guards (delivered, WP-bound, catalogued, not already diverted ã the
  `stock_receipts_pr_uniq` index is the hard guard). It **reverses the WP purchase
  GL entry directly** (`reverse_journal_internal`, Dr 2100/Cr 1400) + **skips any
  pending purchase outbox job**, then inserts the `stock_receipt` (PR-stamped,
  all-in cost ã auto-enqueues Dr 1500/Cr AP), rolls `stock_on_hand`, sets the PR
  `work_package_id = NULL`.
- **`post_purchase_to_gl` is UNCHANGED.** The first attempt (000900) re-enqueued a
  `purchase` job to do the reversal + reordered `post_purchase_to_gl`'s
  reverse-before-suppress ã but that poster only accepts `purchased`/`site_purchased`,
  so a _delivered_ PR raises `P0001` and the reversal never fires. **pgTAP 216
  caught this** (WP-WIP stayed 300 = double-count). The corrective mig 001000
  reverts `post_purchase_to_gl` to LIVE and rewrites the RPC to reverse directly +
  skip the stale job. **Lesson: the async GL poster won't process a status it
  gates on ã reverse synchronously in the RPC.**
- **Async-safe:** purchase posted ã reverse it; still pending ã skip it (no WP-WIP
  ever). Both converge.

**App:** `divertPurchaseToStore({ requestId })` action + `DivertToStoreList`
client component (per-line `Á¡ÂÁ¿Á¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ýÁ¡Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡` via `ConfirmActionButton`). The Á¡Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡ page
reads the project's delivered + WP-bound + catalogued PRs not yet diverted (RLS

- filter out those with a `stock_receipts.purchase_request_id`), gated to
  `canIssue` (SITE_STAFF); renders the list after `StoreManager`. `db:types` regen.

**Test-first** (RED): `tests/unit/divert-to-store-list.test.tsx` (list + confirm
ã `divertPurchaseToStore`). **pgTAP 216 (plan 17, the ledger proof):**
structure/anon-deny; pre-divert WP-WIP=300; guards (visitor/non-member 42501,
not-delivered/WP-less 22023); happy divert; receipt-stamped + on-hand rolled + PR
WP-less; post the GL; **WP-WIP nets to 0 ôñ Inventory=300 ôñ AP net credit=300**;
already-diverted 22023.

**v1 scope:** whole-line divert only (no partial); the PR loses its WP identity in
the list (trace via `stock_receipts.purchase_request_id`); full undo of a divert
(re-attach the WP) is out of scope.

## Spec 198 ã multi-line Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ý (bulk stock check-in), U1 (2026-06-24)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-24** (mig 20260813000800; pgTAP 215; lint ôñ
typecheck ôñ vitest ôñ db:test green). Operator: "checking in items is too
difficult, one at a time ã the check-in list should be the same as delivery."
The Á¡Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡ `Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ýÁ¡ˆÁ¡Á¿Á¡ÙÁ¡` form was single-item-per-submit; U1 makes it a multi-row
**grid** recorded in one atomic call. (Operator chose **Both** grid + pre-fill-
from-delivery; U2 = pre-fill, sequenced next.)

**Test-first** (RED): `tests/unit/store-checkin-grid.test.tsx` ã opens a grid with
one draft row + `Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¿Á¡ÀÁ¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡È` add-row + disabled `Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¡Á¡Á¡ÑÁ¡Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¿Á¡Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡`; enables on a
complete row; records every complete row in one `recordStockInBulk` call; drops
incomplete rows. 4 RED ã green.

**DB:** new `record_stock_in_bulk(p_project_id uuid, p_lines jsonb)` definer RPC
(mig 20260813000800) ã same role gate as the post-197 `record_stock_in`
(site_admin + PM tier + procurement + director), membership (`can_see_project OR
procurement`), per-line validation (qty>0, costãË0, active item, supplier exists),
**atomic** (any bad line rolls back the whole batch ã no partial check-in), each
line inserts a `stock_receipts` row + rolls into `stock_on_hand`. Returns the
count. `CREATE` (new fn) + explicit grants (anon revoked). The single
`record_stock_in` is **KEPT** (spec 195 P3 auto-receipt depends on it). pgTAP 215
(plan 18): structure/anon-deny ôñ 2-line additive happy ôñ 7 validations ôñ atomicity
(good+bad line ã 0 receipts) ôñ visitor/non-member 42501 ôñ site_admin member happy.

**App:**

- `recordStockInBulk({ projectId, lines })` action (`src/app/store/actions.ts`) ã
  maps rows ã jsonb `[{catalog_item_id, qty, unit_cost, supplier_id, note}]`,
  calls the RPC, maps 42501/22023, `revalidatePath` the project store.
- `StoreManager` Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ý sheet rewritten as a draft-row grid (`DraftReceiptRow[]`
  state, `+ Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¿Á¡ÀÁ¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡È` add, per-row `Á¡ËÁ¡` remove, one `Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¡Á¡Á¡ÑÁ¡Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¿Á¡Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡` submit;
  enabled once ãË1 complete row; incomplete rows dropped on submit). Reuses the
  category-grouped item `<select>` per row. Swapped `recordStockIn`ã`recordStockInBulk`.
- Updated the two spec-177 `store-manager.test.tsx` Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ý tests to the grid
  (button `Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¡Á¡Á¡ÑÁ¡Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¿Á¡Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡`, asserts `recordStockInBulk` with a `lines` array).
- `db:types` regenerated (new RPC).

**U2 (pre-fill Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ý from a PO delivery ã incl. the anti-double-book rule vs

**Scope note / open question:** the spec describes Mode B as a "batch submit"
full-list form (every item with an inline counted-qty field, one submit). The
actual `/stock-count` component is **per-row** (a sheet per item) ã the spec
author's recollection of the existing surface was inaccurate. Per the spec's own
overriding rule ("no new store capability ã relocation + consolidation only"), I
**relocated the existing per-row component** rather than build a new batch form
(that would be new capability). If the operator genuinely wants a single-submit
batch grid, that is a follow-up spec, not U2.

`/stock-count?project=ãÎ` ã unreachable now (prod always passes `hidePicker`; the
standalone route redirects), but kept so the spec-178-B2 picker test stays green.

## Spec 197 ã Á¡Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡ as a per-project surface, U1 (2026-06-24)

## Spec 195 follow-up ã dashboard store-material spend (2026-06-24)

Status: **DONE ã 2026-06-24** (no DB; lint ôñ typecheck ôñ vitest 1575 green). Closes
the "Open follow-up" flagged in `docs/feature-specs/195-project-level-purchasing.md`:
the manager dashboard's materials-by-project showed direct WP-bound purchase spend
only, so a project that procures heavily **into the on-site store** read as
artificially low (the cost is real ã it sits in `wp_profit` + Store P&L, just not
on the dashboard). **Fix:** `materials` now adds the project's non-reversed
`stock_issues` (Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡) at **cost** (`total_cost`). Disjoint sources ã store-bound
material comes from WP-less PRs, which `sumMaterials` excludes (ADR 0063) ã so
additive with no double-count (mirrors `wp_profit`'s two-term materials, but at COST
not the sell layer: the dashboard is budget-vs-**money-out**, like labor-at-cost and
purchases-at-supplier-amount; the store's internal transfer margin is not external
spend). New pure helper `sumStoreIssues` (`src/lib/dashboard/spend.ts`, tested) +
two admin reads (`stock_issues` by project_id, `stock_reversals` for the non-reversed
filter) in `src/app/dashboard/page.tsx`. Test-first (dashboard-spend.test.ts).
**Open:** dashboard total ignores store stock procured-but-not-yet-Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡'d (inventory,
not yet WP-consumed) ã deliberate, consistent with the cost-at-usage model.

## Spec 194 ã super_admin override on an approved supply plan (2026-06-24)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-24** (commit 58dc371; mig 20260813000100; pgTAP
209; lint ôñ typecheck ôñ vitest 1567 ôñ db:test 159/0 green). Operator: a super_admin
should be able to revert the status / edit an approved (frozen) supply plan, with
the plan labeled "overridden by [name]" (chose **supply plans first** via
AskUserQuestion). The lifecycle is one-way past approval (PM submit ã PD/super
approve ã frozen; only rejected re-editable); this is the operator escape hatch.
**mig:** `supply_plans` += overridden_by / overridden_at; `reopen_supply_plan(plan)`
definer ã **super_admin only** ã reopens a submitted/approved plan to draft
(clearing the submit/approve stamps), recording overridden_by + overridden_at; the
marker PERSISTS through a later re-approval. **pgTAP 209** (super reopens, non-super
42501, draft can't reopen, execute lockdown). `reopenPlan` action + a "Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¿Á¡
(Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡ËÁ¡ÈÁ¡¯Á¡Á¡)" button on a frozen plan (canOverride = super) + a "ôñ Á¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¿Á¡Á¡Â [name]"
marker (name resolved via admin client). The pattern (reopen RPC + overridden_by
stamp + label) is reusable for other approved entities. **PAIRED REQUEST #1 ã supply
plan ã store redesign ã NOT built (design proposal presented, awaiting the
operator's direction):** the operator wants supply-plan items to procure into the
on-site STORE (project-level, no WP), then WPs Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡ (withdraw) per-WP ã moving WP
attribution to withdrawal (the store already does the Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡ half, spec 177). Key
fork = how procurement lands in the store (light: plan ã pre-filled stock-in; full:
project-level PRs ã PO ã receive-into-store, needs PR work_package_id nullable).

## Spec 192 ã first-real-project readiness, U1 (2026-06-24)

Status: **U1 SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-24** (commit 69d94b0, NO DB; lint ôñ typecheck

pivoted from feature-breadth to **adoption** (the app is feature-complete but

first real project producing data). Two cliffs mapped from the live code; U1 fixes
the **silent membership dead-end**: project visibility is membership-gated
(`can_see_project` = a `project_members` row OR the project_lead, ADR 0056), and
`removeProjectMember` had **no guard** ã a PM could remove the last member (or
themselves) and orphan the project (visible only to super_admin), with no in-app
recovery for the locked-out person. **Fix (invariant: a project keeps ãË1 member):**
`lib/projects/member-removal.ts` pure `evaluateMemberRemoval({totalMembers,
removingSelf})` ã `{blocked (last), needsConfirm (self + others remain)}`;
`removeProjectMember` counts first and refuses the last removal (load-bearing Thai
error); `settings-form.tsx` (+`currentUserId` prop) disables the last member's ã
with a hint, routes a self-removal through the themed `ConfirmDialog`
("ãÎÁ¡Á¡¡Á¡Á¡Á¡¯Á¿Á¡ÀÁ¿Á¿Á¡¨Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡Á¡ÈÁ¡Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡ÈÁ¡Á¡çÁ¿Á¡ÙÁ¡çÁ¡ãÎ"), keeps other-removal one-click, marks the current
user "(Á¡Á¡¡Á¡)". **NO migration** ã an action-level UX-footgun guard at the right
altitude (member ops are direct table writes under RLS, not RPCs; projects are
never hard-deleted, so no DELETE-cascade concern a DB trigger would hit). Tests:
`member-removal.test.ts` + 3 `settings-form.test.tsx` cases. **U2+ (next):**
onboarding leads with "add your team" (+ the visibility why); a non-member 404 ã
"ask a PM to add you" explainer (admin exists-check); a **site-admin daily-loop
home** (log labor/photos/PR in one tap) ã net-new surface, wants a mock-first pass.

## Spec 190 ã dark mode (opt-in night theme), U1 (2026-06-24)

Status: **U1 SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-24** (commit 40358c6, NO DB; lint ôñ typecheck
ôñ vitest 1528 green; verified light+dark via the SSR cookie path + preview
screenshots). Operator asked "how hard is dark mode in settings?" ã I assessed it
against the actual token system and recommended **default light + opt-in toggle**
(operator confirmed). Cheap because the design system was built for re-theming:
100% semantic tokens (enforced by `design-doctrine.test.ts`), OKLCH colors (dark =
invert the L channel, hue preserved), and `@custom-variant dark` already declared
(globals.css even comments "a future night-shift palette overrides :root"). So the
lift is a `.dark` palette + toggle plumbing ã **components are untouched.**
**Default LIGHT is deliberate** (spec-20 sun-first: dark is _worse_ in direct sun =
the field photo-capture flow; dark serves indoor/PM/back-office/portal/night). **U1:**
`lib/ui/theme.ts` (tri-state light/dark/system in a year `theme` cookie; pure
`resolveTheme`/`parseThemeSetting`, default light); no-flash (`layout.tsx` async,
reads the cookie server-side ã `dark` class + `color-scheme` on `<html>` pre-paint,
`ThemeScript` resolves `system` before paint, `suppressHydrationWarning`);
`globals.css` `.dark {}` overriding every `--color-*` + the shadcn primitives (OKLCH
dark, WCAG floors held, amber fill keeps near-black ink, `*-soft` grounds ã low-L
tints); `ThemeToggle` on `/settings` (`Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡ÈÁ¿Á¡ˆÁ¡Á¡Á¡Á¡Ë`, every role; Á¡ˆÁ¡ÏÁ¿Á¡ýÁ¡/Á¡ÀÁ¡ñÁ¡/Á¡ÈÁ¡¯Á¡Á¡, 44px,
tracks OS live on Á¡ÈÁ¡¯Á¡Á¡). Tests: `theme.test.ts`, `theme-toggle.test.tsx`. **TRAP:
the husky Tailwind class-sorter (`prettier-plugin-tailwindcss`) mangled the
whitespace around a `${ternary}` inside the `className` template literal ã
`antialiased${c?" dark":""}` became `antialiaseddark` (junk class; dark only
survived via the JS script, not SSR). Fix: keep the separator space in the STATIC
part of the literal (`antialiased ${c?"dark":""}`); re-read className literals after
the commit hook.** No new route; new components in the existing `features/chrome`
domain (no spec-122 change). **U2 (next, optional polish):** screen-by-screen audit
on authenticated surfaces (cards, `*-soft` status grounds, brand band), shadow/
elevation tuning for dark, PWA status-bar `themeColor` per theme.

## Spec 183 ã approvals are awareness, not a tab (PM) (2026-06-23)

Operator: "Á¡ÈÁ¡ÙÁ¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ÏÁ¡ menu should not be the main menu, but rather notification of
how many Approvals are pending." Design challenge ("don't agree blindly"). Verdict:
operator's instinct ~70% right ã a bottom tab is a _place_, the review queue is a
_transient, often-empty worklist_; the count is the actionable signal. But the
proposal tangles two jobs: **awareness** (count ã badge/card) and **doing the work**
(the queue needs a real home). Since approving IS the PM's primary job, we demote
the _tab-as-urgency-signal_, not the _queue-as-a-place_: relocate it onto the
dashboard (the new PM home) + count badge on the Á¡ Á¡ýÁ¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ÏÁ¡À nav. Operator delegated
placement ("design with ux in mind") and said other approval types get awareness
in later units. Mocked the before/after with show_widget before building.

3-unit arc: U1 count + dashboard hero card ôñ U2 drop the tab + reroute home + badge
pins ôñ U3 the nav count badge (self-fetching). U4+ = other approval types (PR,
bank/consent) ã later.

**U1 SHIPPED 2026-06-23 (NO DB).** `src/lib/approvals/pending-summary.ts`: pure
`summarizePendingApprovals(rows, projectsById)` ã `{count, oldest}` (oldest = min
updated_at, code tiebreak ã mirrors /review ordering) + async
`getPendingApprovalsSummary` (RLS-scoped, mirrors the /review queue query so count
== list). `features/dashboard/pending-approvals-card.tsx`: presentational, attention
(amber) palette when pending / calm muted when empty, links ã /review. Wired into
/dashboard for the PM tier only (site_admin sees the dashboard, not the card).
Tests: pending-approvals-summary (pure, 5) + pending-approvals-card (render, 3).
LESSON: a new `features/<domain>/` folder must be added to the
`feature-components-structure.test.ts` ALLOWED_DOMAINS allowlist (spec 122 guard) ã
caught by the full suite, not the targeted run. vitest 1489/0.

**U2 SHIPPED 2026-06-23 (NO DB).** The nav flip. Dropped `Á¡ÈÁ¡ÙÁ¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ÏÁ¡` from `PM_TABS`
(bottom-tab-bar) + `Á¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡ÈÁ¡ÈÁ¡ÙÁ¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ÏÁ¡` from `PM_HUB_NAV` (hub-nav). Rerouted `roleHome`
PM tier (isManagerRole) ã `/dashboard` (was `/review`). Gave `DASHBOARD_TAB`
`match: ["/review"]` so the queue lights Á¡ Á¡ýÁ¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ÏÁ¡À as its sub-surface (bottom bar);
`/review` page passes HubNav `currentHref="/dashboard"` for the same effect on
desktop. `/review` stays a live route reached from the U1 card. Removed the unused
`ClipboardCheck` import. Pin churn (all 5 located up-front): role-home, role-sets,
require-role (redirect target), hub-nav (PM_ITEMS + assertion), bottom-tab-bar
(PM_TABS pin + two Á¡ÈÁ¡ÙÁ¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ÏÁ¡-lighting cases rewritten to Á¡ Á¡ýÁ¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ÏÁ¡À). The `match` choice
minimized churn AND kept the sun-mode test green (it asserts an active tab exists on
/review ã Á¡ Á¡ýÁ¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ÏÁ¡À now provides it). vitest 1489/0; lintôñtc green.

**U3 SHIPPED 2026-06-23 (NO DB).** The count badge on the Á¡ Á¡ýÁ¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ÏÁ¡À bottom tab (PM
tier) ã the literal "number on the main menu" the operator asked for.
`features/dashboard/pending-approvals-badge.tsx` ('use client'): pure
`formatBadgeCount` (null at 0, cap 99+) + presentational `ApprovalsBadge({count})`

## Spec 174 ã project Google-Maps link (precise pin) (2026-06-22)

Operator: "Add Pinned map, or attach link from gMap." Chose (one question)
**attach a gMap link** ã paste the Maps "Share" URL on the project; the ã sheet's
"open in Maps" link opens the EXACT pin, replacing the spec-173 address-search
fallback. (Embedded pinned map declined ã needs an API key + coordinates.)

**SHIPPED to prod 2026-06-22.** **mig 20260798:** `projects.gmap_url` (nullable) +
CHECK https-only; DROP+CREATE `update_project_settings` with a trailing
`p_gmap_url` (mirrors site_address: null preserves, '' clears) + re-applied EXECUTE
grants. **mig 20260799:** grant SELECT on the column ã `projects` has COLUMN-level
SELECT grants (budget excluded), so the new column did NOT inherit SELECT; granted
authenticated + anon (mirrors site_address). **mig 20260800:** revoke anon EXECUTE
on the recreated RPC ã Supabase default privileges silently re-granted anon EXECUTE
on the DROP+CREATE'd function; the pre-174 RPC had anon revoked (pgTAP 32 pins it).
App: `validateGmapUrl` (https + Google host allowlist ã rejects javascript:,
non-https, look-alike domains, >2048); the form gains a URL field; `gmapUrl` rides
the single settings payload; the project detail page computes
`mapsUrl = gmap_url ?? address-search ?? null` for the existing ã link (no
component change). **LESSONS (both caught by db:test, fixed forward):** (1) a new
column on a column-SELECT-granted table does NOT inherit SELECT ã must grant
explicitly; (2) DROP+CREATE of an RPC re-triggers Supabase's default-privilege
EXECUTE grant to anon ã must revoke anon (CREATE OR REPLACE would have avoided
both, but a new param forces DROP+CREATE). pgTAP 32 (+3, 11-arg sig); unit
validateGmapUrl + settings-form (+1 each). db:types regenerated (signature change).
Verify: db:test 120 / 2301 / 0; pnpm test green; lintôñtypecheckôñbuild green. Builds
on [[spec173-procurement-project-visibility]].

## Spec 161 U10 - per-project defect clawback (ADR 0060 design-rule 1) (2026-06-21)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-21.** Completes the flagged follow-up (a defect-reopen claws back). Migrations `20260773000000_coin_postings_project.sql` + `20260773000100_project_coin_clawback.sql`. **Project tag:** `coin_postings.source_project_id` (nullable FKãprojects, additive); **`post_coins` gained `p_source_project uuid default null`** (DROP+CREATE ã a defaulted-param add via create-or-replace would make a 2nd overload + ambiguate the 4-named-arg callers; plpgsql callers bind at runtime so DROP is safe; only pgTAP 96's signature pin needed updating, calls use ãÊ5 positional args). **`distribute_project_coins` now TAGS** its profit_share postings (HT cut + DC shares) with the project. **`claw_back_project_coins(p_project, p_note)`** super-only: per worker, claws `least(project's REMAINING in-tail coins [signed öÈ of the project's in-window postings ã nets prior clawbacks ã idempotent], worker's total `coin_unvested_balance`)` as a negative `confiscation` (reason `defect_rework`, project-tagged) + a `coin_confiscations` row; per-worker advisory lock. **VESTED coins (past the tail) + OTHER projects' coins are never touched** (the trust invariant). **DECISION ã manual, NOT auto-fired from spec-144 reopen:** (a) a single-WP defect auto-clawing a whole project's distribution is too blunt; (b) reopen is site_admin/PM-callable but minting/forfeiting is super-only ã an auto-call hits the super gate or forces an ungated post_coins bypass. Operator claws back via this RPC (UI next). **pgTAP 110** (12: column + secdef; pmã42501; super claws P ã W1 keeps other-project Q coins [500] but loses P-unvested [1000ãbal 500], W2 P-unvested 800ã0, W3 P-coins VESTEDãuntouched 2000; 2 defect_rework confiscations + 2 project-tagged confiscation postings; idempotent re-run claws 0; unknownãP0001). Updated pgTAP 96 (post_coins 6-arg signature). **Verify:** lintôñtypecheckôñdb:test 110 files/2138/0ôñdb:typesôñtest. Lesson: adding a defaulted param to a function with named-arg callers needs DROP+CREATE (overload would ambiguate), grep the signature pins.

## Spec 161 hardening - coin-engine fixes from adversarial review (2026-06-21)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-21.** Migration `20260772000000_nova_hardening.sql` (5 create-or-replace, signatures unchanged ã grants kept; behaviour unchanged for 104-108). Post-arc adversarial review (3 `caveman:cavecrew-reviewer` agents over the engine SQL + UI) surfaced three real fixes (noise filtered: negative weights impossible via `nova_dials value>=0` CHECK; "vesting locks forever" was a backwards misread ã tail=0 ã fully vested; UI was clean). **A ã `settle_project`:** a MISSING `coin_multiplier` dial silently produced a NULL pool ã now guards ã P0001 (the dial is seeded + RPC-update-only, but a deleted dial must fail loud). **B ã `distribute_project_coins`:** per-worker `round()` drifted ã öÈ shares could over-mint or lose coins ã the LAST worker (by worker_id, via `row_number()/count() over()`) now takes the **exact remainder** (`v_dist ã öÈ allocated`) so **öÈ(minted) == pool EXACTLY**, never over-mints. **C ã TOCTOU race:** `redeem_shop_item`/`confiscate_coins`/`award_savers_bonus` did balance-check-then-post; two concurrent calls could both pass ã overspend/double-confiscate/double-bonus. SQL-only ã no JS/db:types delta. Lessons: per-row round() in a loop drifts ã allocate the last as remainder; balance-check-then-post needs a per-actor advisory lock.

## Spec 161 U6b - saver's bonus + vesting + narrow confiscation (ADR 0060 ôÏ6 + decision c) (2026-06-21)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-21.** Migrations `20260771000000_add_confiscation_coin_source.sql` (enum-add) + `20260771000100_nova_vesting.sql`. The **TRUST layer** (ADR 0061 "can't build inclusion on a currency people fear"; design-rules 1/6/7): **holding is safe.** **Vesting = time-based + external lock**, derived from posting age ã NO project link added to coin_postings (`post_coins` untouched). **`coin_unvested_balance(p_worker)`**: an **external** DC (contractor `dc_temporary`) ã the **whole balance** locked (ôÏ4, generalized ã unlocked only when invited internal); an **internal** DC ã `least(balance, öÈ positive postings within `vesting_tail_days`)` (recently-earned, still in the warranty/defect tail). **`coin_vested_balance`** = balance ã unvested; **`coin_spendable_balance`** = vested (so external spendable = 0). All SECURITY DEFINER + **super/director gate** (null-safe, no PM ã 90/91 untouched). **`redeem_shop_item` REPLACED** (same signature, grants kept) to spend only `coin_spendable_balance` ã the lock is now REAL (U6a built it on the full balance). **Narrow confiscation** (decision c): `confiscation_reason` enum = `('fraud','theft','gross_misconduct','defect_rework')` ã the 3 gross violations + the quality clawback (design-rule 1; same mechanism, distinct reason; **no catch-all `other`** ã never arbitrary) + a new `confiscation` `coin_source` (2nd sink, own enum-add). **`confiscate_coins(p_worker, p_reason, p_note)`** SECURITY DEFINER **super-only**; forfeits **only `coin_unvested_balance`** (vested NEVER touched ã the trust invariant); `unvested ãÊ 0` ã P0001 (fully-vested worker is safe); posts negative `confiscation` + records `coin_confiscations` (append-only, super-read). **`award_savers_bonus(p_worker)`** SECURITY DEFINER super-only; `bal û savers_bonus_rate`; rewards **continued holding** ã first bonus allowed, a later one blocked if a `shop_redemption` posted since the last `savers_bonus` (P0001 'spent since last bonus'); cadence operator-driven. **New seeded dials (PLACEHOLDERS):** `vesting_tail_days 365`, `savers_bonus_rate 0.02`.

## Spec 161 U5 - coin distribution: distribute_project_coins (ADR 0060 ôÏ4) (2026-06-21)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-21.** Migration `20260769000000_coin_distribution.sql`. Turns the U4b settlement **pool** into postings on the spec-160 coin ledger. ADR 0060 ôÏ4: **HT takes a cut off the top** (`ht_cut_pct` dial); the **rest splits by LEVEL WEIGHT** among the DCs who worked the project (SeniorãApprentice; **internal > external**; externals a **flat, level-blind** share). Formulaic from `labor_logs` (the ôÏ5 anti-favoritism pillar ã no subjective input). **A DC's share FOLLOWS THEM across project moves** ã the weight reads `labor_logs` (where work was done), never `workers.project_id`. **`distribute_project_coins(p_project) returns table(ht_coins, dc_distributed, dc_count, total_distributed)`** SECURITY DEFINER ôñ **super_admin ONLY** (minting = peak operator authority ã the `post_coins`/`set_nova_dial` gate; deliberately NOT super+director like U4b settlement, because distribution REUSES `post_coins` which is super-only ã a definer-to-definer call resolves the original caller's role, so a director would hit 42501; null-safe `is distinct from`, **no PM ref ã 90/91 untouched**) ã 42501. Project exists ã P0001; **must be settled** (a `project_settlements` row ã else P0001 'not settled'); **idempotent** (a `project_coin_distributions` row ã P0001 'already distributed'). HT cut = `pool û ht_cut_pct` ã `post_coins(ht,'profit_share',ãÎ)`; distributable = pool ã cut; per-DC `weight = (external? external_factor : level_weight[level]) û days` over CURRENT (non-superseded) DC labor on the project's WPs, **excluding the HT** (no double-dip); a **window `sum(weight) over ()`** over the `weight > 0` set gives öÈweight (ungraded `level NULL` ã weight 0 ã filtered, never dilutes); each DC's `coins = round(distributable û weight/öÈweight, 4)` ã `post_coins(dc,'profit_share',ãÎ)` (source **already in the enum**, no enum-add). Records `project_coin_distributions` (project_id PK = idempotency key; coin_pool/ht_worker_id/ht_coins/dc_distributed/dc_count; **zero authenticated grant**); audits (generic `update`).

**Internal vs external** = the DC's tenure: a worker whose contractor is `contractor_subtype='dc_temporary'` is EXTERNAL; null/other contractor ã INTERNAL (ADR 0060 ôÏ1, the `dc_regular`/`dc_temporary` subtypes; no-contractor DC defaults internal, like `wp_economics.is_external`). **New seeded dials (decision a ã PLACEHOLDERS, operator must calibrate before go-live):** `ht_cut_pct 0.15`, `level_weight_senior 4 / mid 3 / junior 2 / apprentice 1`, `external_factor 1` (< every internal weight ã internal > external). Externals' **invisible + lock** posture: U5 only POSTS; coins already super-only-read (externals can't see them, spec 160 U3) and the **spend lock** lands in U6b. **pgTAP 106** (19 asserts: catalog + secdef; money posture; gate super-only [directorôñpmôñvisitor 42501]; not-settledãP0001; pool 10000, ht_cut 0.2, weights senior 4/mid 2, external_factor 2 ã HT 2000 (cut only, no double-dip), senior 4000, mid 2000 [share follows them ã now on another project], external 2000 [flat level-blind], ungraded 0; recorded ht_coins 2000ôñdc_distributed 8000ôñdc_count 3; total minted = pool 10000; idempotent re-distributeãP0001; unknownãP0001). **Verify:** lintôñtypecheckôñ**db:test 106 files/2073/0**ôñdb:typesôñtest 188/1268 ã all green. **U5 spec detail authored first.** **NEXT = U6a Nova shop** (shop_items + redeem + 'shop_redemption' coin_source) ã U6b saver-bonus + vesting + confiscation. LESSON: reuse `post_coins` from a definer needs the SAME (super-only) gate, else 42501 cascade.

## Spec 161 U4b - project settlement engine: settle_project (ADR 0060 ôÏ3 model-b) (2026-06-20)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-20.** Migration `20260768000000_settlement_engine.sql` (sequenced **above** the concurrent spec 146 U3 equipment block `20260767*`). ADR 0060 ôÏ3 model-b: WPs bank profit as they complete; the **whole project settles ONCE at close** ã `coin_pool = öÈ banked WP profit û coin_multiplier` (U4a dial). Produces the pool **number** + a **frozen snapshot**; distribution = U5. **DECISION ã bank-at-SETTLEMENT with a frozen snapshot (not a completion trigger):** a completion trigger fires under whoever flips the WP status (usually a site_admin on photo-approval) and would call the super/director-gated `wp_profit`/`wp_labor_sell` ã **42501**, forcing an ungated refactor of shipped U3/U3b + failing the completion tx. Instead `settle_project` is an explicit super/director action **at close** that calls `wp_profit` **in its designed caller context** (gate passes) and FREEZES each completed WP's profit into `wp_profit_bank` ã so post-settlement corrections can't move settled coins (U5 reads the frozen bank, never live `wp_profit`). Trade-off accepted: a correction between WP-complete and project-close IS reflected (correct); defect-rework-before-close handled naturally (a WP in 'rework' isn't 'complete' ã excluded). **`settle_project(p_project) returns table(coin_pool, banked_profit_total, coin_multiplier, wp_banked_count, wp_skipped_null_budget_count, equipment_costed)`** SECURITY DEFINER ôñ super+director null-safe `is distinct from` (no PM ref ã **90/91 untouched**) ã 42501; project exists ã P0001; **closed-only** (`status in ('completed','archived')`) ã P0001; **idempotent** (a `project_settlements` row exists ã P0001 'already settled'). Loops WPs `status='complete'`, calls `wp_profit`; **budget-NULL (profit NULL) ã SKIP + COUNT** (`wp_skipped_null_budget_count`, never silently 0); else **freezes** a `wp_profit_bank` row + sums; `coin_pool = total û multiplier`; audits (generic `update`). **`project_settlements`** (project_id PK = idempotency key; coin_multiplier/banked_profit_total/coin_pool/counts/equipment_costed/settled_by) + **`wp_profit_bank`** (frozen 6 wp_profit components per WP, unique per WP) ã both **zero authenticated grant** (money). **Equipment gap CLOSED** by the concurrent spec 146 U3 (`wp_profit` now folds in `wp_equipment_sell`) ã `equipment_costed` aggregates **true**; pool no longer provisional.

**pgTAP 104** (20 asserts: catalog project_settlements+PK / wp_profit_bank / settle_project secdef; money posture both tables; gate pmôñsaôñvisitorã42501; closed project w/ WP-1 budget 5000+senior-full labor 800ãprofit 4200, WP-2 4000ã4000, WP-3 complete-no-budgetãSKIPPED, WP-4 in_progressãignored, multiplier 2.0 ã banked 8200ôñpool 16400ôñbanked_count 2ôñskipped 1ôñequipment_costed trueôñ2 bank rows; director settles a 2nd closed project; idempotent re-settleãP0001; active projectãP0001; unknownãP0001). **Verify:** lintôñtypecheckôñ**db:test 105 files/2054/0**ôñdb:typesôñ**test [vitest]** ã all green. **U4b spec detail authored first.** **CONCURRENCY EVENT:** the spec 146 U3 equipment session was building in the SAME tree + remote DB ã collided on migration version 20260766000000 + pgTAP 104, and its `wp_profit_with_equipment` REPLACE changed the foundation. Operator confirmed (AskUserQuestion) the equipment session finished ã I renumbered above it (768), repaired the orphan remote `20260766000000` (`supabase migration repair --status reverted` ã my botched first-push left a phantom version whose create-table tx rolled back), and built ON the equipment-aware `wp_profit`. **First-RED bug:** seeded projects as 'completed' THEN inserted WPs ã spec-145 trigger `P0002 cannot add a WP to a closed project`; fix = seed active, add WPs, then close. **NEXT = U5 distribution** (HT cut + level-weight split ã coin_postings via post_coins). LESSON: `wp_profit%rowtype` fails (it's a fn, not a relation) ã use `record`; a live concurrent session in one tree/DB = the [[concurrent-session-hazard]] (check list_sessions, renumber, migration-repair the orphan).

## Spec 146 U3 - equipment usage logs: check-out/check-in ã per-WP charge ã wp_profit (ADR 0055 + ADR 0060 ôÏ2) (2026-06-20)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-20** (commits ba8a52d feat ôñ 115d6ab director-fix ôñ 6ed8af0 types; migrations 20260767000000ã000400). Closes the spec 161 U3b equipment gap (`equipment_cost=0`/`equipment_costed=false`): attribute equipment to a WP via a **check-out/check-in usage log**, derive a **per-WP equipment charge live**, wire into `wp_profit`. **Verify:** lintôñtypecheckôñtest **188/1268**ôñdb:push (5 migrations)ôñdb:types (app+worker)ôñ**db:test 105 files (104 passed; my 105=41/41, 102/90/91/86 all green)** ã the **1 failure is `104-settlement-engine.test.sql`, the CONCURRENT session's in-progress file, NOT mine** (its closed-project seed bug; not in any of my commits). **Operator picks (this session, via AskUserQuestion):** (1) granularity = **check-out ã check-in SPAN** (one row/checkout, billed whole days on site û daily rate), NOT row-per-day; (2) the WP is charged the **CHARGE-OUT daily rate computed LIVE** (transfer price, symmetric with DC labor @ SELL; PRC keeps the margin over the batch cost ã Case A + ADR 0060 ôÏ2), NOT a GL-allocated batch-cost share. **This REVISES the roadmap-table U3/U4 sketch** (was per-day log + frozen `wp_equipment_costs`): the live `wp_profit` reuses live reads (`wp_labor_sell`), never the frozen snapshot, so the frozen `wp_equipment_costs`/`freeze_wp_equipment_cost` (old U4) is deferred to budget-vs-spend + a WP-dimensioned equipment GL posting (later seam). **No new GL account this unit** ã the charge-out is a number the GL doesn't hold (GL holds batch COST at batch grain), so computing it live from the usage logs is the transfer-price layer, NOT a second costing path (exactly like `wp_labor_sell` vs the GL's labor COST).

**Builds:** `equipment_usage_logs` (append-only, supersede; `item_id`/`work_package_id` WP-grain/`checked_out_on`/`checked_in_on` null=open/`daily_rate_snapshot` MONEY zero-grant/`superseded_by`/`correction_reason` nullable ã NO `reason-iff-superseded` CHECK since check-in is the first supersede; CHECK inãËout; column-scoped SELECT omitting the rate, like `labor_logs`; append-only block trigger) ôñ `check_out_equipment(item,wp,date)` (gate site_admin/pm/procurement/super; per-item advisory lock; item must be priced + WP not complete + no existing open checkout for the item ã P0001) ôñ `check_in_equipment(log,date)` (closes the open row via a superseding closed successor; in<out ã P0001; re-check-in of closed/superseded ã P0001) ôñ `wp_equipment_sell(p_wp)` (mirror `wp_labor_sell`: super+director gate null-safe, öÈ over CURRENT rows of `greatest((coalesce(checked_in_on,current_date)ãchecked_out_on)+1,0) û daily_rate_snapshot` ã whole days inclusive, open accrues to today, no internal/external branch) ôñ `wp_profit` REPLACE (same signature; `equipment_cost = wp_equipment_sell`, `equipment_costed = true`). pgTAP **file 105** (104 taken by a concurrent Spec 161 U4b settlement-engine session ã renumbered; my migrations likewise 20260766ã20260767 around their pushed settlement_engine) + update `102-wp-profit` (`equipment_costed` falseãtrue). Spec 146 U3 detail authored first.

**ADR 0058 fix (migration 20260767000400):** the check_out/check_in RPC gates + the `equipment_usage_logs` read policy initially named `project_manager` WITHOUT `project_director` ã **pgTAP 90 + 91 (the see-all-PM completeness invariants) caught it** on the first GREEN db:test. Lesson re-confirmed: **any new gate/policy naming project_manager must also name project_director** ([[spec152-project-director-role]]). **Concurrent-session reconciliation:** the half-applied push (table created but unrecorded after the 20260766 collision) was repaired via `supabase migration repair --status applied 20260767000000` then push-the-rest ã NOT a re-create (verified table+fn+trigger+policy+grants all present first via `supabase db query`).

## Spec 161 U4a - settlement multiplier dial: nova_dials (ADR 0060 ôÏ3 + decision a) (2026-06-20)

Per **build-decision (a)** (every dial = editable seeded data, tune anytime) the multiplier ships as a **seeded editable dial**, not a constant ã the settlement engine (U4b) reads it. **`nova_dials`** = the one **key/value home for every economic dial** (the literal ADR-decision-a shape; HT cut % + level weights [U5] + saver-bonus rate [U6] land here as seeded rows in their units): `dial_key text PK`, `value numeric(20,4) ãË0`, updated_by/at. **MONEY/economics posture: zero authenticated grant** (operator reads via admin client behind requireRole; U4b engine reads via definer; setter is sole writer). **Seeded `('coin_multiplier', 1.0)`** ã placeholder (1 baht banked profit ã 1 coin point; coins=abstract points no peg, decision b); **operator MUST calibrate vs utilization before go-live** (standing markup-% open dial ã flagged, not blocking: mechanism ships, number tuned). **`set_nova_dial(p_key,p_value)`** SECURITY DEFINER **super_admin-only** (operator economics, anti-favoritism ôÏ5, like sell-rate dials; null-safe `is distinct from`; **no PM ref ã 90/91 untouched**) ã 42501; valueãË0 (P0001); **update-only on a SEEDED key** (typo'd key ã P0001, no phantom dials); audits (generic `update` action, target nova_dials, payload key+old+new ã no enum-add). **U4a = the dial ONLY**; the settlement math (öÈ wp_profit û multiplier ã pool) + banking-at-completion = **U4b**, mirrors U1-dials-before-U3-read.

**pgTAP 103** (13 asserts: catalog table+dial_key PK+value col+set_nova_dial secdef; seed coin_multiplier=1.0; money posture authenticated-no-SELECT; super tunes to 1.5 + reads back + audited once; negativeãP0001; unknown keyãP0001; pmôñvisitorã42501). ## Spec 161 U3b - WP profit assembly: wp_profit, materials from GL (ADR 0060 ôÏ2 + ADR 0057) (2026-06-20)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-20.** Migration `20260764000000_wp_profit.sql`. Assembles the ôÏ2 read `profit = budget ã labor_sell ã materials ã equipment`, **exposing every term** (returns table). **`wp_profit(p_wp uuid) returns table(budget, labor_sell, materials_cost, equipment_cost, equipment_costed, profit)`** SECURITY DEFINERôñstableôñpinned search_path. **budget** = wp_economics.budget (NULL until PD sets ã profit NULL). **labor_sell** = `wp_labor_sell(p_wp)` REUSED (definer-to-definer: caller's role resolves so its identical super/director gate passes ã no re-impl). **materials_cost DERIVED FROM THE GL** (ADR 0057, NOT a re-sum of purchase_requests): `öÈ(debitãcredit)` on `journal_lines` for the WP on WIP account **1400**, restricted to PURCHASE-sourced entries via `coalesce(orig.source_table, e.source_table)='purchase_requests'` (`left join journal_entries orig on orig.id=e.reversal_of`) ã **reversal-safe** (a reversal carries source_table 'journal_reversal' but copies work_package_id + swaps debit/credit, so an auto-corrected purchase nets via reversal_ofãoriginal's source; verified `post_purchase_to_gl` reverse-and-reposts). **Labor also debits 1400 but EXCLUDED** (source wp_labor_costs); VAT (1300) + equipment (no WP dim) naturally excluded. **profit = budgetãlabor_sellãmaterialsãequipment, NULL if budget NULL.** Gate **super_admin+project_director** (no PM ref ã 90/91 untouched), null-safe `is distinct from` (NULL-role denied) ã 42501; unknown WP ã P0001; execute revoke-public/grant-authenticated; read ã no audit/enum.

**EQUIPMENT GAP (operator-confirmed via AskUserQuestion 2026-06-20 ã chose "build profit w/o equipment, flag it"):** investigation (Explore agent + verified by hand) found `post_rental_batch_to_gl` ([20260743000100:176-178]) posts a rental batch to WIP 1400 at **batch grain with NO work_package_id (nor project_id)** ã equipment cost is **not WP-dimensioned in the GL**, can't be derived per-WP today. Splitting a batch across a project's WPs needs a **business allocation rule** = a follow-up spec touching the equipment poster / ADR 0055 (operator decision). U3b does NOT improvise it (scope rule + "discovering a missing requirement mid-unit isn't license to expand"): **equipment_cost=0 + equipment_costed=false** so the omission is LOUD, never folded silently. U4 minting is blocked anyway ã no payout rides on the partial figure. Profit is OVERSTATED by missing equipment until that follow-up.

**pgTAP 102** (18 asserts: catalog has_function+secdef; gate super+director read / pmôñsaôñvisitor 42501; WP-A all 6 components [budget 5000ôñlabor_sell 800ôñmaterials 1000 (labor 1400 entry EXCLUDED)ôñequipment 0ôñequipment_costed falseôñprofit 3200]; WP-B reversal-safe materials [2000ã2000+1500=1500, profit 2500]; WP-C budget-null ã budget NULL + profit NULL; unknown WP P0001). Journal rows seeded directly (accounting_period 2099-12 + journal_entries/lines, gl_accounts by code) to isolate from the poster machinery. Verify: lintôñtypecheckôñtest **188/1268**ôñdb:pushôñ**db:test 102 files/1980/0** (was 1962 ã +18)ôñdb:types (`wp_profit` added) ã all green. **U3b spec detail authored first.** **NEXT = equipment-per-WP follow-up spec** (allocation rule, gated on operator basis) + **U4 settlement û project multiplier** (gated on utilization data for markup-%/multiplier). LESSONS: reversal entries carry source_table='journal_reversal' (not the original's) but COPY work_package_id + swap debit/credit ã net via reversal_ofãorig.source_table; labor + materials BOTH hit WIP 1400 ã must isolate by source, not account alone.

## Spec 161 U3 - WP labor priced at SELL: wp_labor_sell (ADR 0060 ôÏ2) (2026-06-20)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-20.** Migration `20260763000000_wp_labor_sell.sql`. The **novel core** of the ôÏ2 profit engine ã `WP profit = budget ã (equipment + DC labor @ SELL + materials)` ã built as **only** the SELL-priced DC-labor term (the one number no existing fn produces; `freeze_wp_labor_cost` sums the same logs at COST). **`wp_labor_sell(p_wp uuid) returns numeric`** SECURITY DEFINER ôñ `stable` ôñ pinned search_path. Sums over **CURRENT** labor_logs (anti-join + tombstone filter, ADR 0009 ã mirrors the cost engine) where `worker_type_snapshot='dc'` (own labor = payroll overhead, NOT transfer-priced ã excluded, as it's absent from the ôÏ2 formula), valued at the worker's per-level sell rate: `(fullã1, halfã0.5) û (internal_sell unless wp_economics.is_external ã external_sell)`; `coalesce(ãÎ,0)`. **is_external** = `coalesce((select is_external from wp_economics where wp=p_wp), false)` (no row = internal, U2 posture). **Ungraded DC ã 0** ã the inner join to `sell_rate_table` drops a NULL-level worker, so an ungraded DC can never silently inflate profit; **decision: contribute 0, no side-effect flag** (pure read; surfacing the ungraded-DC-day count = U3b's profit struct). **Level = live grade** (labor_logs has no level snapshot; level-at-time = later refinement, noted). **Gate super_admin + project_director only** (no project_manager ref ã ADR 0058 pgTAP 90/91 untouched); **null-safe `is distinct from` form** denies NULL-role/service-role (rls-self-check-coalesce trap) ã 42501; unknown WP ã P0001 (typo errors, never a misleading 0). Reads zero-grant money tables (definer bypasses RLS); **invoked under the caller's authed session** (real super/director JWT so current_user_role() resolves), never the admin client ã like freeze. Execute lockdown: `revoke all from public; grant execute to authenticated`. Pure read ã **no audit, no enum-add**. **pgTAP 101** (12 asserts: has_function+secdef; gate super+director pass / pmôñsite_adminôñvisitor 42501; internal WP senior-full 800 + mid-half 350 = **1150**; same crew external = **1375** and `>` internal; edge WP = **290** [only junior current-half counts: ungradedã0, own-with-level excluded, superseded-old excluded, tombstone excluded]; unknown WP P0001). Verify: lintôñtypecheckôñtest **188/1268**ôñdb:pushôñ**db:test 101 files/1962/0** (was 1950 ã +12)ôñdb:types (`wp_labor_sell` added) ã all green. **Spec U3 detail authored first** (like U1/U2/U2b). **NEXT = U3b** full profit assembly (subtract equipment [spec 141/146] + materials [purchasing] from `wp_economics.budget`, **reconcile to GL** ADR 0057 ã derive from, not a second costing path) ã U4 settlement û project multiplier ã U5 coin distribution ã U6 shop. **Open dial (flag, not blocking):** markup % still wants real **utilization data** for a solvent default ã rates are editable/seeded, so the mechanism is built; operator should sanity-check sell rates vs actual billable-vs-idle DC-days before go-live.

**U2 detail (SHIPPED 2026-06-20):** migration `20260758000000_create_coin_ledger.sql`. Realizes ADR 0061 invariants 2+3 ã the event-sourced coin-ledger spine, **NO economics** (sources named not valued; no value/earn-rules/settlement/shop/vesting/dials). `coin_source` **enum** (`profit_share`/`savers_bonus`/`behavior_bonus`; pluggable via future `add value`); append-only **`coin_postings`** (`worker_id` FK / `source` / `amount numeric(20,4)` **signed** ã clawback = negative posting, not an edit / `reason` nonblankãÊ500 / `occurred_at` / `created_by` / `created_at`; checks amountã 0 + reason; index worker+occurred_at). **Money/authority posture:** RLS on, `revoke all`, **zero write grant (RPC-only)**, SELECT policy **super_admin-only** (worker-sees-own waits for U3 portal); **self-auditing** like equipment_movements ã no audit_log row, no audit_action. **`coin_balance(worker) numeric`** = `coalesce(sum(amount),0)` ã **SECURITY INVOKER** so it respects the read policy (non-operator sees 0, no leak); **balance always derived, never stored**. **`post_coins(worker,source,amount,reason,occurred_at)`** SECURITY DEFINER pinned search_path, gate **`current_user_role() is distinct from 'super_admin'`** (null-safe ã the rls-self-check-coalesce trap; a single `<>` would open on NULL) ã 42501; validates worker-exists/amountã 0/reason (P0001); inserts with `created_by=auth.uid()`. **No `project_manager` in any gate/policy ã ADR 0058 invariants (pgTAP 90/91) not triggered** (lesson applied from U1 ã super_admin-only is intentional). **pgTAP 96** (28 asserts: catalog table+cols+FK+enum labels; append-only no U/D/INSERT priv; secdef + coin_balance exists; super postsãbalance 100ã150; negative clawback netsã120; ledger grew to 3; zero-amount/blank-reason/unknown-worker P0001; pm/sa/visitor 42501; super reads / non-operator reads 0 via RLS). Verify: lintôñtypecheckôñtest **187/1264**ôñdb:pushôñ**db:test 96 files/1888/0**ôñdb:types ã all green.

**U3 detail (SHIPPED 2026-06-20):** migration `20260759000000_crew_assignments_portal.sql` (read-only RPC, no table/grant change). Realizes ADR 0061 invariant 5/6 (portal = worker's home) as the **first Stage-0 step**: the external DC portal (`/portal`, ADR 0051) crew list now shows **each member's current project** (U1 `workers.project_id`) ã record, not coin. **`get_my_crew_assignments()`** SECURITY DEFINER, returns `(worker_id,name,active,project_id,project_code,project_name)` for the caller's OWN crew (`workers.contractor_id = current_user_contractor_id()`, ADR 0051 binding), left-joined to `projects` ã the definer join lets an external contractor read **only their assigned projects' names** past the staff-scoped projects RLS; unbound/staff caller (NULL binding) ã zero rows; `revoke public/anon, grant execute authenticated` (get_my_dc_payments posture). **`loadPortalData` swaps the crew RLS query for the RPC** (fan size + concurrency unchanged); portal renders project under each crew name or "Á¡ÂÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡ÀÁ¿Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡Á¡°Á¡¨Á¡Á¡Á¿Á¡Á¡ÈÁ¡Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡È" (graceful pre-backfill, like the picker). **COINS DELIBERATELY EXCLUDED from the portal** ã ADR 0060 ôÏ4 makes external DCs' coins **invisible** (unlock only on Internal invite) + ADR 0061 **gift-first** (first experience = record, not the opaque coin); `coin_postings` stays super_admin-only. **pgTAP 97** (10 asserts: secdef; contractor A sees only own crew + project code/name resolved; never B's crew; B sees own + null project when unassigned; unbound/staff ã 0 rows). **vitest** load-portal-data (crew fan member = RPC, assignment shape). Verify: lintôñtypecheckôñtest **187/1264**ôñdb:pushôñ**db:test 97 files/1898/0**ôñdb:types ã all green. **Verified-by-checklist** (portal auth-gated ã preview /login on cloud PC; pgTAP carries RPC security; operator on-device = acceptance).

**STAGE 0 COMPLETE (U1+U2+U3).** **Open / next (own units):** **backfill existing DCs' `project_id`** (data-only ã BLOCKED on operator's DCãproject mapping; lights up both the spec 158 U2 picker's in-project section AND the U3 portal crew-project line). **Worker-sees-own-coins** on the portal ã deferred to the Internal-invite / policy-evolution step (ADR 0060 ôÏ4 + invariant 6); not built. **Economics** (coin value/earn-rules/settlement/shop/vesting, ADR 0060 dials) ã the next major arc, all deferred per ADR 0061 build order until the dials are tuned with the operator. Spec 158 U3 (SA-adds-DC-on-spot; operator sign-off first).

## Spec 159 U1 - subcontractor vs DC terminology consistency (2026-06-20)

Status: COMPLETE (pending full-suite green + commit). Operator: "DC setting is confusing ã Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡ý/DC, Á¡Á¡çÁ¡ÀÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡." Root cause: **"Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡ý" overloaded 3 ways** ã (1) general WP contractor [LEAVE, operator], (2) subcontractor `category=contractor` [firm pays its own crew], (3) DC `category=dc` [PRC pays directly] mislabeled Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡ý on several surfaces. **Taxonomy already exists** (`contractor_category` + `contractor_subtype` enums; Contacts tabs render DC Á¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ÇÁ¡ˋÁ¡ÝÁ¡/Á¡Á¡ÈÁ¡¯Á¡Á¡°/Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¿Á¡ÏÁ¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡Ï) ã NO schema change. **U1:** SSOT `SUBCONTRACTOR_LABEL = "Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡ýÁ¡Á¿Á¡ÏÁ¡"` in labels.ts; rewired the 4 subcontractor surfaces to it (contacts-tabs TAB*LABEL.contractors + CONTRACTOR_FIELDS name + addLabel; contacts/crews title+h1; contacts/[type]/[id] TYPE_CONFIG label; settings crews door label+hint ã kills the `Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡ý/DC` slash-merge ã `Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡ýÁ¡Á¿Á¡ÏÁ¡ / DC`). DC tab/subtypes untouched (already consistent). **CAUGHT: "Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡ý" is a SUBSTRING of "Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡ýÁ¡Á¿Á¡ÏÁ¡"** ã consistency guards assert presence-of-Á¡Á¿Á¡ÏÁ¡ / absence-of-exact-merged-string, never absence-of-Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡ý. **TDD:** source-guard `contact-subcontractor-label.test.ts` (SSOT value; 4 surfaces reference the constant; settings no longer has `Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡ý/DC`). First test wrongly asserted the literal ã but SSOT means surfaces hold the \_constant name*, so the guard checks constant usage (the stronger anti-drift check).

**Open questions (OUT ã own units):** **U2 DC-side de-Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡ý** ã labor-cost-view (`dc: "Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡ý"`, `Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡ý (DC)`), /payroll ("Á¡Á¿Á¡ýÁ¿Á¡ÈÁ¡Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡ý"), the DC-worker **parent picker** (worker-roster-manager + workers/actions + group-workers UNKNOWN label), the DC **portal** ("Á¡Á¡ÙÁ¡ÈÁ¿Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¡ËÁ¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡ý"), the role label `contractor: "Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡ý (DC)"` all still call a DC "Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡ý"; needs the operator's chosen DC-crew word (e.g. Á¡Á¡çÁ¡À DC / Á¡ˆÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¡ DC) first. ## Spec 157 - delete an empty work package (Tier 1) (2026-06-20)

Status: COMPLETE (pending suite green + commit). ADR 0059 ôÏ3. First delete path for WPs. `delete_work_package(p_work_package_id)` SECURITY DEFINER RPC: gate pm/super/**director** + `can_see_wp()`; **refuses (P0001) if ANY child exists** (photo_logs / labor_logs / approvals / purchase_requests / work_package_members / dependencies) else deletes; writes an audit_log row (event wp_deleted + code/name). Server action `delete-actions.ts` maps P0001 ã "cancel instead" message; `WpDeleteControl` (ConfirmDialog, no window.confirm) in the manager-only block, navigates to /projects/[id] on success (the WP is gone ã router.refresh would 404). **TDD:** pgTAP `94` (15 asserts: catalog, FK-blocks-delete, pm empty-delete+gone+audit, super+director see-all, photo/labor/PR ã P0001 + survives, sa-member+visitor role-deny, non-member pm membership-deny) + vitest `wp-delete-control` (confirmãdeleteãnavigate; historyãinline error+no-nav).

**KEY CORRECTION ã the FK premise was wrong.** The investigation + ADR 0059 + spec 157 claimed `labor_logs.work_package_id` was a **bare column with no FK** (orphan risk) needing an "adjacent FK migration." **It already HAS an FK** (`references work_packages(id)`, NO ACTION ã blocks WP delete with 23503; migration 20260619000300 line 22). So spec 157 dropped the FK migration ã **one migration only** (the RPC). ADR 0059 + spec 157 amended in place with correction notes. The empty-guard is still essential anyway: without it, deleting a WP would CASCADE-delete its purchase_requests / members / dependencies (silent data loss) and abort on the append-only photo_logs/approvals triggers. LESSON: verify FK existence by reading the table migration, not a summary ã `references` on the column line is the FK.

**Verify:** db:push (prod) + db:test (file 94) + db:types + lint + typecheck + full test ã green (below).

**Open questions (OUT):** **Tier 2 cancel/restore** for WPs WITH history (`cancelled` status enum value + exclusion from lenses/progress ã own spec, own enum migration); cascade/bulk delete; un-delete (gone is gone ã that's why Tier 2 exists). **ADR 0059 ôÏConsequences "labor_logs FK debt" is now void** (FK exists).

## Spec 155 - bind a work package to a deliverable (2026-06-20)

Status: COMPLETE (pending full-suite green + commit). ADR 0059 ôÏ1. Closes the gap: `work_packages.deliverable_id` was settable ONLY by the manual seed script ã no post-create write path, so in-app WPs were permanently ungrouped. Added `set_work_package_deliverable(p_work_package_id, p_deliverable_id)` SECURITY DEFINER RPC: gate pm/super/**project_director** + `can_see_wp()` membership (ADR 0056/0058, the reopen precedent); NULL = ungroup; a non-null deliverable must share the WP's project (cross-project/unknown ã 22023); no audit (benign metadata). Server action `deliverable-actions.ts` + a manager-only `WpDeliverableControl` native-select on the WP-detail page (Á¡ÂÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡ÀÁ¿Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¡Á¡Á¡ËÁ¡¡Á¿Á¡À + each Á¡Á¡ÏÁ¡Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡); loader gained `deliverable_id`; the project's deliverables ride alongside the loader (planner-gated, no waterfall). **TDD:** pgTAP `92` (13 asserts: catalog, pm-member bind/clear, super + director see-all, cross-project/unknown 22023, sa-member + visitor role-deny 42501, non-member pm membership-deny 42501) + vitest `wp-deliverable-control.test.tsx` (renders ungrouped+each, binds chosen id, clears to null). **Verify:** db:push (prod) + db:test **92 files / 1809 / 0** + db:types + lint + typecheck green.

**Two deviations from the spec doc (both deliberate):** (1) unknown WP ã **42501** (membership gate runs first; can_see_wp is false for a missing WP ã we don't disclose existence to non-members), NOT the doc's "false". (2) Took **two migrations** ã `20260753000000` (RPC) then `20260753000100` (CREATE OR REPLACE adding `p_deliverable_id uuid default null`) ã because supabase typegen marks a no-default arg as required non-null `string`, so the server action couldn't pass null; the default makes it optional ã the house omit-to-clear idiom (set_work_package_schedule). **Lesson: a nullable RPC arg the app must pass NULL/omit needs `default null` so typegen marks it optional ã author it in the first migration.** Transient `cli_login_postgres` SASL circuit-breaker hit when db:push ran concurrent with db:test ã retry alone clears it; don't run two supabase CLI ops at once.

**Open questions (OUT):** `create_deliverable` (in-app Á¡Á¡ÏÁ¡Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡ creation ã until it ships, binding is inert on in-app-created projects); deliverable at CREATE time (extend create_work_package + add-WP-sheet picker); bulk re-bind/drag UI.

## Spec 151 U1 - lazy client bundles: defer offline-queue runner (2026-06-19)

Status: COMPLETE (U1), build-verified; **first-load delta NOT numerically verifiable in this env** (see caveat). Bundle investigation: total client JS ~542kb gz; the 125kb gz chunk = supabase-js (browser client) + zod. zod is imported ONLY by `env.ts`/`env.server.ts` (env validation at import); the browser client by 9 client components ã 8 route-scoped/tap-gated, but **`UploadQueueRunner` is mounted in the root `layout.tsx`**, so it drags that 125kb chunk onto EVERY page's first paint. Verification: lint + typecheck + `pnpm build` all green (exit 0). **CAVEAT ã couldn't prove the win numerically:** Turbopack's prod build emits no per-route First Load JS table, and there's no runnable app here (no auth/prod URL), so the ~110kb first-paint reduction (124kb deferred ã ~14kb split overhead; total bundle ticked 542ã556kb because the chunk still EXISTS, just lazy) rests on the `dynamic(ssr:false)` framework guarantee, not a measurement. **Confirm on laptop:** preview + Network tab (the supabase chunk should load AFTER first paint, not block it), or add `@next/bundle-analyzer`. **Next (later, all need a runnable app to verify):** dynamic-import the 8 tap-gated uploader/sheet components per-route; Tier-2 in-page Suspense; middleware getUser; infra.

## Spec 150 U1 - streaming: route-level loading coverage (2026-06-19)

Status: COMPLETE (U1). ## Spec 147 U4 - DC-portal data-fetch parallelization (2026-06-19)

Status: COMPLETE. **Final unit of the waterfall-fix sweep (rank 4).** The DC self-service portal (`portal`) ran 5 fully-serial reads then own-docs + bank-present (profile -> consents -> crew -> payments-rpc -> pending-bank-change -> own-docs -> bank-present-rpc), all RLS-self-scoped. Pattern + idiom now established (`load-detail` / `load-request-detail` / `load-portal-data`). **Follow-up (NOT this spec):** ranks 5-8 (orders/[poId], deliveries/[deliveryId], schedule, projects hub) = same fix, smaller payoff ã new spec when wanted. ## Spec 152 U3 - project_director role: table write RLS (2026-06-19)

Status: COMPLETE (U3) ã **FEATURE COMPLETE**. Final unit: adds `project_director` to every RLS policy whose role list literally names `project_manager`. **Why it matters:** some core PM actions are direct-table writes gated by RLS, NOT RPCs ã most importantly **approving a work package** (an INSERT into `approvals`), so without U3 a director could not approve. Also covers deliverables/reports/work*packages/photo_logs/photo_markups/purchase_requests writes, project_members/work_package_members manage, and the master-table READS (clients/contractors/suppliers/service_providers/equipment\*/workers) that list PM directly. **Method: reconstructed the 48 policies from the LIVE catalog (`pg_policies`), appended `'project_director'::user_role` to each role `ARRAY[...]` (Postgres reverse-compiles `in()` ã `= ANY(ARRAY[])`, and has no CREATE OR REPLACE POLICY, so DROP+CREATE).** Migration `20260752000000_project_director_write_rls.sql` ã **48 policies / 58 role lists** widened (UPDATE policies carry PM in both USING + WITH CHECK). **NOT touched:** project-scoped SELECTs (gate on `can_see*\*`ã see-all for director since U1, never name PM literally); every super_admin-alone operator policy (no PM literal ã no match). **Test (REDãGREEN):** pgTAP`91`ã completeness catalog (per-field: no policy names PM without director; 48 before ã 0 after), behavioural lives_ok (director inserts an approval + updates a work_package directly on an UNINVOLVED WP ã see-all + role), negative control (visitor still denied ã 42501). No TS change. db:push applied to prod; db:test 91 files / 0 fail. **project_director is now a complete see-all project_manager: sees everything, every RPC action, every direct-table write.** Built in isolated worktree off`main`@#77.

## Spec 152 U2 - project_director role: RPC action gates (2026-06-19)

Status: COMPLETE (U2). Adds `project_director` to every SECURITY DEFINER RPC whose `current_user_role()` gate already admits `project_manager` ã so a director performs every PM action (create project/WP, record purchase, post journal, retention, WHT, equipment, contractor, etc.) across all projects. **Method: sourced the LIVE definitions via `pg_get_functiondef` (the DB is authoritative ã no hand-copying 47+ bodies), appended `'project_director'` to each role list with a regex transform, emitted one migration `20260751000000_project_director_rpc_gates.sql` of CREATE OR REPLACE.** **55 functions / 55 gates** (investigator estimated 47; the live filter found 55 ã more complete). Shape breakdown: 32û `not in ('project_manager','super_admin')`, 9û +site*admin, 6û/3û +procurement, 2û +accounting (gl_trial_balance/gl_reconciliation), 3û `in (...)` allow-forms (record/revoke_contractor_consent, add_contact_document). **Deliberately untouched:** `can_see_project` (its membership branch lists PM but director passes via the see-all branch, U1); `set_accounting_period_status`'s SECONDARY super-only sub-gate (`not v_is_super` for reopening a closed period ã a director still cannot reopen closed periods); the GL posters/plumbing (`post*\*\_to_gl`, `drain_gl_posting`, `resolve_posting_period`) which are service-role/de-gated; every `= 'super_admin'`-alone operator gate. **Test (REDãGREEN):** pgTAP `90-project-director-rpc-gates.test.sql`ã (1) completeness catalog assertion: ZERO PM-gated RPCs lack project_director (was 55 before push ã RED confirmed; 0 after ã GREEN); (2-4) behavioural lives_ok: director may create_project / create_work_package / set_work_package_notes (covers the 2-role, see-all+WP, and 3-role-with-site_admin shapes); (5) negative control: a visitor is still denied (gate didn't fall open). **No TS change** (RPC gates are server-side; U1 did the page gates). db:push applied to prod; db:test 90 files / 1792 asserts / 0 fail. Built in isolated worktree off`main`@#76 (concurrent 147-151 session still in main tree). **Next:** U3 = table write RLS policies (direct `.insert/.update` paths; most writes already go through these RPCs so U3 is the completeness tail). **Director is now FUNCTIONAL as a see-all PM for every RPC-backed action.**
