## Incident: AppSheet EMAXCONNSESSION (2026-06-11)

Operator screenshot: AppSheet app failed to load ã 'max clients reached in session mode, pool_size: 48' on projects + users reads. Diagnosis: AppSheet data source pointed at the SESSION pooler (5432, per go-live checklist Step 2 wording); Supavisor session pools are per-DB-user with a 48-client cap, and AppSheet's parallel sync burst exhausted appsheet_writer's pool. pg_stat_activity showed ZERO held appsheet_writer backends at diagnosis time ã burst, not a leak; nothing to terminate; no prod change made. Fix: operator repoints AppSheet to the TRANSACTION pooler (6543). Checklist Step 2 now documents the port split (5432 = smoke ritual only). Raising session pool_size is not viable (already near the compute tier's max_connections). Open question: if AppSheet misbehaves on transaction mode (prepared-statement quirks), revisit ã fallback is a dedicated session pool budget discussion.

## Unit: architecture revision doc ã entrepreneur lens (2026-06-11)

- **Status:** COMPLETE (doc-only, advisory). Operator brief: "revise the architecture of this app; think like an entrepreneur, not just technical."
- **Deliverable:** [`docs/architecture-revision-2026-06.md`](./architecture-revision-2026-06.md) ã strategic assessment of the whole system by business criteria (cost/month, ops burden per change, engagement, sellability, moat).

### Key positions taken (all pending operator sign-off ã ôÏ6 of the doc)

1. **AppSheet = rented ground.** Stop investing: cancel the unwritten ADR 0029 image bridge, build the in-app procurement surface + suppliers table instead (derive triggers are already writer-agnostic per ADR 0025; `procurement` role waits in the enum), demote AppSheet to read-only, then retire. Kills the per-schema-change operator tax, the Tier-2 write smoke, the EMAXCONNSESSION incident class, and the licence line.
2. **LINE notification outbox promoted to next feature slot** ã audit triggers already detect every hand-off event; they just don't deliver. Outbox table + drainer + LINE Messaging API channel.
3. **Railway retired when touched** ã PDF on-demand (route handler spike first) or Edge Function; end-state two platforms.
4. **Tenancy decided on purpose:** instance-per-customer for now + tenant-clean discipline + spin-up runbook; multi-tenant schema deferred until customer #2 is real.
5. Migration rehearsal stage (preview branch/scratch project) before destructive pushes; photo client-side downscale question raised; crew capability-URL uploads parked as v2 differentiator; dormant owner_id/work_package_members cleanup listed.

### Open questions

- The four ôÏ6 operator decisions (AppSheet sunset, notifications next, tenancy posture, photo downscale).
- No code/schema/test change this unit; suites untouched (555 pgTAP / 283 unit as of a42f083).

### Spec 32 adversarial verification (3-lens workflow) ã fixes landed pre-commit

- **Blast-radius + discipline lens ã MAJOR, fixed:** `.env.example` shipped the two optional vars as empty assignments; dotenv loads `VAR=` as "" and `.optional()` rejects "" ã every fresh "copy .env.example" local boot (and a blank Vercel value) would crash env validation at import time. Fixed both ends: `optionalNonEmpty` preprocess (emptyãabsent) in env.server.ts + lines commented out in .env.example + 3 new env.test.ts cases (the existing per-var missing/empty pattern now covers the new vars).
- **Blast-radius minors, fixed:** photo_logs uploader enrichment included tombstone rows (uploaded_by = REMOVER per ADR 0015) ã `.not("storage_path","is",null)`; no maxDuration on a 50ûN-push route ã `export const maxDuration = 60`; PostgREST 1000-row cap on the uploader query ã loud warn when hit (pilot volumes far below).
- **Security minors, fixed:** drain secret now compared via sha256+timingSafeEqual; LINE 5000-char text limit enforced by truncation in pushLineMessage (an oversized user comment was a deterministic 400 ã burned all 3 attempts ã actor-controlled notification suppression) + unit test; pgTAP file 25 hardened +11 asserts (plan 37): authenticated UPDATE/DELETE denial, anon denial, policies_are ZERO, EXECUTE denial on invoke_notification_drain for anon+authenticated (PostgREST RPC exposure pin), all four capture functions SECURITY DEFINER + pinned search_path, pr_created WHEN-guard negative, and the headline failure-swallowing posture PROVEN (outbox renamed away inside the transaction ã WP write still lands, zero rows captured).
- **Discipline:** payload.ts (5th pure module) had no tests ã notification-payload.test.ts added (key mapping, type-narrowing drops, malformed input); recorded here as declared addition alongside the admin.ts typing pull-in. pr_cancelled trigger breadth (anyãcancelled vs spec's approvedãcancelled) recorded in ADR 0037 as deliberate, with the audit-widening caveat for any future self-cancel unit.

Final suite state: 318 unit / 592 pgTAP / 27 e2e, typecheck+lint clean, drain endpoint live-probed 503 not_configured pre-activation.

## ADR 0034 amendment - atrophy model (2026-06-11)

Operator asked for hybrid pros/cons before AppSheet retirement; evidence pass (2-agent inventory) found the hybrid sounder than the architecture-revision urgency credited: AppSheet write surface = 9 fact columns on ONE table (decide/cancel/create/delivery-by-photo already in-app), derive/audit/notification triggers writer-agnostic, grid bulk-entry value unquantifiable yet (operator: "cannot determine"). ADR 0034 amended: parity build proceeds (in-app purchase/shipment form + suppliers still NEXT) but parity does NOT auto-demote ã both paths coexist; demotion when audit_log principal split shows in-app carrying >80-90% of fact-writes for several weeks, or on forcing event (customer #2 / next AppSheet outage). Column freeze + 3 open TODOs unchanged. Volume question converted to measurement (audit principal field) instead of a bet.

## Spec 34 - client photo downscale (2026-06-11)

Status: COMPLETE (operator phone pass = acceptance, spec ôÏ3). Implements ADR 0036: the downscaled file IS the original; max 2000px long edge, JPEG 0.8; downscale is an optimization NEVER a gate ã every failure path (HEIC on non-Safari, decode/encode errors, toBlob null) uploads the original unchanged; small files pass through with EXIF intact (orientation correct either way: re-encode bakes orientation via createImageBitmap imageOrientation:'from-image', passthrough keeps EXIF).

Built: src/lib/photos/downscale.ts (computeDownscaleTarget PURE + preparePhotoForUpload browser seam) + photoExtToMime in path.ts ã RED confirmed pre-impl, 11 unit tests. Integrated in ALL THREE uploaders at the ext-derivation point (ext flips to jpeg on re-encode BEFORE path building): phase-uploader (PendingUpload now stores prepared blob + lastModifiedMs scalar ã no raw File in state; retries reuse prepared bytes), attachment stager, delivery uploader. No DB/storage diff.

### Adversarial verification (2-lens) ã fixes landed pre-commit

- Transparent PNG/WebP over the cap re-encoded onto a BLACK background (canvas default substrate under toBlob jpeg) ã white fill before drawImage.
- REAL race (stager deferred mode): awaiting prepare BEFORE staging the chip meant a create-form submit during a slow phone decode flushed without the in-flight photo ã orphaned 'staged' chip, and a SECOND submission would have attached it to the WRONG purchase request. Fix: chips stage synchronously as 'preparing' (new status + Á¡Á¡°Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¡ÈÁ¡çÁ¡ÂÁ¡ÀÁ¡ÈÁ¡¿Á¡ãÎ display), prepare jobs tracked in a ref, flush() awaits outstanding prepares THEN reads a fresh items ref (the closure's items is stale after an await ã itemsRef pattern).
- createImageBitmap orientation made explicit (imageOrientation:'from-image' ã old Firefox/WebViews don't default to it); ext! assertions narrowed; stager header comment de-drifted; rounding test now exercises a genuinely fractional edge (3000û1000 ã 667).

Suite: 336 unit / 27 e2e green; pgTAP untouched (627). OPERATOR (acceptance): fresh camera photo on a test-safe WP ã renders correctly oriented; Storage object ~hundreds of KB not MB (dashboard read-only check). Open seams: Web Worker offload (with the offline-queue spec), HEIC polyfill, quality/size UI, retroactive processing (never ã append-only).

## Spec 35 - offline-tolerant upload queue, WP phase photos (2026-06-12)

Status: COMPLETE (operator phone pass = acceptance: airplane mode -> photo -> banner -> close browser -> signal -> reopen -> photo lands). ADR 0039. A selected phase photo is never lost: persisted to IndexedDB at selection (survives crash/close/navigation, iOS + Android ã NO Background Sync dependency), uploads live exactly as before on good signal, global UploadQueueRunner (root layout; banner Á¡ÈÁ¡ÙÁ¡ˆÁ¿Á¡Á¡ÈÁ¡¿Á¡ N Á¡ÈÁ¡¿Á¡ only when items wait) drains leftovers on mount/online/visibility/event/backoff (5sôñ2^n cap 5min).

Architecture: replay is IDEMPOTENT end-to-end so live-path/runner/multi-tab overlap is harmless BY DESIGN ã bytes 409 ã alreadyExists ã advance; addPhoto gains a 23505 replay path. Pure core (processQueue/QueueStore/classify/backoff) test-first vs in-memory store ã 15 unit tests; IDB store + runner are browser seams (house posture). Items NEVER auto-dropped (evidence); attempts only widen backoff.

### Adversarial verification (2-lens, verdict FAIL -> all fixed pre-commit)

- MAJOR (security): the 23505 verify originally checked id-exists only ã photo ids are readable role-wide, so a forged replay with a foreign photo id (e.g. a before-photo id + phase='after') would return ok AND flip the WP to pending_approval with zero after photos. Verify now requires the FULL replayed identity (id + work_package_id + phase + canonical storage_path).
- MAJOR (shared device): queue items now carry userId; the runner SKIPS foreign/ownerless items (uploaded_by is append-only ã misattribution is uncorrectable). Post-logout blob persistence recorded in ADR 0039 as an accepted tradeoff; discard UI = seam.
- MAJOR (live-path resilience): addPhoto invocation throw (the exact flaky-signal case) stuck the tile and ABORTED the multi-file loop (remaining files never queued ã silent loss) -> try/catch in insertOne + per-iteration isolation in handleFiles. Queue I/O (quota/private-mode IDB) wrapped non-fatal ã the safety net can't break the live pipeline.
- MAJOR (idempotency gap): live uploadOne wasn't 409-tolerant ã a runner/live overlap left a permanently-failing retry tile; now classifies alreadyExists and proceeds.
- Minors: banner staleness (notify after live remove; lock-unavailable branch refreshes count + short retry), pass-failure now reschedules (30s) instead of freezing, dead nowMs dep removed, projectId dropped from the persisted item (fileName kept for the discard seam, recorded), header lifecycle comment updated.

Suites: 349 unit / 27 e2e green; pgTAP untouched (627); no DB schema diff (addPhoto change is app-layer only). Open seams: reference/delivery photo queueing, manual discard UI, SW Background Sync, Web Worker downscale. OPERATOR: phone acceptance pass for specs 34+35 together (one outdoor session covers both).

Fixed: foreign items render read-only without fileName (Á¡ÈÁ¡¿Á¡Á¡Á¡ÙÁ¡Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ÙÁ¡ñÁ¿Á¡ ã Á¡ÈÁ¡ÙÁ¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ýÁ¡Á¡ÙÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ýÁ¡ˆÁ¡¿Á¿Á¡ÈÁ¡¯Á¡Á¡).

- Delivery failure copy said "Á¡ËÁ¡ÙÁ¡Á¿Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¿" which would make users re-pick under a NEW uuid ã duplicate rows when both landed. ## Spec 42 - PWA standalone LINE re-login, iOS (2026-06-12)

Status: COMPLETE (operator iPhone pass = acceptance). Operator report: installed PWA loses login after logout; LINE re-login bounces through the LINE app to the system browser, session lands in the wrong cookie jar (iOS standalone jar is separate; CSRF state cookie also splits, so the browser-side callback dies oauth_failed). Fix per spec 42: disable_auto_login=true on the authorize URL for iOS standalone launches (verified against LINE Login v2.1 docs ã keeps the whole flow in the PWA's in-app overlay via LINE web login), CSS-toggled standalone login anchor (?standalone=1, display-mode arbitrary variants, no 'use client' ã ADR 0012 plain-anchor shape preserved), header logout CSS-hidden in standalone (profile-page logout stays, reachable via bottom tab). Android untested ã flag is iOS-UA-gated to avoid regressing the shared-jar WebAPK flow.

Test-first: 3 new route tests (tests/unit/line-start-route.test.ts ã env.server mocked at module level since serverEnv validates at import), 2 LoginButton tests, 1 AppHeader logout-wrapper pin. Playwright note: role-based locators ignore the display-hidden second anchor (a11y tree), so the existing e2e href pin survives untouched ã 8/8 auth e2e green on chromium. Suites: 368 unit / lint / typecheck green; no DB diff.

Recorded limitation + seam: LINE accounts with no registered email/password cannot complete the web login form (mitigation: browser login -> reinstall PWA; site data copies into the container at install). Real fix if it bites = one-time handoff code minting the session in the PWA via the existing generateLink/verifyOtp machinery (spec 42 out-of-scope section). Supabase inactivity timeout must stay "never" (operator check, no code). OPERATOR: iPhone acceptance pass ã install PWA, logout, log back in via LINE web login without leaving the app.

## Spec 44 - handoff resume hardening, iOS process death (2026-06-12)

Status: COMPLETE (operator iPhone re-test = acceptance). First spec-43 field test failed: row reached approved (browser success page shown) but PWA never claimed - iOS killed the backgrounded PWA during the LINE/Safari excursion and sessionStorage died with it (no resume, no poll, idle button). Client-only fix in StandaloneLoginButton: (1) localStorage + expiry stamp (line_handoff_device_code / line_handoff_expires_at, 600s = server TTL; stale stamp reads as nothing-stored in the useSyncExternalStore snapshot, clearing only in handlers - no side effects in render), (2) popup opened SYNCHRONOUSLY in the tap gesture (window.open after await can fall outside iOS transient user activation), opener nulled, navigated after the start POST; blocked popup -> same-window fallback (safe now that the code persists), start failure closes the orphan popup. Server untouched - approved rows wait the full TTL for a late claimer by design. 8 component tests (popup contract, resume, stale-stamp idle, fallback). Suites: 398 unit / auth e2e 8/8. Lesson banked: iOS standalone PWA storage assumptions - sessionStorage NEVER survives the app-switch kill; any cross-app handshake state must live in localStorage with its own TTL.

## Spec 45 - handoff opens LINE in same window, no popup (2026-06-12)

Status: COMPLETE (operator iPhone re-test = acceptance). Spec-44 field test: home app went ALL WHITE on tap - iOS standalone PWAs have NO tab model; the spec-44 synchronous window.open('', '\_blank') swaps the visible view to a dead about:blank and the later popup navigation never reaches the user. Fix (client-only, third round on ADR 0041): popup path deleted; tap -> start POST -> store code (spec-44 localStorage+expiry) -> SAME-WINDOW navigation to LINE (no transient-activation concern). Return trip = spec 44's resume: PWA resumes (user closes out-of-scope top-bar view) or relaunches cold at start_url; any LoginButton page resumes the poll. Cancel pin caught a REAL bug: cancel from a resumed waiting state mutated only storage (no React state delta) so useSyncExternalStore never re-read - storage mutations now emit to subscribers (proper external store, not the noop-subscribe shortcut). Suites: 397 unit / auth e2e 8/8. Lessons banked: (1) standalone PWA = never window.open, same-window nav + persistent resume state is the pattern; (2) noop-subscribe useSyncExternalStore is a trap whenever mutations can happen without an accompanying state change.

## Data-architecture hardening pass (2026-06-13) ã audit ranks 1-9 shipped

Status: COMPLETE (all applied to prod under full operator autonomy; verify = operator can't see it, it's infra). Followed a 4-dimension multi-agent audit (normalization/scale/RLS-tenancy/AI-readiness) + synthesis. Full review + deferred roadmap persisted at docs/data-architecture-review-2026-06.md. Nine ranks, 8 migrations (20260625000100-000800) + 1 app change + 7 new pgTAP files (35-41); suite 865 assertions / 0 failures; typecheck/unit/build green. Shipped: (1+2) hot-path indexes - labor_logs superseded_by partial (anti-join) + work_date (the spec-69 payroll date-window was seq-scanning since both composites lead with worker/wp), purchase_requests(requested_by,supplier_id), work_packages(status,updated_at)+(contractor_id), workers(contractor_id,user_id). (5) revoke PUBLIC/anon EXECUTE on the 5 worker/labor mutation RPCs (the 0624 note-param DROP+CREATEs had reset grants to the PUBLIC default; internal current_user_role() gate was the only defense). (4) prune_notification_outbox daily cron (terminal rows >30d - the only disposable log table; audit_log/photo_logs/labor_logs are evidence, partition later). (6) COMMENT ON all 20 tables + load-bearing columns - was 0 table/4 column comments; makes the schema legible to text-to-SQL/AI. (7) purchase_requests.received_by_id FK (the one genuine free-text-where-FK-belongs column; populated on both write paths - record_site_purchase=auth.uid(), delivery trigger=uploader) + reports.params object CHECK + workers.contractor_id delete-block comment. (3) RLS EVAL-ONCE - the headline: every policy called auth.uid()/current_user_role() BARE, evaluated per-row (EXPLAIN-verified: "Filter: current_user_role()=ANY"). Wrapped in scalar subselects -> InitPlan, once per query (EXPLAIN-verified after). Transformed in-DB from pg_get_expr text (no hand-reproduction). 66/67 policies; photo_markups EXCLUDED - its INSERT policy has an inline self-referential subquery (tombstone-target), wrapping calls in either of its policies makes the self-reference re-apply a wrapped policy -> 42P17 recursion (cure = a SECURITY DEFINER tombstone helper like attachments use; deferred). Three migrations (000600 cursor-skip wrapped 34 + broke markups; 000700 snapshot-then-alter wrapped remaining 32 + began markup revert; 000800 finished markup revert). LESSONS: (a) a plpgsql FOR-IN-SELECT cursor over pg_policies skips rows when you ALTER mid-loop (catalog changes under the cursor) - snapshot into a temp table first. (b) Postgres renders a wrapped call as "( SELECT f() AS f )", so literal-string bare-detection false-positives - use regexp_count(total) > regexp_count(select-prefixed). (8) /requests bounded queries - was select\* unbounded + ?mine filtered in JS = silent 1000-row PostgREST truncation + mine-after-cap drop; split pending/decided, ?mine as DB predicate, decided capped explicitly at 500. (9) pgTAP pin of the no-JWT NULL-deny invariant (appsheet_writer/anon/future-AI-role all depend on current_user_role() returning NULL with no sub). DEFERRED (own units, see review doc): AI access contract (CRITICAL - agents must use authenticated RLS context not admin.ts), semantic/analytics views, ai_insights landing table, evidence-log partitioning, pgvector semantic layer; + multi-tenant org_id seam (before customer #2), /requests keyset paging, photo_markups SECURITY DEFINER helper. Caveat: eval-once win EXPLAIN-verified (InitPlan) not load-benchmarked; partition urgency volume-dependent (unmeasured).

## Spec 81 ã Master data management: clients ôñ suppliers ôñ contractors (2026-06-14, SHIPPED)

Operator picked this from a "what next" menu (build the master-data **screens** + unblock the deferred `suppliers.note`/`contractors.note`). **SHIPPED (migration 20260627000000_masters_notes.sql applied to prod under the db:push gate, pgTAP 935/0):** one PM-gated route `/pm/masters` with a RadioChip segmented control (Á¡ËÁ¡¿Á¡Á¡Á¿Á¡ý/Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡Â/Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡ý) over the three reference masters ã each created inline elsewhere and never editable until now (a name typo on a master that snapshots onto reports/PRs was permanent). App cap 1000 (`validateNotes`), DB CHECK 2000 (specs 71ã75 doctrine). **No RLS policy dropped/created** ã the note rides each table's existing UPDATE/INSERT policy, so the eval-once doctrine (pgTAP file 40) is untouched (this is exactly why a note column needs no RPC: it rides the existing policy). suppliers.note/contractors.note were DEFERRED in specs 74/75 for lack of an edit screen; spec 81 builds the screen, so they land here. **No SECURITY DEFINER RPC.** `/pm/masters` is `requireRole(PM_ROLES)`-gated and PM/super already hold the INSERT/UPDATE policy + column grants on all three (clients pm/super; contractors sa/pm/superãpm/super; suppliers pm/procurement/superãpm/super), so the six actions (`{create,update}{Client,Supplier,Contractor}Record` in `src/app/pm/masters/actions.ts`) write directly under the authenticated session ã the spec-80 project_members precedent. Each action re-checks PM_ROLES before the write: defense-in-depth + a real error, because an RLS UPDATE whose USING fails affects 0 rows SILENTLY (spec-80 lesson) and trusting RLS alone would mask a forbidden edit as success. Update sends only changed keys (omitted=preserve, ""=clear); `norm()` blanksãnull. The existing inline quick-adds (createClient in settings, createSupplier in requests, createContractor in WP assignment) are UNTOUCHED ã they stay note-less and return the new id for immediate selection in their host flow (recorded simplify-seam: a shared insert core could unify them; they differ in return shape, revalidate target, and note support).

**Components.** `master-manager.tsx` ã generic presentational manager driven by a `MasterFieldDef[]` schema (key/label/type text|tel|email|textarea/maxLength); add card + per-row Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¿Á¡ expander; entity actions injected as `onCreate`/`onUpdate` (no server fn imported here ã the NotesField pattern; toast on success spec 76; `active:` press tints spec 77). `masters-tabs.tsx` ã the segmented-control shell, holds the active tab + binds the field-recordãtyped-action mappers. `page.tsx` fetches all three lists (user session, `order by name`) ã MasterRow[] (snakeãcamel) ã MastersTabs; +loading.tsx. Nav: `PM_HUB_NAV` += Á¡Á¿Á¡ÙÁ¡ÀÁ¡¿Á¡ËÁ¡¨Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡ (5 items, desktop strip; no phone bottom-tab entry ã same seam as /workers, /pm/payroll). site-map.md + feature-specs README (79/80/81 added) updated same-unit.

## Spec 95 ã iOS keyboard repaint guard (2026-06-15, SHIPPED, code-only)

Operator phone (WP page screenshot): "whenever user finished typing something and lower down keyboard, a part of screen will go missing, and cannot scroll to top." The spec-64 "keyboard case = next suspect." **ROUND 1 (309a245) shipped on the WRONG hypothesis** ã assumed iOS scrolled the locked DOCUMENT and reset it to 0; operator: "not fixed." **Round-2 diagnosis (AskUserQuestion):** the screen RECOVERS ON ITS OWN the moment you scroll, and Á¡ÈÁ¡çÁ¿Á¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ clears it ã it's a missing-REPAINT glitch, NOT a stuck scroll position. With the body LOCKED (overflow:hidden; PageShell's `<main>` the only scroller), iOS standalone WebKit resizes the viewport back when the keyboard closes but does NOT repaint the locked scroller ã content (sticky header included) present but blank until a scroll forces a repaint. **FIX (round 2):** `ViewportScrollGuard` now reproduces the recovering scroll the instant the keyboard closes ã `scroller.scrollBy(0,1)` then `scrollBy(0,-1)` next animation frame (position-preserving repaint nudge), on the `<main>` scroller. Same triggers (visualViewport `resize` back to ~full; `focusout` fallback) + same guard (skip while another editable is focused). No document-scroll reset (the position was never the problem). spec-64 body-lock + PageShell unchanged. interactive-widget viewport hint NOT used (iOS Safari doesn't honour it). TDD: tests/unit/viewport-scroll-guard.test.tsx (nudges scroller on blur with nothing focused; does NOT nudge while another field is focused). lint / typecheck / build green. Spec: docs/feature-specs/95-ios-keyboard-scroll-guard.md. LESSON: "blank area that recovers on scroll" = iOS missing-repaint after viewport resize, not a scroll offset ã force a repaint (scroll nudge), don't reset position. Acceptance = operator iPhone (PWA: close/reopen or Á¡ÈÁ¡çÁ¿Á¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ after deploy).

## Spec 103 ã Capture the on-site purchase amount (2026-06-15, SHIPPED, SCHEMA)

amount to the site-purchase path only. **Explore-quote trap caught:** the agent quoted record_site*
purchase from 20260622000500, but a LATER migration 20260625000500 re-created it to also set
received_by_id ã verified via grep before DROP+CREATE (would've regressed received_by_id otherwise).
**SHIPPED:** migration 20260630000100 DROP+CREATE record_site_purchase + `p_amount numeric default null`
(CREATE OR REPLACE can't add a param) ã body = the CURRENT (000500) version + amount (positive-when-
given check, amount in INSERT + audit payload), re-grant execute to authenticated (drop drops grant);
amount stays RPC-only-write (zero authenticated grant). App: validate-site-purchase +amount (positive/
finite when given); recordSitePurchase action +amount (omitãRPC default); site-purchase-form +optional
Á¡Á¡°Á¡Á¡ÏÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡ field. database.types hand-extended (record_site_purchase Args +p_amount?) ã db:types regen
reconciled. **Tests:** validate-site-purchase.test value+amount +1 case; pgTAP 33 sig pin ã5 args +3
(plan 27ã30: records w/ amount, amount persisted, amountãÊ0 throws). 767 unit / lint / typecheck / build

docs/feature-specs/103-site-purchase-amount.md. **Amount stays OPTIONAL everywhere** (record_purchase +
site purchase) ã dashboard material spend still "counted where priced"; making it required = separate

## Spec 112 ã Band-relative row health color in the procurement grid (2026-06-15, SHIPPED, code-only)

Operator pushed back on naive grid coloring: "coloring urgent red doesn't help if they already
ordered the things ã design better, think outside the box, ultrathink." KEY REFRAME: request
priority is the REQUESTER's lens, stale once ordered; the buyer's grid color should encode the
BUYER's TIME pressure, **band-relative** (red MEANS a different thing per band). **AskUserQuestion:
"band-relative health RAG"** (over late-only / buyer-SLA-aging). App-only, no DB. **SHIPPED:** (1)
pure `lib/purchasing/row-health.ts` (TDD, +14 unit) ã `rowHealth(status, eta, neededBy, todayIso)` ã
late|at_risk|on_track|waiting, band-aware via procurementBand: **to_order** (not ordered) pressure =
needed_by (pastãlate, ãÊ7dãat_risk, else on_track, no-needãon_track); **in_transit** (ordered) = ETA
pastãlate, ETA>needed_byãat_risk (lands late), else on_track, no-etaãon_track (request urgency
IRRELEVANT here ã the operator's whole point, so rowHealth takes NO priority input); **received**ã
on_track; **awaiting_approval/rejected/cancelled**ãwaiting (not the buyer's move). `HEALTH_SOON_DAYS=7`;
`daysUntil` = UTC-midnight ISO diff (tz-stable). +`rowHealthLabel` Thai (hover title). (2) grid: each
data row's FIRST cell gets `border-l-4` + a health color (late=danger, at_risk=attn, on_track=
done-strong, waiting=edge) + `title` reason; ETA turns text-danger when late. Used all-sides color
tokens (border-danger etc.) NOT border-l-<token> (don't rely on left-specific color generation). (3)
`/requests` passes `today=bangkokTodayISO()` into the grid so health uses the Bangkok civil date, not
the client clock. **Three orthogonal grid signals now:** band=action ôñ mini-bar=stage ôñ color=on-time.
Grid only ã pill/mini-bar/cards/band-header unchanged. 825 unit / lint / typecheck / build green; **no
migration ã pgTAP 1025 untouched**. Spec: docs/feature-specs/112-grid-row-health-color.md. **NOT
preview-verified** (procurement-gated) ã acceptance = procurement user PC: not-ordered-past-needed_by
glows red, shipment-past-ETA red, shipment-landing-after-need amber, on-track green, awaiting neutral;
hover explains. SEAMS: SOON window fixed at 7d (no per-project SLA); receivedãamber on missing invoice
(filing gap) needs attachment query ã deferred; color legend + health on phone cards later; in_transit
no-ETA reads on_track (an "unmanaged PO" amber is a later refinement).

## ADR 0044 + Spec 115 ã Purchase orders (grouping tickets) ã DESIGN LOCKED, build pending (2026-06-16)

Operator asked how admins handle a purchase covering **more than one ticket** + partial delivery.
Found the gap: the only procurement entity is `purchase_requests` (one ticket = one line/WP/qty,
atomic delivery) ã **no PO object**; a buyer ordering 5 tickets from one supplier records 5û, and the
per-ticket amount means one invoice total is split by hand. Partial-**across**-tickets already works
(each ticket delivers independently) but ungrouped; partial-**within**-a-ticket (split qty) is
unmodelled (a later receipts unit). Two AskUserQuestions locked the design: **(1) build PO grouping**
(over partial-receipts / both / workaround); **(2) per-ticket prices** (PO total = sum, over
PO-total-+-split / lump) ã preserves per-WP material spend (specs 100/103/106 read amount per ticket).
**ADR 0044 (Accepted)** + **spec 115** written: new `purchase_orders` table (po_number seq, supplier_id
FK + snapshot, eta, ordered_at, notes, created_by; **no money column** ã total is computed);
`purchase_requests.purchase_order_id` nullable FK; **atomic SECURITY DEFINER `create_purchase_order`**
(back-office gate on the AUTHENTICATED session per the spec-68 lesson; per-line guard status=approved ã
amount/supplier/eta/purchased_at/status=purchased/po_id; audit per line + PO row); ship+delivery stay
per-ticket (partial-across works); **PO status DERIVED** (openãorderedãpartially_receivedãreceived,
pure helper, not stored); RLS = back-office SELECT (ADR 0026), RPC-only writer (ADR 0038 posture).
**Phased build: spec 115 = data layer** (table+FK+RLS+RPC+helpers+pgTAP+types, schema ã operator gate);
**spec 116 = UI** (grid multi-select bundling, create-PO form w/ per-line prices, grouped display, PO
context in the drawer). NOT YET BUILT ã schema migration is the riskiest change type (immutable once
merged); building it deliberately. SEAMS: within-ticket partial receipts, PO line-set editing, PO PDF.
Also still open: delete the 7 test PRs (2926ã2932) + the /grid-preview page after operator review.

---

## Spec 115 ã Purchase orders: data layer (ADR 0044, phase 1) ã SHIPPED 2026-06-16

**What:** the PO grouping data layer. Migrations `20260701000000` (audit_action `+purchase_order_create`,
own txn ã ADD VALUE can't be used same-txn) + `20260701000100` (table + FK + RLS + RPC) applied to prod
under the operator gate. **No UI** (that's spec 116).

- **`purchase_orders` table:** `po_number` own sequence (mirrors `pr_number`), `supplier_id` FK + `supplier`
  text snapshot (spec-33 pattern), `eta`, `ordered_at`, `notes` CHECK(ãÊ2000), `created_by`, timestamps.
  **NO money column** (ôÏ3) ã the PO total is the computed SUM of member `purchase_requests.amount`, so per-WP
  material spend (specs 100/103/106) stays exact. RLS: back-office SELECT site-wide (site_admin/PM/procurement/
  super, ADR 0026, eval-once wrapped); **NO INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE policy** ã the RPC (function owner) is the
  only writer (ADR 0038). `grant select` to authenticated only; appsheet_writer unaffected.
- **`purchase_requests.purchase_order_id`** nullable FK ã `purchase_orders(id)` (ôÏ2). RPC-only-writable: the
  column-scoped authenticated UPDATE grant (20260616000400) doesn't name it, so app sessions can't set it
  directly. Indexed (PO ã members read). `purchase_orders.supplier_id` also indexed.
- **`create_purchase_order(p_supplier_id uuid, p_eta date, p_lines jsonb)`** SECURITY DEFINER, search_path
  pinned, returns the new PO id (uuid). Back-office gate on the **authenticated session** (spec-68 lesson ã
  service-role has no JWT so auth.uid()/current_user_role() would refuse it; grant execute to authenticated,
  revoke from public/anon). Inserts the PO; per line `{request_id, amount}` guards `status='approved'` then
  stamps amount/supplier(snapshot)/eta/purchased_at=now()/status='purchased'/purchase_order_id. **All-or-
  nothing** (one txn ã a non-approved line rolls back the whole bundle). Audit: the per-line approvedãpurchased
  UPDATE fires the **existing** `purchase_requests_audit_appsheet` trigger ã one `purchase_request_purchase`
  row per line (mirrors record_purchase, null-actor/principal=authenticated); the RPC writes ONE additional
  `purchase_order_create` row carrying the real actor + po_number/supplier/eta/request_ids.
- **Pure helpers** `src/lib/purchasing/purchase-order.ts` (TDD-first, 10 unit): `derivePurchaseOrderStatus`
  (openãorderedãpartially_receivedãreceived; on_route counts as ordered; rejected/cancelled EXCLUDED;
  empty roll-up ã open) + `purchaseOrderTotal` (sum of non-null line amounts).
- **pgTAP file 49** (+48): catalog/columns/notes-CHECK/RLS posture (1 SELECT policy, no write policy, no
  authenticated INSERT/UPDATE)/member FK; RPC signature (SECURITY DEFINER + search_path + returns uuid +
  authenticated-only execute) + behaviour (bundles approved ã purchased/priced/stamped/snapshotted; sums 300;
  PO-create + 2 per-line purchase audit rows; refuses non-approved line / empty set / unknown supplier; atomic
  rollback). Enum pins updated in files 03 + 18 (grep-all-enum-pins lesson).
- **database.types.ts** hand-extended then `db:types` reconciled ã content byte-identical (only delta was the
  `purchase_orders` block ordering; Supabase sorts it before `purchase_requests`).

**Gate honored:** built local-green (lint / typecheck / 842 unit / build), AskUserQuestion ã "Apply now" ã
db:push (migration FIRST), db:types reconcile, db:test 1073/0-fail, THEN commit + push. **Suites:** 842 unit /
1073 pgTAP.

**Acceptance (no UI):** `create_purchase_order` bundles approved tickets into a PO (each line ã purchased,
priced, stamped), refuses a non-approved line, is back-office-gated; per-WP spend still reads each line's
amount; pgTAP green. **Next:** spec 116 = the UI (grid multi-select bundling, create-PO form with per-line
prices, grouped display, PO context in the review drawer). Out (later units): within-ticket partial receipts
(split qty), PO line-set editing, PO PDF.

**Still open (test artifacts, delete on operator's "done reviewing"):** the 7 seeded test PRs
(`delete from public.purchase_requests where pr_number between 2926 and 2932;`) + the temporary
`src/app/grid-preview/page.tsx` (spec 113) + its `nav-back-affordance.test.ts` EXCLUDED_ROUTES entry.

## Spec 116 ã Purchase orders: create-PO UI (ADR 0044, phase 2) ã SHIPPED 2026-06-16

**What:** the screen to actually create a multi-ticket PO (spec 115 shipped only the engine). On the
procurement desktop grid, the buyer checks several **approved** (`to_order`) tickets ã a sticky
`Á¡ˆÁ¡ÈÁ¿Á¡ýÁ¡ PO (n)` bar ã a bottom-sheet form (supplier picker + ETA + per-line price inputs + live total) ã
`createPurchaseOrder` action ã the `create_purchase_order` RPC bundles them atomically. **No schema**
(pure UI on the spec-115 data layer).

- **Pure validator** `src/lib/purchasing/validate-create-purchase-order.ts` (TDD, 8 unit): ãË1 line, a
  supplier UUID, each amount null-or-positive, no duplicate request ids, and a **required** valid ETA
  (deliberate ã a PO commits a delivery date; ad-hoc `record_purchase` stays ETA-optional. Optional-PO-
  ETA is a recorded seam needing the RPC's `p_eta` to gain a SQL default first).
- **Server action** `createPurchaseOrder({ supplierId, eta, lines })` in `src/app/requests/actions.ts`
  ã runs on the **authenticated user session** (`getActionUser`, NOT the admin client, because the RPC
  is role-gated on `current_user_role()`); calls `supabase.rpc("create_purchase_order", ãÎ)`, maps
  42501/P0001 to Thai, `revalidatePath("/requests")`, returns `{ ok, poId }`.
- **`CreatePurchaseOrderSheet`** (`src/components/features/create-purchase-order-sheet.tsx`, client):
  supplier `<select>`, ETA date, per-line price inputs, live total via `purchaseOrderTotal`. Submit ã
  action ã on success clears the selection, closes, `router.refresh()` (bundled rows leave `to_order`,
  appear in `in_transit`). Component test (4): renders lines + live total, submits the right payload,
  surfaces errors, rejects a bad price client-side.
- **`procurement-grid.tsx`**: a checkbox on each approved (`to_order`) row + the sticky bundle bar +
  the sheet ã **all gated on `canBundle` (suppliers present)**, so the spec-113 preview/smoke (no
  suppliers) stays selection-free and router-free.

**LESSON (the smoke test earned its keep):** `ProcurementGrid` initially mounted `CreatePurchaseOrderSheet`
unconditionally; the sheet's top-level `useRouter()` threw "app router not mounted" in the no-router
smoke test. Gating the mount on `canBundle` fixed it ã a component that calls `useRouter` must not be
mounted on a surface that has no router (preview/smoke). All create-PO props are clientãclient (the
Á¡Á¡¿Á¿Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡Â serverãclient function-prop lesson does not bite here).

**Gate:** 860 unit / lint / typecheck / build green. No schema ã no operator gate; committed + pushed.
**Acceptance** (procurement can't be preview-verified ã preview only renders `/login`): a procurement
user (Pattrawut) on a PC checks 2+ approved tickets ã Á¡ˆÁ¡ÈÁ¿Á¡ýÁ¡ PO ã supplier + ETA + prices ã creates the
PO; tickets become purchased/priced/stamped and leave the to-order band.

**OUT (deferred follow-ups):** grouped PO display (a PO + its members as a group) + PO context in the
review drawer; PO line-set editing; PO PDF; phone multi-select; optional-PO-ETA. Also still queued: the
**documents+photos attachments** unit the operator asked for (Q1 answered = documents + photos; build
after this).

## Spec 119 / ADR 0045 ã VAT capture on purchases (phase 1) ã SHIPPED 2026-06-16

**What:** operator asked about partial delivery + VAT. **Partial delivery = CLOSED** (across-ticket
already works via the spec-115 PO roll-up; within-ticket split-quantity declined). **VAT** ã operator:
"user can pick whether the price is inclusive or exclusive"; spend = GROSS. SHIPPED (migration
`20260701000200` applied to prod under the gate; 874 unit / 1075 pgTAP / lint / typecheck / build).

- **Model (ADR 0045):** `amount` is canonically the GROSS (what you pay; spend/budget/PO-total read it
  unchanged). New `purchase_requests.vat_rate numeric(5,2) default 0` (CHECK 0ã100); **net/VAT DERIVED**
  (`src/lib/purchasing/vat.ts`, TDD 8 unit: `deriveVatBreakdown` net+VAT sum back to gross;
  `grossFromEntry`; `rateForMode`; `VAT_RATE=7`). The mode (inclusive/exclusive/none) is an entry
  convenience ã only gross + rate are stored.
- **Migration:** vat_rate column + the 3 amount-entry RPCs (`record_purchase`, `create_purchase_order`,
  `record_site_purchase`) DROP+CREATE with `+p_vat_rate` (default 0 ã existing callers/tests/appsheet
  unaffected; bodies reproduced verbatim + the rate). vat_rate = amount's posture (RPC-write, not in the
  authenticated UPDATE grant). RPC sig pins updated (files 26/33/49, +numeric). pgTAP file 49 +2.
- **UI (this push ã PO checkout only):** `CreatePurchaseOrderSheet` gains a VAT mode picker; per-line
  prices resolve to gross via the mode; **live net/VAT/gross breakdown**; `createPurchaseOrder` passes
  `p_vat_rate` (one rate per PO). Sheet test +1 (exclusive ã +7%).

**Gate honored:** local-green ã "Apply now" ã db:push (migration first) ã db:types reconcile (content
byte-identical; only the `create_purchase_order` Args line reflowed) ã db:test 1075/0-fail ã commit+push.

**OUT (additive follow-ups ã RPCs already accept the rate, NO further schema):** VAT picker on the
`record_purchase` + `record_site_purchase` forms; a **persistent net/VAT readout** on the request detail
page + the grid/drawer. **OUT (v3 accounting):** withholding tax, tax-invoice (Á¿Á¡Á¡Á¡°Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¡Á¡ Á¡ýÁ¡ˋÁ¡ç) docs, reports.

## Spec 121 ã PDF support in purchasing attachments (ADR 0046 Layer A) ã SHIPPED 2026-06-16

**What:** the deferred documents+photos foundation. Purchasing attachments are image-only today
(`pr-attachments` bucket = jpeg/png/webp/heic, downscaled ã spec 34). Layer A makes a **PDF** attachable

- viewable on the **existing** surfaces (invoice uploader + reference stager) ã attach a PDF quote/
  invoice to a request. Layers B (PO-level source-doc + side-by-side create-PO surface) and C (AI
  extraction) are separate later units, untouched.

* **kind decision = new `'pdf'`** (over a non-downscale `image` branch): ADR 0046 names `kind image|pdf`;
  viewer dispatches cleanly on kind (iframe vs lightbox); `pra_purpose_kind` auto-blocks a PDF from a
  delivery-confirmation slot; the image-only token trigger skips PDFs; semantic honesty.
* **Migrations (operator-gated):** (1) re-assert `pr-attachments` `allowed_mime_types` += `application/pdf`
  (25 MiB cap stays) + `alter type ãÎ add value 'pdf'` (no pdf-literal usage in the same file ã
  same-txn-safe). (2) `pra_pdf_shape` CHECK (pdf content row carries `storage_path`, no `url`) ã separate
  file because the CHECK _uses_ `'pdf'`.
* **No-downscale upload:** raw PDF bytes (`contentType: application/pdf`) to the canonical
  `.../{att}.pdf` path; metadata-after-upload (spec-24 pattern). PDFs NOT offline-queue-bracketed this
  unit (manual-retry, mirrors invoice uploader ã recorded seam; `QueuedUpload.ext` stays `PhotoExt`).
* **Viewer:** `AttachmentPdf` (signed-URL `<iframe>` + open-in-new-tab); detail page groups by kind
  (reference images/PDFs/links; invoice images/PDFs); signed URLs minted for image + pdf rows.

**Money posture unchanged.** Gate honored: lint / typecheck / build / **881 unit** local-green ã
AskUserQuestion "Apply now" ã db:push (migrations `20260702000000` + `20260702000100` applied to prod) ã
db:types reconcile (**byte-identical** to the hand-extension) ã db:test **1081/0**. Then commit + push.

**Build notes (reusable):** (1) `buildPrAttachmentStoragePath` widened `PhotoExt` ã `AttachmentExt`
(`PhotoExt | "pdf"`) ã its existing pin test asserted `pdf` ã null; flipped to assert it builds, added a
truly-invalid-ext case (TDD redãgreen anchor). (2) The detail page's reference grouping used
`kind !== "image"` for links ã a pdf would have leaked into the link list (and been dropped, url=null);
fixed to `kind === "link"` + a new `referencePdfs`/`invoicePdfs` split. (3) Signed-URL minting widened
to `image || pdf` rows (pdfs were getting no URL). (4) Server actions derive the stored kind from the
validated ext (`attachmentKindForExt`) ã client-passed kind is not trusted; `findLandedAttachment` now
pins the actual kind (image-only check would mis-replay a pdf). (5) `addDeliveryConfirmationPhoto` stays
image-only on purpose (a receipt photo; `pra_purpose_kind` enforces). **Acceptance owed:** procurement/
back-office user attaches a PDF quote/invoice on `/requests/[id]` ã uploads un-downscaled + renders in
the iframe viewer; images still work. (Auth-gated route ã operator-on-live, not preview-verifiable.)
**Recorded seam:** PDF reference attachments are NOT offline-queue-bracketed (manual-retry, mirrors the
invoice uploader; `QueuedUpload.ext` stays `PhotoExt`). **NEXT:** ADR 0046 Layer B (document-first
create-PO: PO-level source-doc + side-by-side surface) ã Layer C (AI extraction, Claude).

## Spec 125 ã PO source-document attachments (ADR 0046 Layer B, Unit 1) ã SHIPPED 2026-06-16

**What:** the quotation/invoice a PO is created from now attaches at the **PO level** (ADR 0046
decision 2). Operator picked the **phased "attach-doc first"** cut: this unit = data layer + a doc picker
in the **existing** create-PO sheet (uploaded when the PO is created) + a viewer on the request detail
page. The full **side-by-side wide doc|form surface** (ADR 0046 decision 4) is the next unit.

- **Decisions** (ADR 0046 left these "to decide at spec time"): grain = a **`purchase_order_attachments`
  table** (mirrors pr_attachments; append-only + tombstone-ready; kind image|pdf; **no `purpose` column**
  v1 ã every PO doc is the source doc, YAGNI; **no token side-table** ã vestigial AppSheet bridge).
  Storage = a **new private `po-attachments` bucket** (image + application/pdf from day one ã the Layer A
  lesson), path `{po_id}/{att}.{ext}` (a PO spans projects ã po_id is the scope). Writer = **direct INSERT
  under RLS** (mirror pr_attachments), **content rows only** (no tombstone arm/removal UI v1).
- **Upload-on-submit** (ADR 0046 decision 3, resolves the no-po_id-yet chicken-and-egg): the sheet keeps
  the file client-side; `createPurchaseOrder` returns `poId` ã browser uploads to `po-attachments/{poId}/ãÎ`
  ã `addPurchaseOrderAttachment` records the row. PDFs raw (no spec-34 downscale), images prepared. A
  failed doc upload is **non-fatal** (the PO stands; the doc is optional) ã toast warns; no re-attach
  surface until the PO-doc page lands (recorded seam).
- **Viewer:** the PR detail page (`/requests/[id]`) shows the PO's source doc when the ticket has a
  `purchase_order_id` (there's no PO detail page yet) ã reuses the Layer A `AttachmentPdf` / `ZoomablePhoto`.

**Money posture unchanged.** Gate honored: lint / typecheck / build / **885 unit** local-green ã
AskUserQuestion "Apply now" ã db:push (`20260703000000` table+bucket; **`20260703000100` fix-forward**) ã
db:types reconcile (content byte-identical; only view-block ordering differed, regen committed) ã db:test
**1104/0**.

**KEY LESSON (reusable):** the new RLS policies first shipped with **bare** `current_user_role()` /
`auth.uid()` (I mirrored pr_attachments' migration SOURCE, which predates the rank-3 eval-once hardening ã
the LIVE policies were since wrapped). **db:test file 40 (rls-eval-once) caught it** (2 failures) ã a
fix-forward migration (`20260703000100`) DROP+CREATEs both policies wrapped in `(select ãÎ)`. **Any NEW
public RLS policy must wrap auth calls in `(select ãÎ)` from the start** ã don't copy a pre-2026-06-25
migration's bare form. **Acceptance owed:** procurement user creates a PO + attaches a PDF/photo quote ã
PO created, doc saved; any member ticket's detail page shows the source doc. (Procurement-gated route ã
operator-on-live.) **NEXT:** ADR 0046 Layer B Unit 2 (the side-by-side wide create-PO surface) ã Layer C
(AI extraction). Seams: PO-doc removal/replace UI; multi-doc + quote/invoice `purpose` split; PO detail page.

## Spec 131 U1 - DC onboarding packet: data layer (2026-06-16)

Status: COMPLETE ã 2026-06-16. Migrations applied to prod; pgTAP **56 files / 1215 asserts / 0 failures**; lint clean ôñ 925 unit green ôñ build green ôñ types reconciled. (pgTAP caught a real security bug, fixed-forward in `20260709000200`: the consent RPCs' self-check `v_is_self := current_user_contractor_id() = p_contractor` is NULL for an unbound caller, so `if not (NULL or false)` = `if NULL` never fired ã an unbound visitor BYPASSED the gate and could record/revoke any contractor's consent. Fix: `coalesce(ãÎ = ãÎ, false)`. **Lesson: a `helper() = x` self-check needs coalesce-to-false whenever the helper can return NULL ã 3-valued logic silently opens the gate.** Audited the session's other RPCs: submit_contractor_bank_change + get_my_dc_payments already null-guard explicitly; only the consent pair had it.) Defines what we collect from a DC (operator: DCs are individuals ã ID, background-check consent, bank+book, phone, emergency contact; "think what might happen"; differ by type). Full design spec 131. Also recorded the LINE-OA decision (ADR 0051 addendum): one OA now (staff+DC, per-user menus, audience-gated notifications), client OA later. **Migration A** `20260709000000_contact_doc_types`: ALTER contact_doc_purpose += consent, house_registration, insurance, company_cert, vat_cert, contract (own txn; no pgTAP pin on this enum). **Migration B** `20260709000100_contractor_consents`: contractors += emergency_contact_name/relation/phone + date_of_birth (PII not money ã ride contractors grant/RLS incl. spec-130 own-row read; added to staff column write-grants); `contractor_consent_kind` enum (pdpa_data|background_check); `contractor_consents` table (dated, REVOCABLE ã PDPA; recorded_by, document_idãsigned doc, revoked_at) RLS own-contractor + staff read, RPC-only writes; `record_contractor_consent` (self-for-own OR staff) + `revoke_contractor_consent` (self-for-own OR pm/super) SECURITY DEFINER. **Consent is a first-class record, not a checkbox (PDPA spine).** pgTAP file 51 (15 asserts: catalog/columns/new doc-type cast; record gates self/staff/refused-other; read own/staff/visitor-0; revoke own + revoked_at set + unrelated-party-refused + denied-revoke-intact). **App:** pure `contractorPacketStatus` + `dcTypeOfSubtype` + required-by-type constants (TDD, 8 tests) ã completeness derived, not stored; individual checklist (ID/phone/emergency/bank/bankbook/PDPA+bg-consent) vs company (+reg cert/Á¡ Á¡.20); insurance/house-reg available but NOT required. **No TS hand-extend** this unit ã nothing in TS consumes the new schema yet (helper is self-contained, UI is U2); db:types regenerates post-push, sync guard stays green. ## Spec 134 U4a-i - PO-attachment purpose discriminator (migration) (2026-06-17)

Status: SCHEMA MIGRATION ã on branch `feat/spec134-u4a-po-attachment-purpose`, **awaiting operator PR + merge + `db:push`** (change-management gate; NOT merge-auto ã the risky/schema exception). ## Spec 134 U3 - Within-ticket partial delivery via split-on-receipt (2026-06-17)

Status: COMPLETE on prod ã 2026-06-17 (ADR 0052 accepted). Migration `20260714000000_purchase_request_partial_split` merged + `db:push`ed (dry-run clean); `db:test` **60 files / 1280 assertions / 0 failures** (new file 60 = 24); `db:types` regenerated app+worker (commit 7291dd8). The 1ã2% within-ticket case. **Schema:** `split_from_request_id` lineage column (RPC-only by the column-scoped grant posture, ADR 0038) + `split_purchase_request_on_receipt(p_request_id, p_received_qty, p_received_by?, p_delivery_note?, p_delivered_amount?)` SECURITY DEFINER RPC. Splits an in-transit PO member into a delivered portion (the ORIGINAL, reduced ã sets delivered_at so the existing derive trigger flips it to `delivered` + the audit trigger logs delivery) + a REMAINING child (new row, on_route, same PO, `split_from_request_id`=original, pr_number from the sequence default). Guards: back-office, in-transit member (purchased/on_route), `0<received<ordered`, delivered-amount range. **Amount (ADR 0052 ôÏ4, operator: proportional default + buyer-editable):** omit `p_delivered_amount` ã `round(amountûreceived/ordered,2)`; supply ã buyer value; remainder = original ã delivered (family sum = original exactly, per-WP spend preserved). One split audit row (action 'update', ADR 0027/0031 no-new-enum precedent). **UI (U3-ii):** `splitPurchaseRequestOnReceipt` action (relays the RPC) + `PartialReceiveControl` (a "Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡Á¡ˆÁ¿Á¡ÏÁ¡" expander on each in-transit PO-detail line ã qty + editable proportional-prefill amount [back office only] + note); after submit the PO badge becomes `partially_received` via the roll-up (no new derive/display logic ã the split yields ordinary tickets). **Verified-by-checklist** for the UI (auth-gated; the RPC carries the pgTAP). **Spec 134 partial-delivery story (U1 detail ôñ U2 a+b grouping ôñ U3 split ôñ U4a proof) is COMPLETE on prod.** Only U4b (Lalamove auto-POD) remains, blocked on sandbox creds.

(I recommended + built; aligns with the locked SA action-state lens, [[worklist-priority-alignment]].) ## Spec 95 (hardening) - iOS keyboard-freeze: scroll-independent repaint for short forms (2026-06-17)

Status: code COMPLETE, **NOT device-verified** (desktop preview cannot reproduce the WebKit/iOS-PWA quirk ã operator must confirm on a real iOS PWA, especially a SHORT form). **App-only, no migration.** lint ôñ typecheck ôñ **999 unit** ôñ green. **Operator: "fix the frozen screen after closing the keyboard for good."** Recurrence #2 of the spec-95 blank-after-keyboard glitch (recurrence #1 = the still-focused-field case, fixed 436ee6f). **Root cause:** every `ViewportScrollGuard.repaintScroller` path forced the repaint via `scroller.scrollBy(0,1)` ã which only repaints when `<main>` can actually scroll. A form that fits the viewport (no overflow) can't scroll ã scrollBy moves nothing ã the locked scroller (spec 64: body overflow:hidden, `<main>` the only scroller) stays blank. The 85% of long forms recovered; short ones froze "for good". **Fix:** `repaintScroller` now ALSO does a scroll-INDEPENDENT repaint ã a 1px `transform: translateY(1px)` nudge on `<main>`, restored on the next rAF (preserves any existing transform; the 1px shift is invisible for one frame) ã re-rasterizing the layer regardless of content height. Belt-and-suspenders with the existing scroll nudge; both the focusout (force=false, keeps the mid-edit field-to-field skip) and visual-viewport-resize (force=true, the still-focused recurrence) paths get it. TDD: 3rd test in `viewport-scroll-guard.test.tsx` asserts the transform is set inside the repaint and cleared next frame. **Verified-by-checklist** (jsdom has no layout/WebKit; the unit test pins the DOM contract, the real proof is the operator's device test). If it recurs again: next levers are lowering the 80px keyboard-down threshold, nudging on `geometrychange`, or firing across more frames of the ~250ms keyboard slide.

**Recurrence #3 ã "hidden, not frozen" (2026-06-17):** operator reported the prior fix didn't take and reframed the symptom ã the screen feels **hidden** (pushed off), not blank/frozen. That's a DIFFERENT bug than the missing-repaint one. The layout comment (`app/layout.tsx`) says the guard's job is to "snap the locked document back to top ãÎ (otherwise the header is pushed off)", but `git log -S scrollTo` proves the guard **never** snapped to top ã only the net-zero nudge ever existed, so the header-pushed-off case was unhandled the whole time. Mechanism: body is locked (spec 64 overflow:hidden) so `window`/document scroll should always be 0, but iOS pans the document up to reveal a focused field near the bottom and doesn't always undo that pan on keyboard-close ã the sticky header sits ABOVE the visible viewport ("hidden"). The net-zero nudge can't fix a real offset. **Fix:** `repaintScroller` now also `window.scrollTo(0, 0)` on keyboard-close (always safe ã a locked body cannot legitimately scroll; does NOT touch `<main>`'s own scroll = the reading position); gated by the same force/mid-edit logic so it never yanks the viewport while the keyboard is still up. TDD: +2 tests (snaps to top on close; does NOT snap while another field is being edited). **1001 unit** ôñ lint ôñ typecheck green. **Still NOT device-verified** ã operator must confirm on a real iOS PWA. If still seen: the pan may be a visual-viewport offset rather than a layout scroll ã next lever is also zeroing `document.documentElement.scrollTop` / handling `visualViewport.offsetTop`.

**Recurrence #4 ã "BOTTOM BLANK GAP" ã actual root cause (2026-06-17):** prior two fixes (repaint, snap-to-top) didn't take. Diagnostic questions cracked it: operator says a **blank gap at the BOTTOM** (not top, not frozen), recovered by **rotate / navigate / refresh but NOT by scrolling**. That discriminator rules out both earlier hypotheses ã not a paint bug (scrolling would fix it), not a scroll offset (snap-to-top didn't fix it). It's a **stale viewport HEIGHT**: iOS standalone PWA leaves the locked body/`<main>` at the keyboard-REDUCED `100%`/`h-full` height after the keyboard closes, so the vacated bottom strip stays blank; rotate/navigate/refresh fix it because they all force a fresh relayout at the restored height. **Fix:** `repaintScroller` now also pins `document.body.style.height` to the live `window.innerHeight` for one frame, then releases it back to the CSS `h-full` lock on the next rAF ã replicating the rotate relayout so `100%` re-resolves against the correct viewport (own rAF, restores even with no `<main>`). TDD: +1 test (pins to innerHeight, clears next frame). **1002 unit** ôñ lint ôñ typecheck green. The guard now does FOUR things on keyboard-close: height relayout (bottom gap) ôñ window snap-to-top (hidden header) ôñ scroll nudge (blank scrollable) ôñ transform nudge (blank short form). **Still NOT device-verified** ã if the bottom gap persists, escalate from the one-frame toggle to PERMANENT height tracking (set body height = innerHeight on every resize/orientationchange, the `--app-height` pattern) rather than relying on iOS to recompute `100%`.

**Recurrence #5 ã STOP guessing, instrument (2026-06-17):** the height-relayout toggle (#4) also didn't take on device ã operator: "problem still there". Three blind fixes missed because the surface is auth-gated + iOS-PWA-only (no desktop repro), so the actual stale dimension is still unknown. Switched from guessing to MEASURING: new **`ViewportDebug`** flag-gated diagnostic overlay (`src/components/features/chrome/viewport-debug.tsx`, mounted in `app/layout.tsx`) ã renders null unless `?vpdebug=1` (or `localStorage.vpdebug="1"`), otherwise a fixed top-left overlay printing live `innerHeight / visualViewport.height/offsetTop/pageTop / documentElement.clientHeight / body.rectH / main.rectH+clientH+scrollH+scrollTop / window.scrollY / doc.scrollTop / activeElement`, updated on resize/scroll/orientationchange/focusin/focusout (+vv resize/scroll). Operator opens the broken screen with `?vpdebug=1`, closes the keyboard, screenshots the numbers in the blank-gap state ã tells us which dimension is wrong ã one definitive fix instead of a 4th guess. TDD: `viewport-debug.test.tsx` (renders null without flag; overlay with flag). **App-only, flag-gated, zero impact on normal use.** lint ôñ typecheck ôñ test green. **TEMPORARY ã remove once the real fix lands.** The viewport-scroll-guard fixes (#2ã#4) stay in (each is harmless and may help one of the sub-cases); the next fix targets whatever the device numbers reveal.

**REGRESSION + REVERT (2026-06-17):** fixes #2ã#4 were NOT harmless ã operator: the orange Á¡Á¿Á¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡ÈÁ¡¿Á¡ hero bar (phase-uploader, `position: fixed inset-x-0 bottom-0`, a descendant of PageShell `<main>`) was "hovering all over the screen". Cause: the #4 `transform: translateY(1px)` nudge on `<main>` ã a CSS transform makes the element the **containing block for its `position:fixed` descendants**, so the fixed capture bar (and any fixed chrome: tab bar, modals, toasts) detaches from the viewport and tracks `<main>`. Worse, the guard's resize path fires `repaintScroller(true)` whenever `innerHeight - vv.height < 80`, which is TRUE even with no keyboard (vv.height ã innerHeight), so incidental iOS visualViewport resize/scroll events re-applied the transform constantly ã the bar wandered. **Action:** reverted `viewport-scroll-guard.tsx` + its test to the last-good pre-regression commit `4b90a3a` (436ee6f baseline = net-zero `scrollBy` nudge only); dropped the transform nudge, the `window.scrollTo(0,0)`, and the body-height pin (all three unverified, all three fired on the always-true gate). **The keyboard bug itself is still UNFIXED** ã but the guard is back to a known-good state and the regression is gone. The `ViewportDebug` overlay (af25bc5/6253d14) stays ã it's a fixed top-left `pointer-events:none` box that transforms no ancestor, so it's safe ã and it's now the path to a real diagnosis. **Lesson:** never put a `transform` on the scroll container ã it reparents all fixed chrome; and the `< 80` resize gate is too loose (fires without a keyboard), so anything behind it must be a true no-op when no keyboard is present.

**Recurrence #7 ã THE FIX (browser-verified) (2026-06-17):** operator sent the actual screenshots. They settled it: post-revert the orange bar is correctly bottom-fixed (regression gone), and the `/requests` create form is **physically clipped at the focused field (Á¡Á¡°Á¡Á¡ÏÁ¡/Á¡¨Á¡Á¿Á¡ÏÁ¡Â) with a giant blank gap below** ã the scroller is collapsed to the keyboard-reduced height, not merely unpainted. Confirms the stale-height mechanism: the locked `html ã body ã main` chain is all `h-full` (=100%); iOS standalone shrinks the web view for the keyboard and never recomputes `100%` on close, so the root stays short ã `<main>` clipped ã blank gap. The #4 one-frame toggle failed because it released back to the broken `100%`. **Fix = new `AppHeightTracker`** (`src/components/features/chrome/app-height-tracker.tsx`, mounted in `app/layout.tsx`): pins `documentElement` + `body` height to the live `window.innerHeight` and re-applies on `resize` / `visualViewport resize` / `orientationchange` / `pageshow` / `focusout`(+100ms settle), so the keyboard-close resize restores the full height for real instead of relying on iOS to recompute `100%`. `<main>`'s `h-full` follows the corrected root. **No transform** (the regression lesson) ã only an explicit root height. **Browser-VERIFIED in the preview** (the first fix in this arc confirmed before shipping): at 812 the tracker pins html/body/main = 812px; shrink the viewport to 500 + fire resize ã all track to 500; restore to 812 + fire resize ã all restore to 812 (the keyboard openãclose cycle); zero console errors. TDD: `app-height-tracker.test.tsx` (pins on mount; re-applies the restored height on resize). lint ôñ typecheck ôñ **1002 unit** (147 files) green. **Still owed: operator device confirmation** on the real iOS PWA (the in-app keyboard fires the resize/visualViewport events the preview can't), but the mechanism is now proven, not guessed. `ViewportDebug` overlay stays until confirmed, then both it and any vestigial guard nudge can be removed.

**Recurrence #8 ã wrong API found by research; corrected to visualViewport (2026-06-17):** #7 didn't work either, and web research (martijnhols.nl OSK article, htmhell viewport guide, quirksmode) explained why: **on iOS the soft keyboard is a SEPARATE LAYER ã the layout viewport never changes, so `window.innerHeight` stays constant and the window `resize` event does NOT fire when the keyboard opens/closes.** #7's `AppHeightTracker` was built on innerHeight + window resize, so it literally could not respond to the keyboard. Also confirmed: `interactive-widget=resizes-content` is NOT implemented in iOS Safari, so the declarative fix is out. **The only reliable signal is `window.visualViewport`** (`.height` shrinks; the `resize`/`scroll` events fire). **Rewrote `AppHeightTracker`** to publish `Math.round(visualViewport.height)` as the **`--app-vh`** CSS variable on `documentElement`, driven by `visualViewport.resize`/`scroll` (+ window resize/orientationchange/pageshow + focusout fallbacks + a 300ms delayed re-read for iOS's close-lag where visualViewport.height doesn't settle immediately). **PageShell's `<main>`** is now `style={{ height: "var(--app-vh, 100%)" }}` (h-full class stays as the pre-JS/non-iOS fallback) ã so the scroller tracks the actually-visible area: it shrinks above the keyboard and restores to full on close. CSS variable only ã **NO transform** (the reverted regression) and no scroll change, so fixed chrome is untouched. **Browser-VERIFIED in the preview:** at 812 ã `--app-vh` 812px, main computed 812px; shrink the visual viewport to 500 ã main 500 (the `visualViewport.resize` listener fires automatically, unlike window resize); restore to 812 ã main 812; zero console errors. TDD: `app-height-tracker.test.tsx` rewritten with a mocked `window.visualViewport` (publishes --app-vh on mount; restores on visualViewport resize). lint ôñ typecheck ôñ test green. **Device pass still owed** ã the preview proves the wiring + the right API, but only the real iOS keyboard fires the genuine visualViewport events. If it STILL fails, enable `ViewportDebug` (cornerû5 / `?vpdebug=1`) and screenshot ã the live vv.height vs innerHeight numbers will confirm the model.

**Recurrence #9 ã THE ACTUAL CAUSE, from on-device numbers (2026-06-17).** Made `ViewportDebug` ON by default (#8.5) so the next screenshot carried the metrics. It did, and it ended six rounds of guessing. **Broken state, keyboard CLOSED (`active=body`): `window.scrollY = 389`, `document.documentElement.scrollTop = 389`** (also `vv.height=744`, `vv.offsetTop=49`, `doc.clientH=793`). The body is LOCKED (spec 64 overflow:hidden) so the document must always be at scroll 0 ã it was at **389**. iOS scrolls the documentElement to reveal the focused input when the keyboard opens and **does not reset it on close**, leaving the whole page shifted up ~389px = exactly the bottom blank gap. **Not paint, not main-height, not a stale 100% ã a stuck DOCUMENT scroll.** Every prior fix was the wrong axis; the `--app-vh`/visualViewport-height experiment (#8) even made `<main>` 49px short (744 vs the 793 layout) and is now REVERTED. **Fix:** `ViewportScrollGuard` rewritten to force `documentElement.scrollTop` / `body.scrollTop` / `window.scrollTo(0,0)` back to 0 when the keyboard is DOWN (`innerHeight - visualViewport.height < 100`, so it never fights iOS revealing the input mid-edit), fired on focusout + visualViewport resize/scroll + orientationchange/pageshow, with 300ms/600ms re-reads for iOS's late settle. Only the document scroll is touched ã `<main>`'s reading scroll is left alone; no transform, no height changes. Reverted: deleted `AppHeightTracker` + its test, removed it from layout, PageShell `<main>` back to plain `h-full`. TDD: guard test rewritten (resets doc scroll to 0 when keyboard down; does NOT reset when keyboard up). lint ôñ typecheck ôñ test green; preview confirms no regression (main full height, no console errors). `ViewportDebug` stays default-on for the confirmation screenshot ã expectation: in the broken-flow re-test, `window.scrollY`/`doc.scrollTop` now read 0. Remove the overlay once the operator confirms.

**Recurrence #10 ã THE REAL ROOT: iOS auto-zoom on input focus (2026-06-17).** After the doc-scroll-reset, operator: **"zooming out to 100% solves the blank portion."** That reframes it ã the page was ZOOMED IN, and the `scrollY=389` pan was the zoom-pan, not an independent document scroll. Cause confirmed in code: the form fields are NOT the `ui/input` primitive (which is `text-base`=16px on mobile) ã they're hand-rolled `<input>`/`<select>`/`type=date`/`<textarea>` at **`text-sm` = 14px** (`purchase-request-form.tsx` lines 201/222/241/297/308/358, and the same pattern across other forms). **iOS auto-zooms into any focused input whose font-size < 16px**, and a standalone PWA leaves the page zoomed + panned after blur ã the blank portion; manual zoom-to-100% clears it. **Fix (design-preserving, global):** viewport meta now `width=device-width, initial-scale=1, maximum-scale=1, user-scalable=no` (Next `viewport` export: `maximumScale:1, userScalable:false`) ã a standalone PWA honors it and iOS no longer auto-zooms on focus, so the field-first `text-sm` sizes stay unchanged. **Trade-off:** disables pinch-zoom app-wide (acceptable for a native-feel ops PWA; operator framed zoom as the bug). Alternative if pinch-zoom must stay: bump every form input to 16px (enlarges field text, many files) ã offered to operator. Verified in preview: the rendered `<meta name=viewport>` content = `ãÎmaximum-scale=1, user-scalable=no`; no console errors. Added `vv.scale` to `ViewportDebug` so the operator can confirm scale stays 1.00. The doc-scroll-reset (#9) stays as defense. lint ôñ typecheck ôñ test green.

## Spec 95 ã RESOLVED + cleanup (2026-06-18)

Operator confirmed on device: **no more zoom, no blank portion.** Root cause = iOS auto-zoom on `<16px` form inputs; fix = `maximum-scale=1` in the root `viewport` export (global ã the only `viewport` export in the app, so it covers every form on every screen). **Cleanup refactor:** removed the temporary `ViewportDebug` overlay (component + test + layout mount + corner-tap gesture); confirmed no dangling `--app-vh` / `AppHeightTracker` / `vpdebug` references remain. **Kept** `ViewportScrollGuard`, reframed as defense-in-depth for the spec-64 body-lock invariant (document scroll stays 0 if iOS scrolls the documentElement to reveal a focused input) ã a cheap no-op in the normal case; its header comment now points at `maximum-scale=1` as the primary fix. Browser-verified: overlay gone, viewport meta still `ãÎmaximum-scale=1, user-scalable=no`, no `--app-vh` leftover, no console errors. lint ôñ typecheck ôñ test green. The spec-95 saga (#1ã#10) is closed; memory `ios-keyboard-repaint-freeze` rewritten to lead with the auto-zoom root cause + the process lesson (for device-only bugs: ship a metrics overlay first, get one screenshot, then fix the named dimension). **Possible follow-up (not done, scope):** the 14px hand-rolled inputs duplicate styling across forms ã a shared form-field input component would centralize the size decision and document the <16px-zoom trap.

## Spec 138 U4 ã KPI hero tiles tap-to-filter (2026-06-18)

Status: COMPLETE ã 2026-06-18. **App-only, no migration**; no db:push. lint ôñ typecheck ôñ **1019 unit** (+4 net: the `worklist-kpis` test rewrote from 4 ã 8 cases) ôñ green. U4 = the final mock affordance: the Á¡ÈÁ¡ÙÁ¡ˆÁ¡ÝÁ¿Á¡Á¡Á¡ñÁ¿Á¡Ù (`to_order`) and Á¡Á¡°Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¡Á¡ˆÁ¿Á¡ (`in_transit`) KPI hero tiles are now clickable band toggles (deferred from U2 "needs the bandãstatus mapping", which U3 then built), reusing the U3 band axis. **Pure helper** (`src/lib/purchasing/worklist-kpis.ts`): `buildWorklistKpis` now takes `{ summary, outstanding, filter }` (dropped the pre-built `overdueHref`/`overdueActive` pair) and derives every tile's `href`/`active` internally via `buildWorklistQuery` ã mirroring the U3 `buildWorklistStatusChips` so the toggle logic lives in one place. A `bandTile(band)` helper builds the Á¡ÈÁ¡ÙÁ¡ˆÁ¡ÝÁ¿Á¡Á¡Á¡ñÁ¿Á¡Ù/Á¡Á¡°Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¡Á¡ˆÁ¿Á¡ tiles as band toggles: `href` sets that band while clearing `overdue` (`band === key ? null : key` ã re-tapping the active tile clears it back to Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¿Á¡Á¡¨Á¡ÀÁ¡); `active = !filter.overdue && filter.band === key` (so neither band tile reads active while the overdue chase is on). ## Spec 139 U1 ã App-feel slice 3: optimistic worker active-toggle (2026-06-18)

Status: COMPLETE ã 2026-06-18. **App-only, no migration**; no db:push. lint ôñ typecheck ôñ **1021 unit** (+2 new TDD) ôñ green. App-feel slice 3 (optimistic UI) was the last deferred slice ã done CAREFULLY per-surface, payroll-safe only. U1 = the worker active-toggle on `/workers` (`WorkerRow` in `src/components/features/labor/worker-roster-manager.tsx`), the clean safe pick: already a client component, the toggle reads `worker.active` only for presentation (name colour, `(Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡)` suffix, button label), nothing server-computed beside it. **Introduces React 19 `useOptimistic`** (was zero usage in the codebase). **Change:** replaced the toggle's `busy` + success-only `router.refresh()` with `committedActive = useState(worker.active)` (post-mount truth, advanced only by a successful flip) + `optimisticActive = useOptimistic(committedActive, (_, next) => next)` + `useTransition` (`isToggling`). `toggleActive` is now sync: inside `startToggle(async ãÎ)` it `setOptimisticActive(next)` (instant flip), awaits `updateWorker({ id, active: next })`, and on ok `setCommittedActive(next)` (commit ã the optimistic falls through to it when the transition ends, **no `router.refresh`** ã the flicker is gone), on `!ok` `toast.error(result.error)` (the optimistic auto-reverts to `committedActive` = the rollback, now explained via the slice-1 toast channel ã the toggle previously failed **silently**). The row renders name colour / `(Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡)` suffix / button label from `optimisticActive`; button `disabled={isToggling}` (no double-fire race). **Untouched** (out of scope): the add-worker form + per-row edit-save stay pessimistic (they surface server validation + need the new/edited row to appear ã keep `router.refresh`; `useRouter` import stays); the action + RPC + page unchanged; no styling/class change (design-doctrine green). **Tests** (`tests/unit/worker-roster-manager.test.tsx`, +2): optimistic flip-before-server + commit (deferred-promise: label flips to Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡ + `(Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡)` suffix appears while pending, `updateWorker({id:"w1",active:false})`, **no `router.refresh`**; resolve ok ã stays flipped); rollback + toast (`{ok:false}` ã reverts to Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡, suffix gone, `toast.error` fired, no refresh). The 4 existing notes/picker tests unchanged. **Verified-by-checklist** (auth-gated pm/super `/workers` ã no preview; the component tests carry correctness; operator on-device eyeball = acceptance, the slice-76/77/78 convention). ## Spec 140 U1 ã App-feel slice 5: staggered list-enter motion (2026-06-18)

Status: COMPLETE ã 2026-06-18. **App-only, no migration**; no db:push. lint ôñ typecheck ôñ **1025 unit** (+4 new TDD) ôñ **build green** (CSS compiles ã ran `pnpm build` since CI/eslint don't cover globals.css). Route View Transitions stay a guarded spike (out of scope). **Pure helper** `src/lib/ui/list-enter.ts` `listEnterProps(index)` ã `{ className:"list-enter", style:{"--enter-index": step} }` where `step = clamp(trunc(index), 0, LIST_ENTER_STAGGER_CAP=8)` ã the cap is load-bearing (a long list's tail must not wait seconds; rows past the cap share the last step), the testable seam (4 tests: index, clamp-0/negative, cap-tail, trunc-fraction, TDD). **`globals.css`** `@keyframes list-enter` (opacity 0ã1, translateY 6pxã0) + `@media (prefers-reduced-motion: no-preference){ .list-enter{ animation: list-enter 240ms ease-out both; animation-delay: calc(var(--enter-index,0) * 35ms) } }` ã matches the spec-76 `toast-in` / spec-78 `sheet-up` pattern; `both` holds the row invisible through its stagger then settles visible; reduced-motion users get static fully-visible rows (the `from{opacity:0}` only applies while the animation is attached, which only happens inside the no-preference query ã no FOUC). **`WorklistRow`** gained optional `enterIndex?: number` (merged into the root `<Link>` ã appends the class + sets the style var; omitted ã every existing caller untouched). **`work-package-list.tsx`** passes `enterIndex={i}` from the map index at the 3 WorklistRow render sites (grouped-by-band / flat action-state / deliverable-group `<li>`) so the WP list glides in uniformly in every group mode. Server-safe (no `'use client'`; class+style are plain markup), zero data risk. **Verified-by-checklist + build** (auth-gated project page ã no preview; the helper test carries the cap logic; CSS animation isn't unit-testable ã operator on-device eyeball = acceptance, the slice-77 visual-slice precedent; design-doctrine green ã "list-enter" trips no green-\*/min-h-9 rule). ## Spec 143 U1 ã membership-scoped project visibility (ADR 0056) (2026-06-18)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-18.** lint ôñ typecheck ôñ **1086 unit** ôñ green; **pgTAP file 70 green post-push (30/30; full suite 70 files / 1455 asserts, 0 failures)**; `db:push` applied `20260728000000`; `db:types` reconciled. Operator's 2nd ask: **project_manager + site_admin now see only the projects they're involved with** (a `project_members` row OR `project_lead_id`); **project_coordinator + super_admin see all**; **procurement keeps** its spec-102 cross-project read on projects/work_packages/purchase_requests. **Full RLS isolation** (operator decision) ã enforced on every project-scoped table, not just the hub. **ADR 0056** (amends 0013) written + indexed; spec 143 written + indexed. **Migration** `20260728000000_project_visibility_scope.sql`: two SECURITY DEFINER STABLE helpers ã `can_see_project(uuid)` (super/coordinatorãtrue; pm/site_adminãmember-or-lead; else false, never NULL ã closes the [[rls-self-check-coalesce]] trap) and `can_see_wp(uuid)` (resolves WPãproject, coalesce false); definer so they read project_members/projects/work_packages without re-triggering the policies that call them (ADR 0011, no recursion). **Leadãmember backfill** in the same migration (idempotent `on conflict do nothing`) keeps current leads visible. **Rewrote 7 SELECT policies** (writes untouched), each preserving its exceptions: projects/work_packages = `procurement OR can_see_project`; deliverables = `can_see_project`; photo_logs/approvals = `can_see_wp`; purchase_requests = `requested_by=auth.uid() OR procurement OR can_see_wp` (separate appsheet_writer policy untouched); reports = `can_see_project AND role<>'site_admin'` (spec 19 ã reports still never reach site_admin). Eval-once wrapped form throughout (file 40). **Authoritative current policies pulled from pg_policies first** (not stale migration files) ã caught that spec 102 had added procurement to projects+work_packages. **pgTAP file 70** (plan 30): helper behaviour across 8 role/involvement combos + can_see_wp; projects/work_packages end-to-end per-row visibility (member sees, non-member doesn't, procurement keeps all, visitor none); child-policy wiring (qual references the right helper; reports excludes site_admin; PR keeps requester self-read). **Blast radius (expected ã access-model change):** 15 existing pgTAP suites hard-coded the old "PM/site_admin see everything" and broke on the read; fixed by seeding each fixture's PM/site_admin test users as project_members of its fixture project (scoped by test code + `auth.users.email` subquery ã `public.users` has no email column, the first attempt's trap). One ADR-0026 qual pin (file 17: "PR SELECT admits site_admin site-wide") was obsoleted by 0056 and re-pinned to the new `can_see_wp` gate. **No app code changed** ã RLS filters every cross-project list automatically (hub, worklists, payroll, reports). **ROLLOUT HEADS-UP (operator):** turning this on hides existing projects from PMs/site_admins who aren't a member/lead. Prod data is tiny (2 projects, 2 PMs, 3 site_admins; backfill enrolled the 1 lead) + super_admin sees all, so add the right people to each project via project settings (spec 80 UI). **Verified-by-checklist** (RLS is the SUT; pgTAP 70 + the regression suite carry correctness; operator on-device pass = acceptance). **Next:** U2 ã enable `project_coordinator` as a real role (roleHome ã `/projects` + add to PROJECT_VIEW_ROLES so the see-all coordinator can actually browse; currently lands on /coming-soon). Then onboarding U5ãU7 (WP seeding) remain.
