## Spec 143 U3 ã complete the membership-scoping U1 missed (2026-06-18)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-18.** lint ôñ typecheck ôñ **1096 unit** ôñ green; **full pgTAP suite 73 files / 1489 asserts, 0 failures** post-push; `db:push` applied `20260731000000` + `20260732000000` (fix-forward, below); `db:types` reconciled. A **full-project-lifecycle audit** (4 parallel explorers) found U1's "full isolation" was incomplete: three project-scoped child tables still had role-level SELECT (cross-project leak to PM/site_admin), and the SELECT-only U1 left the app write policies role-level (a non-member could write a row for a project they can't read). **Migration `20260731000000`:** scoped `labor_logs` (staff SELECT only ã the bound-contractor self-read untouched) + `work_package_dependencies` SELECT via `can_see_wp`; mirrored the membership gate onto the **8 app write policies** (photo_logs INSERT, approvals INSERT, purchase_requests app-INSERT, deliverables INSERT+UPDATE, reports INSERT, work_packages UPDATE ã each KEEPS its role list so `project_coordinator` stays read-only; `labor_logs`/`wp_dependencies` are RPC-write-only so no write policy to mirror). Authoritative current policies pulled from `pg_policies` first (not stale files). **Self-inflicted regression + fix-forward:** `20260731000000` also tried to scope `photo_markups` (SELECTã`can_see_photo_log`, + helper). `photo_markups`' INSERT policy self-references `photo_markups` (tombstone-target EXISTS) ã safe only under a trivial role SELECT policy; under a function SELECT policy Postgres raised **42P17 infinite recursion** on every markup INSERT (caught by pgTAP files 31 + the test, but the migration was already pushed ã prod markup-insert briefly broken). **`20260732000000`** reverts `photo_markups` to its original working policies + drops the unused `can_see_photo_log` ã prod un-broken. **pgTAP file 73** (plan 12): labor_logs + wp_dependencies + 7 write-mirror wirings + wp_dependencies end-to-end (member sees dep / non-member doesn't). **Two existing suites repaired:** `29-labor-capture` got a membership seed (its `correct_labor_log` id-lookup reads labor_logs as the PM ã now scoped); `31-photo-markups` returns to green once `photo_markups` reverted. **Verified-by-checklist** (RLS is the SUT; pgTAP 73 + the suite carry it). **Lesson:** scoping a SELECT policy on a table whose own write policy self-joins that table triggers 42P17 (ADR 0011 trap) ã needs a SECURITY DEFINER tombstone-target helper (pr_attachment_tombstone_target_ok precedent). **Remaining leak (documented, deferred to U4):** `photo_markups` is still role-level (low sensitivity ã drawing annotations). `labor_logs` (the sensitive one ã worker/day data) IS closed. **SPEC 143 now: U1 (RLS) + U2 (coordinator) + U3 (labor_logs/wp_dependencies + write-mirror) on prod; U4 (photo_markups via definer helper) is the one open item.**

## Spec 145 ã lock new work on a completed project (warranty-aware) (2026-06-18)

Status: **SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-18.** lint ôñ typecheck ôñ **1100 unit** ôñ green; **full pgTAP suite 76 files / 1521 asserts, 0 failures** post-push; `db:push` applied `20260735000000`; `db:types` reconciled. Operator decision: a project locks once completed ã **caveat:** completion ã  full closure (client retains a warranty %, Buildall 5% for a year; defects surface in that window), so the lock blocks NEW work but must NOT block warranty defect-rework. **Enforcement = a `BEFORE INSERT` trigger on `work_packages`** (`work_packages_block_insert_on_closed_project`, raises `P0002`) gated by `project_is_open(uuid)` (status in active/on_hold) ã **one chokepoint** over every WP-creation path (manual/template/copy/CSV) without re-typing the 3 creation RPCs, and **INSERT-only** so spec-144 reopen-to-rework (an UPDATE) + the rework WP's capture/labor/approval cycle keep working on a completed project (the warranty carve-out falls out for free; gates on WP status, not project status). The **project record stays editable** (status ã active to reopen the project; record retention notes in settings). **Actions** map `P0002` ã "Á¿Á¡Á¡ÈÁ¡Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡ÈÁ¡Á¡çÁ¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡Á¿Á¡ËÁ¿Á¡Ï Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¡ÈÁ¡Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡ÈÁ¡Á¿Á¡ÙÁ¡ãÎ" (createWorkPackage/copyWorkPackages/applyWpTemplate/importWorkPackagesCsv). **UI (project page):** added `status` to the project select + `projectOpen`; when closed, hides the seeding controls + onboarding checklist and shows a lock banner pointing to settings. **pgTAP file 76** (plan 11): helper truth table, direct-insert + all 3 RPCs blocked on a completed project (P0002), create still works on active, **reopen-for-defect still works on a completed project (warranty)**; fixtures seed WPs while active then flip to completed (so the seed doesn't trip the trigger). **Verified-by-checklist** (DB lock pgTAP'd; UI gate + action mapping are thin glue over the tested DB behavior). **Out of scope (deliberate):** retention %/warranty billing ã a finance feature the app resists (status-only at most, per ceo-review); not built. **Project lifecycle now complete:** active/on_hold (full edit) ã completed (locked for new work; warranty: defects reopen individual WPs to rework ã fix ã re-approve) ã archived; reopen the project via statusãactive. **Audit-found project-status gap closed.**

per-line `Trash2` remove ã `removePlanLine`; **submitted/approved = read-only** (no add/remove). **Actions** `addPlanLine` (get-or-create `create_supply_plan` ã `add_supply_plan_line`) / `removePlanLine`: `getActionUser` + RPC + map `23505`("already planned")/`42501`/`22023` + `revalidatePath(supplyPlanHref)`. **Entry:** a `ClipboardList` chip on the project header (isManagerRole block) ã `supplyPlanHref`. **Feature folder `supply-plan` added to `feature-components-structure` ALLOWED_DOMAINS** (the 4th anti-drift guard hit this session). **Decision:** U2 form **requires a WP** per line (the core qty-per-WP case) ã avoids the nullable-uuid RPC-arg typing issue (a non-null `uuid` arg types as non-null `string`); site-general (null WP) stays schema-supported for a later "Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¿Á¡Á¿Á¡Á¡ÈÁ¡Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡È" option. **Tests:** `supply-plan-manager.test.tsx` (4) + pgTAP 177 (9). **NEXT:** U3 submit + PD approve/reject (freeze the baseline), then U4 reactive reason codes, U5 measurement.

## Spec 176 ã Supply Plan, U3: submit + PD approve/reject (2026-06-22)

## Spec 177 ã Store + Stock-In (Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ý) at cost (inventory Phase 3), U1: data foundation (2026-06-22)

Status: **U1 SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-22.** lint ôñ typecheck ôñ **vitest 213 files / 1402** (DB-only ã no unit-test delta) ôñ **db:test 130 files / 2445 / 0** (file 181, 24 asserts) ôñ `pnpm build` green; db:push applied `20260809000000`; db:types regenerated. **Phase 3 of the on-site storage/inventory arc** (after spec 175 catalog + spec 176 supply plan). The store is a transfer-pricing BU; this unit puts STOCK ON HAND ã goods enter the store, at COST, and the store knows what it holds and what it's worth. **Cost-first staging is a locked dial:** the sell-to-WP margin layer + the flip of `wp_profit` to at-issue-sell-price + external sales are LATER phases, explicitly NOT this spec. **Operator decisions (AskUserQuestion, all 3 recommended):** (1) **stock-in source = standalone catalog-keyed receipt** ã a "store buys catalog item X, qty Y, at unit-cost Z from supplier S" entry keyed on `catalog_item_id`; it does **not** touch the existing PR/PO/delivery flow (whose lines are FREE-TEXT, no catalog link), so zero purchasing-break risk; a future POãstore linkage is flagged. (2) **on-hand = per-project, NO `stores` table** ã keyed by `(project_id, catalog_item_id)`, the project's on-site store is implicit ("1 unit per site"), RLS rides existing `can_see_project`, issue-to-WP (Phase 4) stays in-project. (3) **moving-avg cost tracked NOW** ã `qty_on_hand` + `total_value` ã avg = value/qty (the COST basis, not the sell/margin layer). **Design (spec 177 ôÏU1, DB-only ã mirrors the 176-U1 cadence; /store UI is U2):** `stock_receipts` (append-only Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ý events: project_id, catalog_item_id, qty>0, **unit snapshotted from the catalog item at receipt**, unit_costãË0, **`total_cost` GENERATED `qty*unit_cost`**, nullable supplier_id, received_at, note, created_by ã no UPDATE/DELETE policy; corrections = a later reversal unit per CLAUDE.md append-only doctrine) + `stock_on_hand` (derived, PK `(project_id, catalog_item_id)`, qty_on_hand + total_value; moving-avg cost is DERIVED not stored). **RPC `record_stock_in(project, item, qty, unit_cost, supplier, note)`** SECURITY DEFINER: role gate = `BACK_OFFICE_ROLES` (pm/super/procurement/director ã the cost-bearing curation tier; documented Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ý actor is procurement); membership = `can_see_project(project) OR current_user_role()='procurement'` (procurement is a cross-project curator, mirrors spec 171/172); validates project/active-catalog-item/qty>0/unit_costãË0/supplier-exists (all 22023), non-memberã42501; inserts the receipt + **additively** upserts on-hand (`on conflict ãÎ do update set qty+=, value+=`) ã a pure stock-IN needs no weighted-avg recompute (that's issue-OUT, Phase 4). **READ:** both tables SELECT = `can_see_project OR procurement` arm (procurement must read what it writes); no write policy ã the RPC is the sole writer. **Migration `20260809000000`, pgTAP `181`** (structure + anon-deny, procurement cross-project + PM-member happy paths, moving-avg maths across two receipts at different unit costs ã value 600/qty 20 = avg 30, generated total_cost, unit snapshot, every deny/validation branch). **THREE traps caught + fixed forward:** (1) **bare `current_user_role()` in an RLS policy** ã the "no public policy calls current_user_role() bare" guard pgTAP went RED ã Postgres-RLS perf pattern requires `(select public.current_user_role())` (I'd wrapped `can_see_project` but not the role call); fixed both policies (edited the migration file AND applied the wrap live via `supabase db query --file` so file==DB, no noise migration). (2) **`suppliers.created_by` is NOT NULL with no default** ã my fixture inserted only (id, name) ã the whole 181 file errored at setup ("not ok - 181"); added created_by. (3) **plan() undercount** ã `plan(22)` but 24 asserts ran (miscounted the read-posture section) ã `plan(24)`. **Lesson:** when a fixture row errors, the runner reports the whole file `not ok` with the diagnostic hidden if you grep-filter the output ã re-run unfiltered to a file to see the `# ERROR:` line. **Out of scope (flagged):** /store UI (read on-hand + record form) = U2; Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡/Issue + two-party custody + weighted-avg-cost decrement = Phase 4; GL posting of stock-in (Dr Inventory/Cr AP into the spec-149 outbox) = later; POãstore linkage (needs catalog_item_id on PR/PO lines first); receipt reversal/correction; required supplier; stock count/variance; SA self-receive (self-governance). **NEXT (Phase 3 cont.):** U2 = the `/store` surface (read on-hand per project + the record-stock-in form, back-office tier).

## Spec 177 ã Store + Stock-In, U3: Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡/Issue (the first OUT flow), at weighted-avg cost (2026-06-22)

Status: **U3 SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-22.** lint ôñ typecheck ôñ **vitest 214 files / 1409** (DB-only ã no unit-test delta) ôñ **db:test 131 files / 2465 / 0** (file 182, 20 asserts) ôñ `pnpm build` green; db:push applied `20260809000200`; db:types regenerated. The first OUT flow: a work package draws stock from its project's store; the store issues it OUT at the **moving-average cost** (the COST basis ã the sell/margin layer stays locked out). **Design (spec 177 ôÏU3, DB-only ã mirrors the U1 cadence; the Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡ UI is U4):** `stock_issues` (append-only Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡ events: project_id, catalog_item_id, **work_package_id NOT NULL** = the WP drawn for, qty>0, **unit snapshot**, **unit_cost = moving-avg at issue**, **`total_cost` GENERATED**, note, issued_by, issued_at ã no UPDATE/DELETE policy; corrections = a later reversal). **RPC `issue_stock(project, item, wp, qty, note default null)`** SECURITY DEFINER: role gate = **SITE_STAFF_ROLES** (site_admin draws at the WP + the PM tier ã **NOT procurement**, which does Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ý IN not Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡ OUT ã the gate that differs from U1/U2) + `can_see_project`; validates qty>0 / WP-in-project / active-catalog-item / **sufficient on-hand** (all 22023), non-memberã42501; **locks the on-hand row (`for update`)**, computes `avg = round(total_value/qty_on_hand, 2)`, decrements `qty_on_hand -= qty` and `total_value -= qty*avg` ã **fully depleting forces total_value to 0** so rounding dust never lingers ã and writes the issue at the snapshot avg cost. **READ:** `stock_issues` SELECT = `can_see_project OR procurement` (consistent with receipts/on-hand; policy uses the wrapped `(select current_user_role())` ã the U1 guard lesson applied up front). **Migration `20260809000200`, pgTAP `182`** (structure + anon-deny; site_admin issues 5 of 20@avg30 ã on-hand 15 / value 450, issue unit_cost 30 / total_cost 150; issue the remaining 15 ã qty 0 / value forced 0; insufficient-stock 22023; PM-member issues a 2nd item; qtyãÊ0 + WP-from-another-project 22023; non-member + visitor 42501; member reads 3 issues, outsider 0). **Clean first push ã no traps** (the U1/U2 lessons preempted them: policy wrapped, fixtures complete, plan count correct). **Out of scope (flagged):** the Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡ UI (a button on the WP detail and/or /store) = **U4**; **two-party custody handshake** (store-keeper hands / receiver attests, reuse polymorphic consents) = later; **wiring issue cost into `wp_profit`** (the WP material cost = at-issue cost) = the cost-attribution/margin layer, deliberately deferred; ## Spec 177 ã Store + Stock-In, U9: stock count / variance (shrinkage) (2026-06-22)

Status: **U9 SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-22.** lint ôñ typecheck ôñ **vitest 216 files / 1426** (DB-only ã no unit delta) ôñ **db:test 133 files / 2502 / 0** (file 184, 19 asserts) ôñ `pnpm build` green; db:push applied `20260809000400`; db:types regenerated. The self-governance shrinkage mechanism: a physical count reconciles on-hand to reality, and the variance valued at cost is the store-BU P&L hit. **Design (spec 177 ôÏU9, DB-only; the count UI is U10):** `stock_counts` (append-only physical-count events: project_id, catalog_item_id, **system_qty snapshot**, counted_qtyãË0, **unit + unit_cost snapshot** (the moving-avg at count), **GENERATED `variance` = counted ã system** and **`variance_value` = (counted ã system) û unit_cost** ã both generated from plain columns only, no generated-from-generated chain; note, counted_by ã no UPDATE/DELETE policy; a wrong count is corrected by a fresh count). **RPC `record_stock_count(project, item, counted_qty, note default null)`** SECURITY DEFINER: role gate = **SITE_STAFF_ROLES** (site_admin keeps the physical store + the PM tier ã NOT procurement) + `can_see_project`; `counted_qty >= 0` (22023); **locks the on-hand row ã counting is limited to items the store already tracks** (no on-hand row ã 22023 "not stocked"; cataloguing found-untracked stock is a Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ý, not a count); snapshots the unit (even a DEACTIVATED-but-still-on-hand item counts), computes `avg = round(value/qty, 2)` (the unchanged cost basis ã a count adjusts QUANTITY not unit cost), logs the count, and **reconciles on-hand to the counted truth** (`qty_on_hand = counted`, `total_value = round(counted û avg, 2)`). **READ:** `stock_counts` SELECT = `can_see_project OR procurement` (the wrapped `(select current_user_role())` from the start). **Migration `20260809000400`, pgTAP `184`** (structure + anon-deny; count DOWN 100ã90 ã on-hand 90/value 900, variance ã10 / variance_value ã100 / system_qty 100; count UP 90ã95; count to ZERO ã value 0; unstocked-item + negative-qty 22023; non-member + visitor 42501; member reads the count history). **Clean first push ã no traps** (the prior units' lessons held: policy wrapped, fixtures complete, plan count correct). **Out of scope (flagged):** **U10 = the count UI** (a Á¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ÏÁ¡Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¡ action per on-hand row on /store ã counted-qty form ã `record_stock_count`, showing the variance); Status: **U10 SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-22.** lint ôñ typecheck ôñ **vitest 216 files / 1430 (+4: store-manager count)** ôñ `pnpm build` green. **No DB change** (reuses the U9 `record_stock_count` RPC) ã no migration, no db:test delta. Self-inflicted test fix: `getByText(/-2/)` also matched the `PRC-2026-002` project option ã tightened to `/Á¡ˆÁ¿Á¡ÏÁ¡Á¡Á¿Á¡ýÁ¡ -2/`. **Browser pass = operator on-device.** **Out of scope (flagged):** a site_admin store-count surface; a count-history view; reversals of receipt/issue; found-untracked-stock costing; wiring issue cost into `wp_profit`; the late margin layer; the deferred /store-manager receiver picker + manager confirm-on-behalf. **NEXT (Phase 3 cont.):** reversals (append-only negative receipt/issue correction), then the late margin layer (sell-to-WP per-level, flip `wp_profit` to at-issue-sell-price ã the cost-first dial is still locked).

## Spec 177 ã Store + Stock-In, U11: reversals (undo a wrong Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ý / Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡) (2026-06-22)

Status: **U11 SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-22.** lint ôñ typecheck ôñ **vitest 216 files / 1430** (DB-only ã no unit delta) ôñ **db:test 134 files / 2520 / 0** (file 185, 18 asserts) ôñ `pnpm build` green; db:push applied `20260809000500`; db:types regenerated. The correction mechanism: a wrong stock movement is undone by an append-only reversal that reverses its on-hand effect ã never by editing the original. **Design (spec 177 ôÏU11, DB-only; the reversal UI is U12):** `stock_reversals` (append-only: project_id, catalog_item_id, **a TYPED FK to the reversed `receipt_id` OR `issue_id` ã exactly one** per CLAUDE.md's no-mixed-content-reference rule, enforced by a `(receipt_id is not null) <> (issue_id is not null)` CHECK; `qty` + `value_delta` (the on-hand value change applied ã negative for a receipt reversal, positive for an issue reversal); note, reversed_by ã no UPDATE/DELETE policy). **A partial unique index per FK (`where ãÎ is not null`) blocks reversing the same movement twice (ã 23505).** **RPC `reverse_stock_receipt(receipt_id, note default null)`** (BACK_OFFICE gate ã the Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ý audience; membership = `can_see_project OR procurement`): loads the receipt, **locks on-hand and guards `qty_on_hand >= receipt.qty`** (you cannot un-receive stock that has since been issued out ã 22023), inserts the reversal (unique check first), then subtracts `qty` + `total_cost` (depletion ã value 0). **RPC `reverse_stock_issue(issue_id, note default null)`** (SITE_STAFF gate + `can_see_project`): inserts the reversal, then **adds the issue's `qty` + `total_cost` back** to on-hand (no negative risk). **READ:** `stock_reversals` SELECT = `can_see_project OR procurement` (wrapped role call). **Migration `20260809000500`, pgTAP `185`** (structure + anon-deny; procurement reverses a 30-receipt ã on-hand 50ã20 / value 500ã200 / value_delta ã300; double-reverse ã 23505; a receipt whose qty > on-hand ã 22023; site_admin reverses a 10-issue ã on-hand 20ã30 / value_delta +100; double-reverse issue ã 23505; visitor + non-member denies 42501; member reads the reversal history). **One trap caught by db:test + fixed forward ã [[prc-ops-db-migration-lessons]]:** the receipt reversal checked the on-hand guard (`qty >= receipt.qty`) BEFORE the insert, so a double-reverse ã where the first reversal already dropped on-hand below the receipt qty ã raised 22023 (guard) instead of the intended 23505 (unique). Fix: **do the unique insert FIRST**, then the on-hand guard (a failed guard still rolls the insert back since the whole RPC call aborts atomically); applied live via `CREATE OR REPLACE` + edited the migration file (file==live). Lesson: **when an RPC has both a uniqueness constraint and a state guard, attempt the unique write before the state check** so the "already done" error wins over the "state changed" error. **Out of scope (flagged):** **U12 = the reversal UI** (a Á¡Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡È button on the recent-receipts/issues lists ã `reverse_stock_receipt`/`reverse_stock_issue`, with a confirm); the custody implication of reversing a CONFIRMED issue (the material returns after the worker attested ã allowed as a correction, surfaced later); intervening-activity makes a receipt reversal's avg approximate (exact for the immediate-mistake case); the late margin layer. **NEXT (Phase 3 cont.):** U12 ã the reversal UI, then the late margin layer (needs an operator decision ã it rewires `wp_profit`).

## Spec 177 ã Store + Stock-In, U12: the reversal UI (Á¡Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡È on /store) (2026-06-22)

Status: **U12 SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-22.** lint ôñ typecheck ôñ **vitest 216 files / 1435 (+5: store-manager reversal)** ôñ `pnpm build` green. **No DB change** (reuses the U11 `reverse_stock_receipt` / `reverse_stock_issue` RPCs) ã no migration, no db:test delta. The U11 reversal engine gets its UI: undo a wrong Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ý/Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡ from /store with a confirm. **Surface:** `/store` gains a **Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ýÁ¡ËÁ¿Á¡ýÁ¡ˆÁ¡¡Á¡** (recent receipts, last 10) list ã each row a `Á¡Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡È` control; and the existing **Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡Á¡ËÁ¿Á¡ýÁ¡ˆÁ¡¡Á¡** list gains a `Á¡Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡È` control per issue. Both use the **shared `ConfirmActionButton`** (spec 67 ã button ã themed ConfirmDialog ã action in a transition ã refresh; replaces window.confirm) with a per-row confirm message ("ãÎÁ¡Á¡ÙÁ¡Á¡Á¡¯Á¡Á¡¿Á¡Á¡Á¡ÝÁ¡Á¡ÙÁ¡ÙÁ¡Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡Á¡ˆÁ¿Á¡Á¡ÈÁ¿" / "ãÎÁ¡Á¡ÙÁ¡Á¡Á¡¯Á¡Á¡¿Á¡Á¡Á¡ñÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ýÁ¡ˆÁ¿Á¡Á¡ÈÁ¿"). **Gates (the key asymmetry):** receipt reversal = `reverse_stock_receipt` gate = **BACK_OFFICE = exactly the /store audience**, so the receipt Á¡Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡È shows for **every /store user (incl. procurement ã it records Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ý)**; issue reversal = `reverse_stock_issue` gate = SITE_STAFF ã on /store that is the **manager tier**, so the issue Á¡Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡È is gated on `canIssue` (procurement can't reverse an issue). **`StoreManager`** gains a `receipts` prop + the two `ConfirmActionButton`s; **`reverseStockReceipt` / `reverseStockIssue` server actions** (`src/app/store/actions.ts`) map the RPCs' 42501 / 23505 ("Á¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡ÈÁ¡Á¡çÁ¿Á¡Á¡¿Á¡Á¡Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ËÁ¿Á¡Ï") / 22023 ("Á¡Á¡ÙÁ¡Á¡Á¡¿Á¡Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡Á¡ÙÁ¡ÙÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ËÁ¿Á¡Ï Á¡Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡ÈÁ¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ýÁ¿Á¡ÀÁ¿Á¿Á¡Á¿"). **Page:** /store fetches the project's recent `stock_receipts` (last 10, joined catalog_items). **No DB / migration / guards / nav.** **Test (written first, RED proven ã 4 failed/17 passed before, 21/21 after):** `store-manager.test.tsx` reversal describe (the recent-Á¡ÈÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡ý list + its Á¡Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡È control for any user; the receipt reversal after confirm ã `reverseStockReceipt`; the issue Á¡Á¡ËÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¡ÈÁ¡ýÁ¡ÂÁ¡Á¡ýÁ¡È only when `canIssue`; the issue reversal after confirm ã `reverseStockIssue`). **Browser pass = operator on-device.** **Out of scope (flagged):** reversal controls on the WP-detail issues list (only /store for now); bring the design choice via AskUserQuestion before building.

## Spec 178 ã Store margin layer (transfer pricing), U1: sell-rate data + setter (2026-06-22)

Status: **U1 SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-22.** lint ôñ typecheck ôñ **vitest 216 files / 1435** ôñ **db:test 135 files / 2534 / 0** (+1 file 186, +14 asserts) ôñ `pnpm build` green; db:push applied `20260809000600`; db:types regenerated (app + worker). The BIG FORK resolved: operator AskUserQuestion locked all four recommended dials ã (1) **flat per-item sell rate** (global, not markup, not per-project), (2) sell **captured at issue**, (3) `wp_profit` materials = **ADD store-sell beside GL purchases** (disjoint source, no double-count), (4) external/3rd-party sales **deferred**. U1 = the data foundation (DB-only, mirrors `set_sell_rate` from spec 161 U1): `item_sell_rates` (PK `catalog_item_id`, `sell_rate numeric(12,2) >= 0`, **zero authenticated grant** = the margin-sensitive money posture) + `set_item_sell_rate(p_catalog_item_id, p_sell_rate)` definer (super_admin gate, upsert, audit row, anon EXECUTE revoked). mig `20260809000600`, pgTAP file 186. **Trap caught by db:test (1 file failed, 0 of its asserts ran): the test read the zero-grant `item_sell_rates` while `set local role authenticated` ã permission-denied aborts the WHOLE transactional file (the \_tap_buf inserts roll back too ã "not ok - 186" with 0 assertions). Fix = read the zero-grant table only as OWNER (before `set role` / after `reset role`); only the setter CALLS run under `authenticated` (the spec-161 pgTAP-98 pattern).** Convention note: the store family uses `22023` for value/existence validations (vs the labour family's `P0001`) ã kept `22023` here for store consistency.

## Spec 178 ã Store margin layer, U2: issue snapshots the sell price (2026-06-22)

Status: **U2 SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-22.** lint ôñ typecheck ôñ **vitest 216 files / 1435** ôñ **db:test 136 files / 2546 / 0** (+1 file 187, +12 asserts) ôñ `pnpm build` green; db:push applied `20260809000700`; db:types regenerated (+sell_price/total_sell on stock_issues, app + worker). The WP "buys" the stock at issue: `stock_issues` += `sell_price numeric(12,2)` (nullable ã legacy/cost-only rows have none) + `total_sell numeric(16,2)` generated `qty * sell_price`. `issue_stock` (**same 6-arg signature ã CREATE OR REPLACE, body-only, grants + pgTAP 182/183 sig pins preserved, no DROP**) computes `v_sell = coalesce((select sell_rate from item_sell_rates where catalog_item_id=ãÎ), v_avg)` ã the **costing rule**: an unpriced item sells AT COST (zero store margin), never null, so wp_profit (U4) is never understated. The snapshot is immutable (append-only) ã changing a rate only affects future issues (pgTAP proves: bump 50ã80, the old issue keeps 50). issue_stock is SECURITY DEFINER so it reads the zero-grant `item_sell_rates` as owner. **Lesson re-applied:** miswrote `plan(10)` for 12 assertions (the bare `set_item_sell_rate` call isn't an assertion but the 3 post-bump checks are) ã fixed to `plan(12)`. NEXT = U3 `store_pnl` read (per-item cost/sell/margin + shrinkage, reversed issues excluded).

## Spec 179 ã Purchase request links a catalog item (2026-06-22)

Status: **U1+U2 SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-22.** lint ôñ typecheck ôñ **vitest 217 files / 1441 (+6: validate-purchase-request catalogItemId ôñ purchase-request-form-catalog)** ôñ **db:test 137 files / 2554 / 0** (+1 file 188, +8 asserts) ôñ `pnpm build` green; db:push applied `20260809000800`; db:types regenerated (app + worker). Procurement's request (spec 171): "items not selectable yet" ã operator AskUserQuestion chose the **real FK link** (not a UI snapshot). `purchase_requests` gains a **nullable `catalog_item_id` FK ã catalog_items** (spec 175 master); picking a catalog item links it AND prefills `item_description` (`baseItem` + ` specAttrs`) + `unit` (a human snapshot that survives a later catalog edit/deactivation); the off-catalog free-text path stays (link null). **Posture mirrors `reason_code` (spec 176 U4):** nullable, NO default (legacy rows null), link set ONCE at create ã INSERT-granted, not UPDATE-granted. **THE GRANT TRAP (caught proactively, not by a red db:test):** `purchase_requests` carries **column-scoped INSERT grants** to `authenticated` (mig `20260616000400` revoked table-level insert + re-granted an explicit column list), so a new column is NOT covered ã the session-client insert would be denied; the migration adds `grant insert (catalog_item_id) ãÎ to authenticated`. **SELECT is table-level (mig `20260608120000`, never revoked) ã the new column is readable without a grant** (unlike the spec-174 column-grant-SELECT trap ã different table, different posture). No RLS change (the INSERT policy pins requested_by/source/role only; the FK is unconstrained + nullable). **Validator** `validateCreatePurchaseRequest` += optional `catalogItemId` (uuid-or-null; blank/null/omitted ã null; bad uuid ã "Á¡ÈÁ¡¨Á¡ÝÁ¡ˆÁ¡ÏÁ¡ÝÁ¡ˆÁ¡Á¡¡Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¡Á¡Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡ËÁ¿Á¡ÙÁ¡Á¿Á¡ÀÁ¿Á¡Á¡¿Á¡Á¡Á¿Á¡ÙÁ¡"); the exact-shape `toEqual` test updated with `catalogItemId: null`. **Action** `createPurchaseRequest` writes `catalog_item_id`. **Form** (`purchase-request-form.tsx`) += optional `catalogItems` prop (omitted/empty ã picker hidden = free-text-only, **so the existing form tests are unaffected**) + a `Á¿Á¡ËÁ¡ñÁ¡ÙÁ¡Á¡ÏÁ¡ÝÁ¡ˆÁ¡Á¡¡Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¡Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡ËÁ¿Á¡ÙÁ¡` `<select>` grouped by `item_category` (mirrors the supply-plan picker; option `baseItem ôñ specAttrs (unit)`, a `Á¡Á¡ÙÁ¡Á¿Á¡Á¡Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡ËÁ¿Á¡ÙÁ¡ (Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡ÀÁ¡Á¿Á¿Á¡ÙÁ¡)` value="" escape hatch); picking prefills the description + unit (a catalog unit outside COMMON_UNITS falls to the Á¡ÙÁ¡ñÁ¿Á¡ Á¿ free-text unit input). **Both form callers feed the active catalog:** `projects/[id]/work-packages/[wpId]` (procurement + SA ã added to the existing Promise.all) and `review/work-packages/[wpId]` (PM review ã a new fetch). **Migration `20260809000800`, pgTAP `188`** (column nullable-uuid + no-default; FK to catalog_items; INSERT+SELECT granted, UPDATE not ã set once). **Test-first proven:** 6 validator/form cases RED before impl. **Out of scope (flagged):** reconciling PR ã stock-in ã on-hand by `catalog_item_id` (the payoff the link unlocks ã a later store unit); spend-by-item analytics; back-filling historical free-text requests; a typeahead/search picker (the grouped `<select>` matches supply-plan; a search box is a later UX unit if the catalog grows). **NEXT = the rest of procurement's "few requests" (operator to explain).**

## Spec 180 ã PR item picker, U3: category tap no longer ghost-selects an item (2026-06-23)

Status: **U3 SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-23.** lint ôñ typecheck ôñ **vitest unchanged (217 / 1445)** ôñ `pnpm build` green. **No DB change, single-file fix.** Operator: "tapping item categories sometimes turns into item selection." Root cause: the category chips are `RadioChip`s (an sr-only native radio). Tapping one focuses the radio ã `BottomSheet`'s panel `onFocus={handleFocusCapture}` runs `scrollIntoView({ block: "center" })` (rAF) on the focused control ã intended to lift a text input above the keyboard, but on a chip it **scrolls the result list up under the finger**, so the synthesized touch `click` lands on a result row. The rAF timing is why it's intermittent ("sometimes"); it only misfires when the chip wasn't already centered. **Fix (`catalog-item-picker.tsx`):** `onFocusCapture={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}` on the category chip-row `<div>` ã a capture-phase stop halts the focus event before it bubbles to the panel's `onFocus`, so the sheet doesn't re-center on a chip (the radio still focuses; selection/a11y intact). The search input is untouched ã still centers for the keyboard. **Not unit-testable** (the bug is touch + scrollIntoView layout timing, absent in jsdom ã no real scroll/touch); existing category-chip filter test still green; verified on-device by the operator. **NEXT = the rest of procurement's "few requests".**

a non-member PM stays denied (procurement arm didn't widen PM); anon still can't EXECUTE (CREATE OR REPLACE preserved the revoke ã no DROP+CREATE anon re-grant). **Clean first push ã no traps** (CREATE OR REPLACE preserved grants; ## Spec 181 ã Supply Plan bulk PR, U3: the generation engine (2026-06-23)

Status: **U3 SHIPPED to prod ã 2026-06-23.** lint ôñ typecheck ôñ **db:test 140 files / 2584 / 0** (+1 file 191, +10 asserts) ôñ **vitest unchanged** (DB + action only, no UI) ôñ `pnpm build` (pending the U3+U4 ship ã built green at U2) ; db:push applied `20260809001100`; db:types regenerated (+`supply_plan_line_id` column + `generate_purchase_requests_from_plan` RPC). The "bulk PR" engine: an approved plan's selected lines ã purchase_requests in one call. **Schema:** `purchase_requests.supply_plan_line_id` (nullable FK ã supply_plan_lines) + a **PARTIAL unique index** `where supply_plan_line_id is not null` (a line converts at most once = idempotency; NULL ã the vast majority ã unconstrained). No authenticated INSERT grant needed for the new column ã the definer RPC owns the insert. **RPC `generate_purchase_requests_from_plan(p_plan_id, p_line_ids uuid[])`** (mig `20260809001100`): gate PM/super/director/**procurement** (membership skipped for procurement); plan must be **`approved`** (else 22023); loops the selected lines, **born-`approved` PRs** (status='approved', `approved_by = the plan's approver`, decided_at=now, reason_code NULL, source 'app', requested_by=auth.uid(), supply_plan_line_id=line) ã **inherits the plan's PD approval, no per-PR re-approval**; **skips already-linked lines** (idempotent, returns the count); **whole-project lines (null WP) ã 22023** (a PR is raised against a WP). **Born-approved is SAFE ã verified the triggers:** the only AFTER-INSERT trigger `notify_pr_created` fires `when (new.status = 'requested')` so a born-approved PR sends NO false "needs approval" notification; every other purchase_requests trigger (audit_decision/cancellation/appsheet, derive, set_updated_at, notify_status_change) is AFTER/BEFORE **UPDATE** ã none fire on insert. **`auth.uid()` inside SECURITY DEFINER returns the CALLING user** (procurement), not the owner ã JWT claims are session context, role is what DEFINER swaps (same as approve_supply_plan). **Accuracy fix (the design catch):** `supply_plan_accuracy` (CREATE OR REPLACE, grants preserved) gains `and r.supply_plan_line_id is null` in the prs CTE ã **plan-generated PRs (reason NULL but PLANNED) are excluded from the reactive/untagged counts**, else every planned order would read as a planning miss. **Action `generatePlanPurchaseRequests`** relays the RPC (maps 42501/22023; revalidates /supply-plan + /requests). pgTAP `191`: procurement generates 2 ã born-approved + approved_by=PD; idempotent re-gen ã 0; null-WP ã 22023; non-approved plan ã 22023; **accuracy: the 2 generated PRs excluded from untagged (0), the 1 reactive PR still counts as unplanned_miss (1)**. Generated PRs flow into the existing create_purchase_order (operates on approved PRs) = procurement's price-compare/PO step. **NEXT = U4** ã the convert-mode UI (checkboxes on an approved plan's lines + Á¡ˆÁ¡ÈÁ¿Á¡ýÁ¡Á¡Á¡°Á¡Á¡ÙÁ¡Á¡ñÁ¿Á¡Ù, per-row PR-Á¿Á¡ËÁ¿Á¡Ï badge), per the mockup.

**BUG FIX (from feedback triage) SHIPPED prod 2026-06-25 (mig `20260813001500`, pgTAP 11 6/6) ã
project_director could not upload photos.** Symptom (real report 0e3a7f3d, a PD): adding a photo
stuck forever on "Á¡ÈÁ¡ÙÁ¡ˆÁ¿Á¡Á¡ÈÁ¡¿Á¡ãÎÁ¿Á¡ÀÁ¡ñÁ¿Á¡ÙÁ¡ÀÁ¡çÁ¡ˆÁ¡ÝÁ¡Á¡Á¡ýÁ¡" on every device with working net. **ROOT CAUSE:** ADR 0058
(spec 152, mig 20260752000000) made project_director a see-all writer and added it to the
`photo_logs` INSERT policy ã but that sweep only reconstructed `public.*` table policies from
pg_policies; the `photos` STORAGE bucket upload policy (on `storage.objects`, mig 20260524040000)
was MISSED. So a PD's capture enqueued ã bytes upload to `photos` denied by RLS ã offline queue
(`src/lib/photos/upload-queue.ts`) stuck at step `upload`, retried forever ã the generic "waiting
for signal" banner never cleared (it never reached the photo_logs insert, which already admits PD).
**FIX:** DROP+CREATE "photos uploads by sa/pm/super" adding `project_director` (kept the policy name
ã precedent: 20260752 added PD to "photo_logs insert by sa/pm/super" without renaming). Verified
live (pg_policies with_check now lists project_director). Test-first: pgTAP 11 +assert (plan 5ã6,

(treats authz denial like a connectivity wait ã classifyStorageUploadError only detects alreadyExists).

## Spec 205 ã WP labor budget, U1: data layer (set_wp_labor_budget) (2026-06-25)

Status: **U1 SHIPPED prod 2026-06-25 (migs `20260813002200` + harden `20260813002300`, pgTAP 226 21/21).**
Operator directive: "Each WP will have its own labor budget which will be set by either PM or PD."

**Decision (no new ADR ã extends ADR 0060):** labor budget = a money (baht) **cost ceiling**
for labor, distinct from `wp_economics.budget` (the PD-only profit denominator). Money, not
man-days ã the whole labor/profit stack is baht (`wp_labor_costs`, `wp_profit`, `budgetStatus`);
a man-day budget would have nothing to compare against. Single total (not own/dc split). Lives on
`wp_economics` (DRY with budget/is_external, same zero-grant MONEY posture + upsert+audit setter).
Does NOT feed `wp_profit` ã display target only. **Gate = PM or PD** (`project_manager`,
`project_director`, `super_admin`) ã deliberately **widens** vs `set_wp_budget` (PD-only) because
the PM owns crew cost; mirrors `set_wp_external`; names project_manager so project_director rides
along (ADR 0058 / pgTAP 90, still green).

**DB:** `wp_economics.labor_budget numeric(20,4)` nullable + non-negative check;
`set_wp_labor_budget(p_wp, p_budget)` definer, upsert preserving budget/is_external, audits
`{field:'labor_budget'}`. **Server action** `setWpLaborBudget` (`src/lib/labor/actions.ts`):
shape+non-negative validate, gate PM_ROLES on the authed session, call RPC on the user client.

**Adversarial review (workflow, 15 agents) caught a real medium security bug ã harden migration
`20260813002300`:** the first migration revoked EXECUTE only from `public`, not `anon` (Supabase
auto-grants EXECUTE to anon on new functions), and the gate was null-unsafe (`current_user_role()`
is NULL for anon ã `NULL not in (...)` is NULL ã 42501 never fired ã anon could write `labor_budget`
via direct PostgREST with `actor_id` NULL). Fixed: `revoke ... from public, anon` + null-safe gate
(role captured once into `v_role`, explicit `is null` check). Verified live: anon_exec=false,
auth_exec=true. Also softened the table comment ("read by PM review page" ã "spec 205 U2, not built
yet"). **pgTAP 226 (21):** catalog + zero-grant col + anon/auth EXECUTE lockdown ôñ PM/PD/super set ôñ
0 accepted (ã  NULL) ôñ SA/visitor/null-role denied (42501) ôñ unknown/negative/null (P0001) ôñ upsert
preserves budget+is_external ôñ audit count. Full suite green (vitest 1699/1699, typecheck, lint);
pgTAP 176 files / 3000 assertions / 0 failures incl. 90/99/36. **U2 (PLANNED):** budget-vs-actual
card on `/review/work-packages/[id]` Á¡Á¿Á¡ýÁ¿Á¡ÈÁ¡ section + inline set control.

**Follow-up surfaced (out of scope):** `set_wp_budget` / `set_wp_external` (20260761000000) have NO
grant management at all ã share the latent anon-exec exposure; should get the same `from public, anon`
revoke + null-safe gate in a hardening sweep. (Spawned as a background task.)

## Spec 205 ã WP labor budget, U2: budget-vs-actual UI (ARC COMPLETE) (2026-06-25)

Status: **U2 SHIPPED 2026-06-25 (code-only, no DB). SPEC 205 COMPLETE (U1 data + U2 UI).**

Budget-vs-actual surface in the `Á¡Á¿Á¡ýÁ¿Á¡ÈÁ¡` section of the PM WP review page
(`/review/work-packages/[id]`). **Pure** `src/lib/labor/budget.ts` ã `laborBudgetSummary(budget,
spend)`: purpose-built (NOT a thin `budgetStatus` wrapper as the spec first sketched ã the review
flagged that `budgetStatus` treats 0 as "no budget", but the data layer stores 0 ã  NULL on purpose,
so the card must distinguish set-zero from unset). Returns `isSet` (budget !== null), remaining,
`pctUsed` (null when budget 0 with spend), `over`, and a `tone` (ok / attn ãË90% / over). Unit-tested
8/8 incl. the two 0-budget cases. **UI:** `LaborBudgetCard` (server, presentational ã money rendered
server-side) shows Á¡Á¡Á¡Á¿Á¡ýÁ¿Á¡ÈÁ¡ ôñ Á¿Á¡Á¿Á¿Á¡ (with %) ôñ Á¡Á¡Á¿Á¡¨Á¡ËÁ¡ñÁ¡Ù/Á¿Á¡Á¡ÇÁ¡Á¡Á¡ + a toned progress bar; embeds
`LaborBudgetControl` (client, mirrors the equipment `SetDailyRate` ã BottomSheet + numeric input ã
`setWpLaborBudget`). Card test 3/3 (unset prompt / under / over). Labels SSOT'd in `labels.ts`
(`LABOR_BUDGET_*`). The card always renders on this PM-gated page (the PM/PD can set a ceiling before
any labor); `LaborCostView` self-gates to actual cost. Page reads `wp_economics.labor_budget` via the
admin client (zero-grant) next to the existing `wp_labor_costs` read; compares against
`costSummary.total`. **Verified with a real render** (temp route + preview MCP screenshot, 4 states:
unset / under-42% green / attn-94% amber / over-128% red ã all correct). Render gate: the `Á¡Á¿Á¡ýÁ¿Á¡ÈÁ¡`
section now always shows on the review page. **Adversarial review (10 agents) ã 4 low/nit fixes
applied:** (1) `pctUsed` floors instead of rounds ã rounding up showed a full 100% bar with money
still remaining on a fractional spend, and tripped amber at 89.5%; floor keeps the % honest and the
90% boundary exact (over stays the single source of the full-bar truth) ôñ (2) same fix makes the attn
threshold exactly 90% ôñ (3) progress bar gains `role="progressbar"` + aria-valuenow/min/max + Thai
aria-label (matches work-package-list's bar) ôñ (4) spec body updated from the stale "thin wrapper"
sketch to the as-built purpose-built helper. +3 tests (fractional near-budget, 90% boundary,
progressbar role). Full suite green, typecheck + lint clean.
